# app.R — CSS/PMS Buddy (hybrid persistent login: localStorage + cookie) + footer + responsive topbar
suppressPackageStartupMessages({
  library(shiny); library(bslib); library(shinyWidgets); library(shinyjs); library(DT)

# ---- Safe scalar coalescer ----
nz1 <- function(x) !is.null(x) && length(x) >= 1 && !is.na(x[1]) &&
  !(is.character(x[1]) && identical(x[1], ""))
`%||%` <- function(a, b) if (nz1(a)) a[1] else b

# ---- Active-binding shim for option labels (so UI can do opt_text$A etc.) ----
.cssbuddy_make_opt_text <- local({
  labs <- list(A="A) ", B="B) ", C="C) ", D="D) ")
  obj  <- structure(list(labs=labs), class="cssbuddy_opttext")
  function() obj
})
`[[.cssbuddy_opttext` <- function(x, i, ...) x$labs
`[.cssbuddy_opttext`  <- function(x, i, ...) x$labs
`$.cssbuddy_opttext`  <- function(x, name) x$labs[[as.character(name)]] %||% ""
if (exists("opt_text", envir = .GlobalEnv, inherits = FALSE)) {
  try(removeBinding("opt_text", .GlobalEnv), silent = TRUE)
  try(rm(list = "opt_text", envir = .GlobalEnv), silent = TRUE)
}
makeActiveBinding(
  "opt_text",
  fun = function(value) {
    if (missing(value)) return(.cssbuddy_make_opt_text())
    invisible(NULL)
  },
  env = .GlobalEnv
)

# ---- Sessions table (persistent login) ----
ensure_sessions_table <- function(conn){
  DBI::dbExecute(conn, "
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS sessions (
      token TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
      created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
      last_seen  TEXT,
      expires_at TEXT,
      user_agent TEXT,
      ip TEXT,
      FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    )
  ")
  DBI::dbExecute(conn, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sessions_user ON sessions(user_id)")
  invisible(TRUE)
}
ensure_sessions_table(conn)

session_token_new <- function(){
  if (requireNamespace("sodium", quietly = TRUE)) {
    return(sodium::bin2hex(sodium::random(24)))  # 48 hex chars
  }
  paste(sample(c(letters, LETTERS, 0:9), 48, TRUE), collapse = "")
}

session_create <- function(conn, user_id, user_agent = NA_character_, ip = NA_character_, days_valid = 30){
  tok <- session_token_new()
  exp <- format(Sys.time() + days_valid*24*3600, "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  DBI::dbExecute(conn,
                 "INSERT INTO sessions(token, user_id, last_seen, expires_at, user_agent, ip)
     VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?)",
                 params = list(tok, as.integer(user_id),
                               format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"), exp, user_agent, ip)
  )
  tok
}

session_lookup <- function(conn, token, renew_days = 30){
  if (!nzchar(token)) return(NULL)
  df <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "
    SELECT s.user_id, s.expires_at, u.name, u.email
    FROM sessions s JOIN users u ON u.id = s.user_id
    WHERE s.token = ? AND (s.expires_at IS NULL OR s.expires_at > datetime('now'))
    LIMIT 1
  ", params = list(token))
  if (!nrow(df)) return(NULL)
  DBI::dbExecute(conn,
                 "UPDATE sessions
       SET last_seen = datetime('now'),
           expires_at = datetime('now', '+30 days')
     WHERE token = ?",
                 params = list(token)
  )
  list(user_id = df$user_id[1], name = df$name[1], email = df$email[1])
}

session_destroy <- function(conn, token){
  if (!nzchar(token)) return(invisible(FALSE))
  try(DBI::dbExecute(conn, "DELETE FROM sessions WHERE token = ?", params = list(token)), silent = TRUE)
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# ---- Secure Admin Creation System ----
ensure_admin <- function(conn) {
  # Check if admin user already exists
  admin_exists <- tryCatch({
    admin <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id FROM users WHERE email = ?", 
                        params = list("cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com"))
    nrow(admin) > 0
  }, error = function(e) FALSE)
  
  if (admin_exists) {
    return(invisible(TRUE))
  }
  
  # Admin doesn't exist - create setup mechanism
  admin_config_path <- file.path(app_dir, "db", "admin_config.json")
  
  if (file.exists(admin_config_path)) {
    # Load existing admin config
    admin_config <- fromJSON(admin_config_path)
    admin_pass <- admin_config$password
    
    # Create admin user
    try({
      u <- create_user(conn, name = "Admin", email = "cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com", password = admin_pass)
      upsert_profile(conn, u$id, exam_type = "CSS", exam_year = lubridate::year(Sys.Date()) + 1,
                     optional_subjects = character(), prep_level = "Advanced", city = NA)
      message("Admin user created successfully")
    }, silent = TRUE)
    
  } else {
    # First run - create admin setup file
    dir.create(file.path(app_dir, "db"), showWarnings = FALSE, recursive = TRUE)
    
    # Generate secure random password
    generate_secure_password <- function(length = 16) {
      chars <- c(letters, LETTERS, 0:9, "!@#$%&*")
      pass <- paste0(sample(chars, length, replace = TRUE), collapse = "")
      return(pass)
    }
    
    admin_pass <- generate_secure_password()
    
    # Create config file with admin setup instructions
    admin_config <- list(
      setup_required = TRUE,
      email = "cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com",
      password = admin_pass,
      setup_time = format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"),
      instructions = "This file contains the initial admin credentials. After first login, change the password through the admin panel."
    )
    
    write_json(admin_config, admin_config_path, auto_unbox = TRUE, pretty = TRUE)
    
    # Create admin user with generated password
    try({
      u <- create_user(conn, name = "Admin", email = "cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com", password = admin_pass)
      upsert_profile(conn, u$id, exam_type = "CSS", exam_year = lubridate::year(Sys.Date()) + 1,
                     optional_subjects = character(), prep_level = "Advanced", city = NA)
      
      message("==============================================")
      message("ADMIN SETUP COMPLETE")
      message("==============================================")
      message("Admin email: cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com")
      message("Admin password: ", admin_pass)
      message("==============================================")
      message("Please login and change the password immediately!")
      message("Config saved to: ", admin_config_path)
      message("==============================================")
    }, silent = TRUE)
  }
  
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# Initialize admin system
ensure_admin(conn)

# NEW: Essay schema + seed
ensure_essay_schema(conn)
essay_seed_topics(conn)

# Helper to fetch optionals safely for the modal UI
get_optionals <- function(conn){
  tryCatch(DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT name FROM optionals ORDER BY name")$name,
           error = function(e) MASTER_OPTIONALS)
}

# ---- Edit Profile Modal UI ----
edit_profile_modal_ui <- function(ns, optional_choices = character(), user_data = NULL, profile_data = NULL) {
  # Get current optional subjects for the user
  current_optionals <- character()
  if (!is.null(profile_data) && !is.null(profile_data$optional_subjects)) {
    if (is.list(profile_data$optional_subjects) && length(profile_data$optional_subjects) > 0) {
      current_optionals <- unlist(profile_data$optional_subjects)
    }
  }
  
  modalDialog(
    title = NULL,
    footer = NULL,
    easyClose = TRUE,
    size = "l",
    div(class = "auth-professional-container",
        div(class = "auth-professional-header",
            h3("Edit Your Profile"),
            p("Update your information to keep your profile current")
        ),
        div(class = "auth-professional-body",
            div(class = "form-group-professional",
                tags$label("FULL NAME"),
                textInput(ns("edit_name"), NULL, value = user_data$name %||% "", placeholder = "Enter your full name")
            ),
            div(class = "form-group-professional",
                tags$label("EMAIL ADDRESS"),
                textInput(ns("edit_email"), NULL, value = user_data$email %||% "", placeholder = "your.email@example.com")
            ),
            div(class = "form-group-professional",
                tags$label("MOBILE NUMBER"),
                textInput(ns("edit_mobile"), NULL, value = profile_data$mobile %||% "", placeholder = "+92 3XX XXXXXXX")
            ),
            div(class = "form-group-professional",
                tags$label("GENDER"),
                shinyWidgets::radioGroupButtons(ns("edit_gender"), NULL,
                                                choices = c("Male", "Female"),
                                                selected = profile_data$gender %||% "Male")
            ),
            div(class = "row",
                div(class = "col-md-6",
                    div(class = "form-group-professional",
                        tags$label("PREPARATION LEVEL"),
                        selectInput(ns("edit_prep"), NULL, 
                                    c("Beginner","Intermediate","Advanced"),
                                    selected = profile_data$prep_level %||% "Beginner")
                    )
                ),
                div(class = "col-md-6",
                    div(class = "form-group-professional",
                        tags$label("TARGET EXAM YEAR"),
                        numericInput(ns("edit_year"), NULL,
                                     value = profile_data$exam_year %||% (lubridate::year(Sys.Date()) + 1),
                                     min = lubridate::year(Sys.Date()),
                                     max = lubridate::year(Sys.Date()) + 5, 
                                     step = 1)
                    )
                )
            ),
            div(class = "form-group-professional",
                tags$label("OPTIONAL SUBJECTS (SELECT UP TO 6)"),
                shinyWidgets::pickerInput(ns("edit_optional"),
                                          NULL,
                                          choices = optional_choices, 
                                          selected = current_optionals,
                                          multiple = TRUE,
                                          options = list(maxOptions = 6, `live-search` = TRUE,
                                                         `actions-box` = TRUE,
                                                         `selected-text-format` = "count > 2",
                                                         `count-selected-text` = "{0} subjects selected"))
            ),
            div(class = "form-group-professional",
                tags$label("CITY (OPTIONAL)"),
                textInput(ns("edit_city"), NULL, value = profile_data$city %||% "", placeholder = "Enter your city")
            ),
            actionButton(ns("update_profile"), "Update Profile", 
                         class = "btn-professional-success"),
            div(class = "mt-4 text-center", uiOutput(ns("edit_profile_msg")))
        )
    )
  )
}

# ---- Simplified UI ----
ui <- function(req) {
  fluidPage(
    theme = app_theme,
    useShinyjs(),
    
    # ====== Loader markup & scripts ======
    tags$head(tags$style(startup_loader_css)),
    
    # ====== Browser Tab Title with Icon ======
    tags$head(
      tags$title("CssBuddy.pk"),
      tags$link(rel = "icon", href = "data:image/svg+xml,<svg xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg' viewBox='0 0 24 24' fill='%234F46E5'><path d='M12 3L1 9l4 2.18v6L12 21l7-3.82v-6l2-1.09V17h2V9L12 3zm6.82 6L12 12.72 5.18 9 12 5.28 18.82 9zM17 15.99l-5 2.73-5-2.73v-3.72L12 15l5-2.73v3.72z'/></svg>")
    ),
    
    # Overlay HTML
    div(
      id = "app_loader",
      div(class="glass",
          div(class="loader-top",
              span(class="loader-logo", icon("graduation-cap")),
              span(class="loader-title", "CssBuddy.pk is getting things ready…")
          ),
          div(class="orbit",
              div(class="ring r1"), div(class="ring r2"), div(class="ring r3"),
              div(class="planet"), div(class="comet c1"), div(class="comet c2"), div(class="comet c3")
          ),
          div(class="progress-wrap",
              div(class="progress-bar", div(class="progress-fill", id="loader_fill"))
          ),
          div(class="loader-bottom",
              div(class="loader-tip", id="loader_tip", "Tip: Short sessions daily beat marathon cramming."),
              div(class="loader-time", id="loader_time", "00%")
          )
      )
    ),
    # JS to handle timing (5–8s), fun tips, and early hide if server signals
    tags$script(HTML("
      (function(){
        var minMs = 5000; var maxMs = 8000;
        var totalMs = Math.floor(Math.random() * (maxMs - minMs + 1)) + minMs;
        var start = Date.now(); var doneSignal = false; var killed = false;
        var tips = [
          'Tip: Review past papers to learn examiner patterns.',
          'Fact: 25 minutes of focused writing beats 2 hours of distracted reading.',
          'Hint: Convert notes to MCQs to test retention.',
          'Pro move: Space out revisions—forgetting is part of learning.',
          'Shortcut: Use the Guess Papers tab for targeted prep.'
        ];
        var tipEl = document.getElementById('loader_tip');
        var fill = document.getElementById('loader_fill');
        var pctEl = document.getElementById('loader_time');
        function setTip(){ tipEl && (tipEl.textContent = tips[Math.floor(Math.random()*tips.length)]); }
        setTip(); var tipTimer = setInterval(setTip, 1600);

        function tick(){
          if (!fill || killed) return;
          var elapsed = Date.now() - start;
          var pct = Math.min(100, Math.round((elapsed / totalMs) * 100));
          fill.style.width = pct + '%';
          if (pctEl) pctEl.textContent = (pct<10?'0':'') + pct + '%';
          if (elapsed >= totalMs && (doneSignal || elapsed >= totalMs + 1200)){
            hide();
          } else {
            requestAnimationFrame(tick);
          }
        }
        requestAnimationFrame(tick);

        function hide(){
          if (killed) return; killed = true;
          clearInterval(tipTimer);
          var el = document.getElementById('app_loader');
          if (!el) return;
          el.classList.add('hide-loader');
          setTimeout(function(){ if (el && el.parentNode) el.parentNode.removeChild(el); }, 520);
        }

        // Always hide after totalMs; allow server to signal readiness too
        setTimeout(function(){ if (!killed) hide(); }, totalMs + 1500);

        // If server says we're ready, mark signal; actual hide waits for min duration
        if (window.Shiny){
          Shiny.addCustomMessageHandler('cssbuddy:loader-done', function(){
            doneSignal = true;
          });
        }

        // As a safety, if something blocks, kill after 10s
        setTimeout(function(){ if (!killed) hide(); }, 10000);
      })();
    ")),
    
    tags$head(
      tags$script(HTML("
      // run arbitrary JS snippets sent from server (used by Essay module)
      Shiny.addCustomMessageHandler('evaljs', function(p){
        try { eval(p && p.code ? p.code : ''); } catch(e) { /* no-op */ }
      });
    ")),
      
      tags$link(rel = "stylesheet", type = "text/css", href = "style.css?v=20250904"),
      
      # === Simplified CSS without outer layout constraints ===
      tags$style(HTML("
  /* Reset any outer container constraints */
  html, body { margin: 0; padding: 0; height: 100%; overflow: hidden; }
  .container-fluid { padding: 0; margin: 0; width: 100%; height: 100%; }
  
  /* ===== Tabs: never stack hidden panes ===== */
  .nav.nav-tabs { display: none !important; }
  .tab-content { position: relative; width: 100%; min-width: 0; height: 100%; }
  .tab-content > .tab-pane { display: none !important; width: 100%; visibility: hidden; height: 100%; }
  .tab-content > .tab-pane.active { display: block !important; width: 100%; visibility: visible; height: 100%; }

  /* ===== Main app container ===== */
  .app-container {
    display: flex;
    flex-direction: column;
    height: 100vh;
    width: 100vw;
    overflow: hidden;
  }

  /* ===== Topbar ===== */
  .topbar {
    position: sticky;
    top: 0;
    z-index: 1030;
    display: grid;
    grid-template-columns: auto 1fr auto;
    align-items: center;
    gap: 8px;
    height: 60px;
    padding: 0 12px;
    background: var(--bs-body-bg);
    border-bottom: 1px solid var(--bs-border-color);
    flex-shrink: 0;
  }
  .brand { display: inline-flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px; justify-self: start; }
  .brand-logo { width: 36px; height: 36px; border-radius: 12px; display:flex; align-items:center; justify-content:center; background: rgba(79,70,229,.14); color: var(--primary); }
  .brand-title { font-weight: 900; font-size: 2.1rem; letter-spacing: .3px; }
  .topbar-center { text-align: center; justify-self: center; width: 100%; max-width: 100%; }
  .welcome-line { font-weight: 800; line-height: 1.2; font-size: 0.95rem; }
  .welcome-sub  { display: none; color: var(--bs-secondary); }
  .topbar-actions { justify-self: end; display:flex; align-items:center; gap:.25rem; }

  /* ===== DARK THEME TOPBAR TEXT FIX ===== */
  .theme-dark .brand-title,
  .theme-dark .welcome-line,
  .theme-dark .welcome-line .text-primary {
    color: #000000 !important;
  }

        .theme-dark .mcq-bank-card .dataTables_wrapper .dataTables_filter { color: #111827 !important; }
      ")),
      
      # === HYBRID SID storage: localStorage + cookie ===
      tags$script(HTML("
        (function(){
          var KEY = 'cssbuddy_sid';
          function readCookie(name){
            var m = document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(?:^|; )' + name.replace(/([.$?*|{}()\\[\\]\\\\\\/\\+^])/g,'\\\\$1') + '=([^;]*)'));
            return m ? decodeURIComponent(m[1]) : null;
          }
          function writeCookie(name, value, maxAge){
            var secure = (location.protocol === 'https:') ? '; Secure' : '';
            document.cookie = name + '=' + encodeURIComponent(value || '') + '; Path=/'
                              + (maxAge!=null?('; Max-Age=' + maxAge):'')
                              + '; SameSite=Lax' + secure;
          }
          function getLS(){
            try{
              var v = localStorage.getItem(KEY);
              if (v && v !== 'undefined' && v !== 'null') return v;
            }catch(e){}
            return null;
          }
          function setLS(v){
            try{
              if (v) localStorage.setItem(KEY, v); else localStorage.removeItem(KEY);
            }catch(e){}
          }
          function getSID(){ return getLS() || readCookie(KEY) || ''; }
          function setSID(v){
            setLS(v);
            if (v) writeCookie(KEY, v, 2592000); else writeCookie(KEY, '', 0);
          }
          function sendToShiny(){
            var sid = getSID();
            if (window.Shiny) Shiny.setInputValue('cssbuddy_sid', sid || '', {priority:'event'});
          }
          document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', sendToShiny);
          document.addEventListener('shiny:connected', sendToShiny);

          if (window.Shiny){
            Shiny.addCustomMessageHandler('cssbuddy:set-sid', function(p){
              var v = (p && p.value) ? p.value : '';
              if (v) { setSID(v); sendToShiny(); }
            });
            Shiny.addCustomMessageHandler('cssbuddy:clear-sid', function(){
              setSID(''); sendToShiny();
            });
          }
        })();
      ")),
      
      # Send initial hash to R once Shiny is connected
      tags$script(HTML("
        document.addEventListener('shiny:connected', function(){
          try {
            var h = (location.hash || '').replace(/^#/, '');
            Shiny.setInputValue('initial_hash', h, {priority:'event'});
          } catch(e){}
        });
      ")),
      
      # Persist theme + tab highlight + mobile sidebar functionality
      tags$script(HTML("
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){
          try {
            var mode = localStorage.getItem('cssbuddy_theme') || 'light';
            document.body.classList.toggle('theme-dark', mode==='dark');
            var t = document.getElementById('darkToggle');
            if (t) t.setAttribute('data-state', mode);
          } catch(e){}
        });
        
        // Enhanced click handler for better mobile support
        document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
          // Dark mode toggle
          var tog = e.target.closest('#darkToggle');
          if (tog){
            var next = document.body.classList.contains('theme-dark') ? 'light' : 'dark';
            document.body.classList.toggle('theme-dark', next==='dark');
            try { localStorage.setItem('cssbuddy_theme', next); } catch(e){}
            tog.setAttribute('data-state', next);
            return;
          }
          
          // Sidebar menu links
          var link = e.target.closest('.menu-link');
          if (link){
            e.preventDefault();
            var target = link.getAttribute('data-target');
            if (target && window.Shiny && Shiny.setInputValue){
              Shiny.setInputValue('go_tab', target, {priority:'event'});
            }
            // Close mobile sidebar if open
            var mobileSidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar_mobile');
            var overlay = document.getElementById('sidebar_overlay');
            if (mobileSidebar && mobileSidebar.classList.contains('open')) {
              mobileSidebar.classList.remove('open');
              if (overlay) overlay.style.display = 'none';
            }
            return;
          }
          
          // Mobile sidebar overlay click to close
          var overlay = e.target.closest('#sidebar_overlay');
          if (overlay) {
            var mobileSidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar_mobile');
            if (mobileSidebar) mobileSidebar.classList.remove('open');
            overlay.style.display = 'none';
            return;
          }
        });
      ")),
      tags$script(HTML("
        document.addEventListener('shiny:connected', function(){
          Shiny.addCustomMessageHandler('cssbuddy:tab-changed', function(payload){
            var target = payload && payload.id ? payload.id : null;
            if (!target) return;
            try { localStorage.setItem('cssbuddy_last_tab', target); } catch(e){}
            var links = document.querySelectorAll('.menu-link');
            links.forEach(function(l){ l.classList.toggle('active', l.getAttribute('data-target') === target); });
            if (location.hash !== '#'+target) { history.replaceState(null,'','#'+target); }
          });

          // NEW: generic eval hook used by Essay module to initialize Quill safely per-namespace
          Shiny.addCustomMessageHandler('evaljs', function(p){
            try { eval(p && p.code ? p.code : String(p)); } catch(e) {}
          });
        });
      "))
    ),
    
    # ==== Main App Structure ====
    div(class = "app-container",
        # ==== Topbar ====
        div(class = "topbar",
            div(class = "brand",
                span(class = "brand-logo me-1", icon("graduation-cap")),
                span(class = "brand-title", "CssBuddy.pk")
            ),
            div(class = "topbar-center", uiOutput("top_center_title", inline = TRUE)),
            div(class = "topbar-actions d-flex align-items-center gap-2",
                div(id = "darkToggle", class = "toggle theme-toggle", `data-state` = "light",
                    span(class="toggle-icon sun", icon("sun")),
                    span(class="toggle-nub"),
                    span(class="toggle-icon moon", icon("moon"))
                ),
                actionButton("toggle_sidebar_mobile", NULL, icon = icon("bars"),
                             class = "btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary d-lg-none", title = "Menu"),
                uiOutput("top_right_area")
            )
        ),
        
        # ==== Main Content Area ====
        div(class = "main-content",
            # Desktop Sidebar
            tags$aside(
              id = "sidebar_desktop", class = "sidebar",
              div(class = "sidebar-menu list-unstyled",
                  tags$a(href = "#dashboard", class = "menu-link d-flex align-items-center", `data-target` = "dashboard",
                         span(class = "menu-icon", icon("tachometer-alt")), span(class = "menu-label ms-2", "Home")),
                  tags$a(href = "#studyplan", class = "menu-link d-flex align-items-center", `data-target` = "studyplan",
                         span(class = "menu-icon", icon("calendar-alt")), span(class = "menu-label ms-2", "Study Plan")),
                  tags$a(href = "#practice", class = "menu-link d-flex align-items-center", `data-target` = "practice",
                         span(class = "menu-icon", icon("tasks")), span(class = "menu-label ms-2", "Practice")),
                  tags$a(href = "#books", class = "menu-link d-flex align-items-center", `data-target` = "books",
                         span(class = "menu-icon", icon("book")), span(class = "menu-label ms-2", "Books Marketplace")),
                  tags$a(href = "#past", class = "menu-link d-flex align-items-center", `data-target` = "past",
                         span(class = "menu-icon", icon("file-alt")), span(class = "menu-label ms-2", "Past Papers")),
                  tags$a(href = "#news", class = "menu-link d-flex align-items-center", `data-target` = "news",
                         span(class = "menu-icon", icon("newspaper")), span(class = "menu-label ms-2", "News Articles")),
                  tags$a(href = "#premium", class = "menu-link d-flex align-items-center", `data-target` = "premium",
                         span(class = "menu-icon", icon("file-alt")), span(class = "menu-label ms-2", "Notes (Screening/MPT)")),
                  tags$a(href = "#partner", class = "menu-link d-flex align-items-center", `data-target` = "partner",

            div(id = "sidebar_overlay", class = "sidebar-mobile-overlay"),

                div(class = "sidebar-menu list-unstyled",
                    tags$a(href = "#dashboard", class = "menu-link d-flex align-items-center", `data-target` = "dashboard",

server <- function(input, output, session){
  # Auth state
  auth <- reactiveValues(logged_in = FALSE, user = NULL, profile = NULL)
  current_sid <- reactiveVal(NULL)
  
  # ---- Non-reactive admin flag for safe checks outside reactivity ----
  session$userData$is_admin_flag <- FALSE
  observe({
    session$userData$is_admin_flag <- isTRUE(auth$logged_in) &&
      identical(tolower(auth$user$email %||% ""), "cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com")
  })
  
  # Admin? (reactive - for reactive UIs like the sidebar link)
  is_admin <- reactive({
    isTRUE(auth$logged_in) && identical(tolower(auth$user$email %||% ""), "cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com")
  })
  
  # ---- Auth module (login flow) ----
  auth_ret <- mod_auth_server("auth_modal", conn = conn, optional_subjects = MASTER_OPTIONALS)
  
  # On login success -> create session + store SID (localStorage+cookie)
  observeEvent(auth_ret$logged_in(), ignoreInit = TRUE, {
    if (!isTRUE(auth_ret$logged_in())) return()
    auth$logged_in <- TRUE
    auth$user     <- auth_ret$user()
    auth$profile  <- auth_ret$profile()
    removeModal()
    if (exists("refresh_user_env")) refresh_user_env(conn)
    
    uid <- auth$user$id %||% NA_integer_
    if (!is.na(uid)) {
      ua <- try(session$request$HTTP_USER_AGENT %||% NA_character_, silent = TRUE)
      ip <- try(session$request$REMOTE_ADDR %||% NA_character_, silent = TRUE)
      tok <- session_create(conn, user_id = uid, user_agent = ua, ip = ip, days_valid = 30)
      current_sid(tok)
      session$sendCustomMessage("cssbuddy:set-sid", list(value = tok))
    }
  })
  
  # Auto-login on refresh (SID arrives from JS as input$cssbuddy_sid)
  observeEvent(input$cssbuddy_sid, {
    tok <- input$cssbuddy_sid %||% ""
    if (!nzchar(tok)) return()
    if (isTRUE(auth$logged_in)) return()
    look <- session_lookup(conn, tok)
    if (!is.null(look)) {
      auth$logged_in <- TRUE
      auth$user <- list(id = look$user_id, name = look$name, email = look$email)
      auth$profile <- tryCatch(get_profile(conn, look$user_id), error = function(e) NULL)
      current_sid(tok)
      if (exists("refresh_user_env")) refresh_user_env(conn)
    } else {
      session$sendCustomMessage("cssbuddy:clear-sid", list())
      current_sid(NULL)
    }
  }, ignoreInit = FALSE, priority = 100)
  
  # ---- Top-right area ----
  output$top_right_area <- renderUI({
    if (!isTRUE(auth$logged_in)) {
      tagList(
        actionButton("open_login", "Sign in / Sign up",
                     class = "btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary d-none d-md-inline-flex"),
        actionButton("open_login_sm", NULL, icon = icon("user"),
                     class = "btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary d-inline-flex d-md-none",
                     title = "Sign in / Sign up")
      )
    } else {
      div(class = "dropdown",
          tags$button(
            class = "btn btn-sm btn-outline-secondary d-flex align-items-center gap-2 dropdown-toggle",
            id = "userMenuBtn", `data-bs-toggle` = "dropdown", `aria-expanded` = "false",
            span(class = "avatar text-uppercase",
                 substr((auth$user$name %||% auth$user$email %||% "U"), 1, 1)),
            span(class = "user-name-text d-none d-md-inline",
                 (auth$user$name %||% auth$user$email))
          ),
          tags$ul(class = "dropdown-menu dropdown-menu-end", `aria-labelledby` = "userMenuBtn",
                  tags$li(tags$h6(class = "dropdown-header", (auth$user$name %||% auth$user$email))),
                  tags$li(tags$span(class = "dropdown-item-text small text-muted",
                                    paste0("Prep: ", auth$profile$prep_level %||% "-"))),
                  tags$li(tags$span(class = "dropdown-item-text small text-muted",
                                    paste0("Exam year: ", auth$profile$exam_year %||% "-"))),
                  tags$li(tags$hr(class = "dropdown-divider")),
                  # NEW: Edit Profile option
                  tags$li(actionLink("edit_profile", "Edit Profile", class = "dropdown-item")),
                  tags$li(actionLink("logout", "Logout", class = "dropdown-item text-danger"))
          )
      )
    }
  })
  
  # ---- Edit Profile Modal ----
  observeEvent(input$edit_profile, {
    # Get fresh data from database to ensure we have the latest
    user_id <- auth$user$id
    if (is.null(user_id)) return()
    
    # Get current user data
    current_user <- tryCatch({
      dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT name, email FROM users WHERE id = ?", params = list(user_id))
    }, error = function(e) NULL)
    
    # Get current profile data
    current_profile <- tryCatch(get_profile(conn, user_id), error = function(e) NULL)
    
    if (is.null(current_user) || is.null(current_profile)) {
      showNotification("Error loading profile data", type = "error")
      return()
    }
    
    # Get optional subjects
    opts <- get_optionals(conn)
    
    # Show edit profile modal
    showModal(edit_profile_modal_ui(
      ns = function(x) x,  # No namespace needed for main app
      optional_choices = opts,
      user_data = current_user,
      profile_data = current_profile
    ))
  })
  
  # ---- Update Profile ----
  observeEvent(input$update_profile, {
    user_id <- auth$user$id
    if (is.null(user_id)) return()
    
    # Debug the input values
    cat("DEBUG: Edit profile form submitted\n")
    cat("DEBUG: User ID:", user_id, "\n")
    cat("DEBUG: Selected optional subjects:", paste(input$edit_optional, collapse=", "), "\n")
    cat("DEBUG: Number of selected subjects:", length(input$edit_optional), "\n")
    
    # Validate inputs
    if (!nzchar(input$edit_name %||% "")) {
      output$edit_profile_msg <- renderUI(
        div(class = "alert alert-danger alert-professional", "Please enter your name.")
      )
      return()
    }
    
    if (!nzchar(input$edit_email %||% "") || !grepl(".+@.+\\..+", input$edit_email)) {
      output$edit_profile_msg <- renderUI(
        div(class = "alert alert-danger alert-professional", "Please enter a valid email address.")
      )
      return()
    }
    
    # Check if email is already taken by another user
    email_check <- tryCatch({
      existing <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id FROM users WHERE email = ? AND id != ?", 
                             params = list(input$edit_email, user_id))
      nrow(existing) > 0
    }, error = function(e) FALSE)
    
    if (email_check) {
      output$edit_profile_msg <- renderUI(
        div(class = "alert alert-danger alert-professional", "This email is already registered by another user.")
      )
      return()
    }
    
    # Validate mobile number if provided
    mob <- trimws(input$edit_mobile %||% "")
    if (nzchar(mob) && !grepl("^[0-9+ ()-]{7,}$", mob)) {
      output$edit_profile_msg <- renderUI(
        div(class = "alert alert-danger alert-professional", "Please enter a valid mobile number.")
      )
      return()
    }
    
    tryCatch({
      # Update user table
      dbExecute(conn, "UPDATE users SET name = ?, email = ? WHERE id = ?",
                params = list(input$edit_name, input$edit_email, user_id))
      
      # Update profile
      upsert_profile(conn, user_id,
                     exam_type = "CSS",
                     exam_year = input$edit_year,
                     prep_level = input$edit_prep,
                     city = input$edit_city %||% NA,
                     mobile = mob %||% NA,
                     gender = input$edit_gender %||% NA)
      
      # FIX: Ensure we're passing all selected subjects correctly
      selected_subjects <- input$edit_optional
      if (is.null(selected_subjects)) {
        selected_subjects <- character()
      }
      
      cat("DEBUG: Passing to upsert_user_optionals:", paste(selected_subjects, collapse=", "), "\n")
      cat("DEBUG: Number of subjects to pass:", length(selected_subjects), "\n")
      
      # Update optional subjects - FIXED: Pass all selected subjects
      upsert_user_optionals(conn, user_id, selected_subjects)
      
      # Refresh auth data
      auth$user$name <- input$edit_name
      auth$user$email <- input$edit_email
      auth$profile <- get_profile(conn, user_id)
      
      if (exists("refresh_user_env")) refresh_user_env(conn)
      
      # Show success message and close modal
      showNotification("Profile updated successfully!", type = "message")
      removeModal()
      
    }, error = function(e) {
      output$edit_profile_msg <- renderUI(
        div(class = "alert alert-danger alert-professional", paste("Error updating profile:", e$message))
      )
    })
  })
  
  # ---- Admin link in sidebar (conditional render - reactive) ----
  output$sidebar_admin_link <- renderUI({
    if (!isTRUE(is_admin())) return(NULL)
    tags$a(
      href = "#admin",
      class = "menu-link d-flex align-items-center",
      `data-target` = "admin",
      span(class = "menu-icon", icon("user-shield")),
      span(class = "menu-label ms-2", "Admin")
    )
  })
  
  output$sidebar_admin_link_mobile <- renderUI({
    if (!isTRUE(is_admin())) return(NULL)
    tags$a(
      href = "#admin",
      class = "menu-link d-flex align-items-center",
      `data-target` = "admin",
      span(class = "menu-icon", icon("user-shield")),
      span(class = "menu-label ms-2", "Admin")
    )
  })
  
  # Center title
  rand_motivation <- reactiveVal({
    pool <- getOption("cssbuddy.motives_pool", default = c("Stay consistent. Compounds daily."))
    if (!length(pool)) "Stay consistent. Compounds daily." else sample(pool, 1)
  })
  output$top_center_title <- renderUI({
    logged <- isTRUE(auth$logged_in)
    nm <- if (logged) (auth$user$name %||% auth$user$email %||% "Buddy") else "Buddy"
    nm <- htmltools::htmlEscape(nm)
    tagList(
      div(class = "welcome-line",
          HTML(sprintf("Welcome back, <span class='text-primary fw-bold'>%s</span>!", nm))
      ),
      div(class = "welcome-sub", tags$i(rand_motivation()))
    )
  })
  
  observeEvent(input$open_login, ignoreInit = TRUE, {
    # Re-arm the auth module so clicks always work
    if (!is.null(auth_ret$reset) && is.function(auth_ret$reset)) auth_ret$reset()
    opts <- get_optionals(conn)
    showModal(modalDialog(size = "l", easyClose = TRUE, footer = NULL,
                          mod_auth_ui("auth_modal", optional_choices = opts)))
  })
  observeEvent(input$open_login_sm, ignoreInit = TRUE, {
    if (!is.null(auth_ret$reset) && is.function(auth_ret$reset)) auth_ret$reset()
    opts <- get_optionals(conn)
    showModal(modalDialog(size = "l", easyClose = TRUE, footer = NULL,
                          mod_auth_ui("auth_modal", optional_choices = opts)))
  })
  
  # Logout
  observeEvent(input$logout, ignoreInit = TRUE, {
    tok <- current_sid() %||% ""
    if (nzchar(tok)) session_destroy(conn, tok)
    session$sendCustomMessage("cssbuddy:clear-sid", list())
    auth$logged_in <- FALSE; auth$user <- NULL; auth$profile <- NULL
    current_sid(NULL)
    # Re-arm the module for the next login attempt
    if (!is.null(auth_ret$reset) && is.function(auth_ret$reset)) auth_ret$reset()
    if (exists("refresh_user_env")) refresh_user_env(conn)
  })
  
  # Mobile sidebar toggle - FIXED VERSION
  observeEvent(input$toggle_sidebar_mobile, {
    shinyjs::runjs("
      (function(){
        var sidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar_mobile');
        var overlay = document.getElementById('sidebar_overlay');
        if (!sidebar) return;
        
        if (sidebar.classList.contains('open')) {
          sidebar.classList.remove('open');
          if (overlay) overlay.style.display = 'none';
        } else {
          sidebar.classList.add('open');
          if (overlay) overlay.style.display = 'block';
        }
      })();
    ")
  })
  
  # Close mobile sidebar when clicking overlay
  observeEvent(input$click, {
    # This will be triggered by any click, but we'll handle specific cases in JavaScript
    # The main overlay click is handled in the JavaScript click handler above
  })
  
  # ---------- Navigation ----------
  ALL_TABS       <- c("dashboard","studyplan","practice","books",
                      "past","news","premium","partner","essay","admin")
  
  PROTECTED_TABS <- c("premium","partner","essay")
  ADMIN_TABS     <- c("admin")
  
  nav_guard <- reactiveVal(FALSE)
  set_hash <- function(target, mode = "replace"){
    nav_guard(TRUE)
    updateQueryString(paste0("#", target), mode = mode)
    session$sendCustomMessage("cssbuddy:tab-changed", list(id = target))
  }
  open_auth_modal <- function(){
    # Re-arm module before showing (works even if already armed)
    if (!is.null(auth_ret$reset) && is.function(auth_ret$reset)) auth_ret$reset()
    opts <- get_optionals(conn)
    showModal(modalDialog(size = "l", easyClose = TRUE, footer = NULL,
                          mod_auth_ui("auth_modal", optional_choices = opts)))
  }
  switch_to_tab <- function(target){
    if (!(target %in% ALL_TABS)) return(invisible())
    # Use non-reactive flag here (works anywhere)
    if (target %in% ADMIN_TABS && !isTRUE(session$userData$is_admin_flag)) {
      open_auth_modal()
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "main_tabs", selected = "dashboard")
      set_hash("dashboard", mode = "replace")
      return(invisible())
    }
    logged <- isTRUE(auth$logged_in)
    if (!logged && (target %in% PROTECTED_TABS)) {
      open_auth_modal()
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "main_tabs", selected = "dashboard")
      set_hash("dashboard", mode = "replace")
      return(invisible())
    }
    updateTabsetPanel(session, "main_tabs", selected = target)
    set_hash(target, mode = "replace")
    invisible()
  }
  
  # From clicks in sidebar
  observeEvent(input$go_tab, { switch_to_tab(input$go_tab) })
  
  # Reactively handle hash changes after load
  observeEvent(session$clientData$url_hash, {
    if (isTRUE(nav_guard())) { nav_guard(FALSE); return() }
    h <- sub("^#", "", session$clientData$url_hash %||% "")
    if (nzchar(h)) switch_to_tab(h)
  }, ignoreInit = FALSE)
  
  # Reactively handle the initial hash sent from JS on connect
  observeEvent(input$initial_hash, {
    h <- input$initial_hash %||% ""
    if (nzchar(h)) switch_to_tab(h) else switch_to_tab("dashboard")
  }, ignoreInit = TRUE, once = TRUE)
  
  # Personalized bits for dashboard
  exam_date <- reactive({
    yr <- auth$profile$exam_year %||% lubridate::year(Sys.Date())
    as.Date(paste0(yr, "-02-15"))
  })
  streak_value <- reactiveVal(1L)
  
  # Dashboard
  mod_dashboard_server(
    "dashboard",
    conn = conn,
    user_profile = reactive(auth$profile %||% list(
      name = NULL, prep_level = NULL, exam_year = NULL, optional_subjects = list(character())
    )),
    exam_date = exam_date,
    streak_value = streak_value
  )
  
  # Other modules
  mod_studyplan_server("studyplan", is_logged_in = reactive(isTRUE(auth$logged_in)))
  mod_practice_server("practice", conn = conn, is_logged_in = reactive(isTRUE(auth$logged_in)))
  
  # books
  mod_books_server(
    "books",
    conn = conn,
    is_logged_in = reactive(isTRUE(auth$logged_in)),
    user = reactive(auth$user),
    open_login_modal = function() {
      # Re-arm the auth module so clicks always work
      if (!is.null(auth_ret$reset) && is.function(auth_ret$reset)) auth_ret$reset()
      opts <- get_optionals(conn)
      showModal(modalDialog(size = "l", easyClose = TRUE, footer = NULL,
                            mod_auth_ui("auth_modal", optional_choices = opts)))
    }
  )
  
  mod_pastpapers_server("past")
  mod_news_server("news")
  mod_premium_server("premium", user_email = reactive({
    if (isTRUE(auth$logged_in)) {
      auth$user$email
    } else {
      NULL
    }
  }))
  
  # Study Partner module
  mod_partner_server(
    "partner",
    user_id = reactive(auth$user$id),
    conn = conn
  )
  
  # Essay module
  mod_essay_server(
    "essay",
    conn = conn,
    is_logged_in = reactive(isTRUE(auth$logged_in)),
    user = reactive(auth$user),
    is_admin = reactive(isTRUE(auth$logged_in) && identical(tolower(auth$user$email %||% ""), "cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com"))
  )
  
  # In your main server function
  nav_target <- reactiveVal(NULL)
  
  observeEvent(nav_target(), {
    req(nav_target())
    updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = nav_target())
    nav_target(NULL)
  })
  # Admin
  mod_admin_server("admin", conn = conn)
  
  # ===== Signal that server is ready (loader will hide after min 5–8s window) =====
  session$sendCustomMessage("cssbuddy:loader-done", list(ok = TRUE))
}
shinyApp(ui, server)

      }

      }

        }
        
        .auth-professional-body {
          padding: 2.5rem 2rem;
        }
        
        .auth-professional-header {
          padding: 2.5rem 2rem;
        }
        
        .auth-professional-header h3 {
          font-size: 2.1rem;
        }
        
        .btn-professional-primary,
        .btn-professional-success {
          padding: 1.1rem 1.5rem;
          font-size: 1rem;
        }
      }
      
      /* Focus states for accessibility */
      .btn:focus,
      .form-control:focus,
      .selectize-input.focus {
        outline: none;
        box-shadow: 0 0 0 3px rgba(52, 152, 219, 0.2) !important;
      }
    "))
  )
  
  # PROFESSIONAL CONTAINER
  div(class = "auth-professional-container",
      custom_css,
      div(class = "auth-professional-header",
          h3("CSS BUDDY"),
          p("Your Gateway to Civil Service Excellence")
      ),
      div(class = "auth-professional-body",
          div(class = "auth-professional-tabs",
              shinyWidgets::radioGroupButtons(
                inputId = ns("mode"), 
                label = NULL,
                choices = c("Sign In" = "signin", "Sign Up" = "signup"),
                selected = "signin",
                justified = TRUE
              )
          ),
          
          # --- Sign In ---
          conditionalPanel(
            condition = sprintf("input['%s'] == 'signin'", ns("mode")),
            div(id = ns("signin_form"),
                div(class = "form-group-professional",
                    tags$label("EMAIL ADDRESS"),
                    textInput(ns("si_email"), NULL, placeholder = "Enter your email address")
                ),
                div(class = "form-group-professional",
                    tags$label("PASSWORD"),
                    passwordInput(ns("si_password"), NULL, placeholder = "Enter your password")
                ),
                actionButton(ns("do_signin"), "Sign In to Your Account", 
                             class = "btn-professional-primary"),
                
            )
          ),
          
          # --- Sign Up ---
          conditionalPanel(
            condition = sprintf("input['%s'] == 'signup'", ns("mode")),
            div(id = ns("signup_form"),
                div(class = "form-group-professional",
                    tags$label("FULL NAME"),
                    textInput(ns("su_name"), NULL, placeholder = "Enter your full name")
                ),
                div(class = "form-group-professional",
                    tags$label("EMAIL ADDRESS"),
                    textInput(ns("su_email"), NULL, placeholder = "your.email@example.com")
                ),
                div(class = "form-group-professional",
                    tags$label("PASSWORD"),
                    passwordInput(ns("su_password"), NULL, placeholder = "Create a strong password")
                ),
                
                div(class = "row",
                    div(class = "col-md-6",
                        div(class = "form-group-professional",
                            tags$label("MOBILE NUMBER"),
                            textInput(ns("su_mobile"), NULL, placeholder = "+92 3XX XXXXXXX")
                        )
                    ),
                    div(class = "col-md-6",
                        div(class = "form-group-professional",
                            tags$label("GENDER"),
                            shinyWidgets::radioGroupButtons(ns("su_gender"), NULL,
                                                            choices = c("Male", "Female"),
                                                            selected = "Male")
                        )
                    )
                ),
                
                div(class = "row",
                    div(class = "col-md-6",
                        div(class = "form-group-professional",
                            tags$label("PREPARATION LEVEL"),
                            selectInput(ns("su_prep"), NULL, 
                                        c("Beginner","Intermediate","Advanced"))
                        )
                    ),
                    div(class = "col-md-6",
                        div(class = "form-group-professional",
                            tags$label("TARGET EXAM YEAR"),
                            numericInput(ns("su_year"), NULL,
                                         value = lubridate::year(Sys.Date()) + 1,
                                         min = lubridate::year(Sys.Date()),
                                         max = lubridate::year(Sys.Date()) + 5, 
                                         step = 1)
                        )
                    )
                ),
                
                div(class = "form-group-professional",
                    tags$label("OPTIONAL SUBJECTS (SELECT UP TO 6)"),
                    shinyWidgets::pickerInput(ns("su_optional"),
                                              NULL,
                                              choices = optional_choices, 
                                              multiple = TRUE,
                                              options = list(maxOptions = 6, `live-search` = TRUE,
                                                             `actions-box` = TRUE,
                                                             `selected-text-format` = "count > 2",
                                                             `count-selected-text` = "{0} subjects selected"))
                ),
                
                div(class = "form-group-professional",
                    tags$label("CITY (OPTIONAL)"),
                    textInput(ns("su_city"), NULL, placeholder = "Enter your city")
                ),
                
                actionButton(ns("do_signup"), "Create Your CSS Buddy Account", 
                             class = "btn-professional-success"),
                
            )
          ),
          
          div(class = "mt-4 text-center", uiOutput(ns("auth_msg")))
      )
  )
}

# Keep the same server logic but add debug output
mod_auth_server <- function(id, conn, optional_subjects){
  moduleServer(id, function(input, output, session){
    ns <- session$ns
    logged_in <- reactiveVal(FALSE)
    user <- reactiveVal(NULL)
    profile <- reactiveVal(NULL)
    
    # Switch between signin and signup modes
    observeEvent(input$go_signup, { 
      updateRadioButtons(session, "mode", selected = "signup") 
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$go_signin, { 
      updateRadioButtons(session, "mode", selected = "signin") 
    })
    
    # --- Sign In ---
    observeEvent(input$do_signin, ignoreInit = TRUE, {
      output$auth_msg <- renderUI(NULL)
      em <- normalize_email(input$si_email %||% "")
      pw <- trimws(input$si_password %||% "")
      if (!nzchar(em) || !grepl(".+@.+\\..+", em)) {
        output$auth_msg <- renderUI(div(class = "alert alert-danger alert-professional", "Please enter a valid email.")); return()
      }
      if (!nzchar(pw)) {
        output$auth_msg <- renderUI(div(class = "alert alert-danger alert-professional", "Please enter your password.")); return()
      }
      
      u <- try(verify_user(conn, em, pw), silent = TRUE)
      if (inherits(u, "try-error") || is.null(u)) {
        output$auth_msg <- renderUI(div(class = "alert alert-danger alert-professional", "Invalid email or password.")); return()
      }
      
      user(u)
      p <- get_profile(conn, u$id)
      if (is.null(p)) {
        p <- upsert_profile(conn, u$id,
                            exam_type = "CSS",
                            exam_year = lubridate::year(Sys.Date()) + 1,
                            prep_level = "Beginner",
                            city = NA, mobile = NA, gender = NA)
      }
      refresh_user_env(conn)
      profile(p); logged_in(TRUE)
    })
    
    # --- Sign Up ---
    observeEvent(input$do_signup, ignoreInit = TRUE, {
      output$auth_msg <- renderUI(NULL)
      nm <- trimws(input$su_name %||% "")
      em <- normalize_email(input$su_email %||% "")
      pw <- trimws(input$su_password %||% "")
      
      if (!nzchar(em) || !grepl(".+@.+\\..+", em)) {
        output$auth_msg <- renderUI(div(class = "alert alert-danger alert-professional", "Please enter a valid email.")); return()
      }
      if (nchar(pw) < 6) {
        output$auth_msg <- renderUI(div(class = "alert alert-danger alert-professional", "Password must be at least 6 characters.")); return()
      }
      mob <- trimws(input$su_mobile %||% "")
      if (nzchar(mob) && !grepl("^[0-9+ ()-]{7,}$", mob)) {
        output$auth_msg <- renderUI(div(class = "alert alert-danger alert-professional", "Please enter a valid mobile number.")); return()
      }
      
      # Debug the input values
      cat("DEBUG: Signup form submitted\n")
      cat("DEBUG: Selected optional subjects:", paste(input$su_optional, collapse=", "), "\n")
      cat("DEBUG: Number of selected subjects:", length(input$su_optional), "\n")
      
      u <- try(create_user(conn, nm, em, pw), silent = TRUE)
      if (inherits(u, "try-error")) {
        msg <- tryCatch(as.character(attr(u, "condition")$message), error = function(e) "Signup failed. Try another email.")
        output$auth_msg <- renderUI(div(class = "alert alert-danger alert-professional", msg)); return()
      }
      
      p <- upsert_profile(conn, u$id,
                          exam_type = "CSS",
                          exam_year = input$su_year,
                          prep_level = input$su_prep,
                          city = input$su_city %||% NA,
                          mobile = mob %||% NA,
                          gender = input$su_gender %||% NA)
      
      # FIX: Ensure we're passing all selected subjects correctly
      selected_subjects <- input$su_optional
      if (is.null(selected_subjects)) {
        selected_subjects <- character()
      }
      
      cat("DEBUG: Passing to upsert_user_optionals:", paste(selected_subjects, collapse=", "), "\n")
      cat("DEBUG: Number of subjects to pass:", length(selected_subjects), "\n")
      
      # Save normalized optionals mapping - USE THE CORRECT FUNCTION FROM utils_db.R
      upsert_user_optionals(conn, u$id, selected_subjects)
      
      refresh_user_env(conn)
      user(u); profile(p); logged_in(TRUE)
    })
    
    # -- Public reset so parent can re-arm the module after logout/open --
    reset_auth <- function(clear_inputs = TRUE){
      logged_in(FALSE)
      user(NULL); profile(NULL)
      output$auth_msg <- renderUI(NULL)
      if (clear_inputs) {
        # Clear visible inputs via update*; modal will be re-rendered anyway on show
        updateTextInput(session, "si_email", value = "")
        updateTextInput(session, "su_name", value = "")
        updateTextInput(session, "su_email", value = "")
        updateTextInput(session, "su_mobile", value = "")
        updateTextInput(session, "su_city", value = "")
        updateSelectInput(session, "su_prep", selected = "Beginner")
        updateNumericInput(session, "su_year", value = lubridate::year(Sys.Date()) + 1)
        updateRadioButtons(session, "mode", selected = "signin")
      }
      invisible(TRUE)
    }
    
    list(logged_in = logged_in, user = user, profile = profile, reset = reset_auth)
  })
}

# ---- Database Functions ----

# Normalize email
normalize_email <- function(email) {
  tolower(trimws(email %||% ""))
}

# Create user
create_user <- function(conn, name, email, password) {
  email_norm <- normalize_email(email)
  pw_hash <- sodium::password_store(password)
  
  # Check if user already exists
  existing <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id FROM users WHERE email = ?", 
                              params = list(email_norm))
  if (nrow(existing) > 0) {
    stop("User with this email already exists")
  }
  
  # Insert new user
  DBI::dbExecute(conn,
                 "INSERT INTO users (name, email, password_hash, created_at) 
                 VALUES (?, ?, ?, datetime('now'))",
                 params = list(name, email_norm, pw_hash))
  
  # Get the new user
  user_id <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT last_insert_rowid() AS id")$id
  list(id = user_id, name = name, email = email_norm)
}

# Verify user
verify_user <- function(conn, email, password) {
  email_norm <- normalize_email(email)
  user <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, 
                          "SELECT id, name, email, password_hash FROM users WHERE email = ?",
                          params = list(email_norm))
  
  if (nrow(user) == 0) return(NULL)
  
  if (sodium::password_verify(password, user$password_hash[1])) {
    list(id = user$id[1], name = user$name[1], email = user$email[1])
  } else {
    NULL
  }
}

# Get user profile - FIXED: Use the same structure as utils_db.R
get_profile <- function(conn, user_id) {
  # Get profile
  p <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT * FROM profiles WHERE user_id = ?", 
                       params = list(user_id))
  if (nrow(p) == 0) return(NULL)
  
  # Get optional subjects - FIXED: properly get multiple optional subjects
  optionals <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, 
                               "SELECT o.name 
                                FROM user_optionals uo 
                                JOIN optionals o ON o.id = uo.subject_id 
                                WHERE uo.user_id = ?", 
                               params = list(user_id))
  
  # Return as data frame with list column to match utils_db.R structure
  p$optional_subjects <- list(if (nrow(optionals) > 0) optionals$name else character())
  p[1,]
}

# Upsert profile
upsert_profile <- function(conn, user_id, exam_type, exam_year, prep_level, city, mobile = NA, gender = NA) {
  now <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  has <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT 1 FROM profiles WHERE user_id = ?", params = list(user_id))
  if (!nrow(has)){
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "INSERT INTO profiles (user_id, exam_type, exam_year, prep_level, city, mobile, gender, updated_at)
                     VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
                   params = list(user_id, exam_type, exam_year, prep_level, city, mobile, gender, now))
  } else {
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "UPDATE profiles SET exam_type=?, exam_year=?, prep_level=?, city=?, mobile=?, gender=?, updated_at=? WHERE user_id = ?",
                   params = list(exam_type, exam_year, prep_level, city, mobile, gender, now, user_id))
  }
  get_profile(conn, user_id)
}

# Get optional subject IDs for subject names
subject_ids_for <- function(conn, subject_names){
  if (!length(subject_names)) return(integer())
  placeholders <- paste(rep("?", length(subject_names)), collapse = ",")
  query <- sprintf("SELECT id, name FROM optionals WHERE name IN (%s)", placeholders)
  q <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, query, params = as.list(subject_names))
  q$id[match(subject_names, q$name)]
}

# Upsert user optionals - FIXED: Use the same logic as utils_db.R
upsert_user_optionals <- function(conn, user_id, subject_names) {
  # Debug output
  cat("DEBUG: upsert_user_optionals called with user_id:", user_id, "and subjects:", paste(subject_names, collapse=", "), "\n")
  
  # Clear existing optionals for this user
  DBI::dbExecute(conn, "DELETE FROM user_optionals WHERE user_id = ?", params = list(user_id))
  
  if (!length(subject_names)) {
    cat("DEBUG: No subjects to insert\n")
    return(invisible(TRUE))
  }
  
  # Get subject IDs
  sids <- subject_ids_for(conn, unique(subject_names))
  cat("DEBUG: Found subject IDs:", paste(sids, collapse=", "), "\n")
  
  if (!length(sids)) {
    cat("DEBUG: No valid subject IDs found\n")
    return(invisible(TRUE))
  }
  
  # Use transaction for safety
  DBI::dbExecute(conn, "BEGIN TRANSACTION")
  tryCatch({
    for (sid in sids) {
      cat("DEBUG: Inserting user_id:", user_id, "subject_id:", sid, "\n")
      DBI::dbExecute(conn, 
                     "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO user_optionals (user_id, subject_id) VALUES (?, ?)",
                     params = list(user_id, sid))
    }
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "COMMIT")
    cat("DEBUG: Successfully inserted", length(sids), "subjects\n")
  }, error = function(e) {
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "ROLLBACK")
    cat("DEBUG: Error inserting subjects:", e$message, "\n")
    stop("Failed to save optional subjects: ", e$message)
  })
  
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# Get user's optional subjects
get_user_optionals <- function(conn, user_id) {
  DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, 
                  "SELECT o.name FROM user_optionals uo 
                   JOIN optionals o ON o.id = uo.subject_id 
                   WHERE uo.user_id = ? 
                   ORDER BY o.name",
                  params = list(user_id))$name
}

# Refresh user environment
refresh_user_env <- function(conn) {
  # This function can be used to refresh any user-specific environment variables
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# Create tables if they don't exist - FIXED: Use consistent column names with utils_db.R
create_tables <- function(conn) {
  # Users table
  DBI::dbExecute(conn, "
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      name TEXT NOT NULL,
      email TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
      password_hash TEXT NOT NULL,
      created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
      updated_at TEXT
    )
  ")
  
  # Profiles table - REMOVED optional_subjects_text column
  DBI::dbExecute(conn, "
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS profiles (
      user_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
      exam_type TEXT DEFAULT 'CSS',
      exam_year INTEGER,
      prep_level TEXT,
      city TEXT,
      mobile TEXT,
      gender TEXT,
      updated_at TEXT,
      FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    )
  ")
  
  # Optionals table
  DBI::dbExecute(conn, "
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS optionals (
      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      name TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL
    )
  ")
  
  # User-optionals relationship table - FIXED: Use subject_id column name to match utils_db.R
  DBI::dbExecute(conn, "
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS user_optionals (
      user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
      subject_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (user_id, subject_id),
      FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
      FOREIGN KEY(subject_id) REFERENCES optionals(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    )
  ")
  
  # Create indexes
  DBI::dbExecute(conn, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_user_optionals_user ON user_optionals(user_id)")
  DBI::dbExecute(conn, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_user_optionals_subject ON user_optionals(subject_id)")
  
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# Remove legacy optional_subjects_text column from profiles table
remove_legacy_optional_subjects_column <- function(conn) {
  # Check if the legacy column exists
  cols <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "PRAGMA table_info(profiles)")$name
  if ("optional_subjects_text" %in% cols) {
    cat("Removing legacy optional_subjects_text column from profiles table...\n")
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE profiles_new AS SELECT user_id, exam_type, exam_year, prep_level, city, mobile, gender, updated_at FROM profiles")
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "DROP TABLE profiles")
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "ALTER TABLE profiles_new RENAME TO profiles")
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_profiles_user ON profiles(user_id)")
    cat("Legacy column removed successfully\n")
  }
}

# Seed optional subjects
seed_optionals <- function(conn, optional_subjects) {
  # Insert optional subjects if they don't exist
  for (subject in optional_subjects) {
    DBI::dbExecute(conn,
                   "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO optionals (name) VALUES (?)",
                   params = list(subject))
  }
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# Migrate from JSON optional subjects to proper relational structure
migrate_optionals_json <- function(conn){
  # Check if old optional_subjects column exists in profiles
  cols <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "PRAGMA table_info(profiles)")$name
  if (!"optional_subjects" %in% cols) return(invisible(TRUE))
  
  # Get profiles with optional_subjects data
  rows <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, 
                          "SELECT user_id, optional_subjects FROM profiles 
                           WHERE optional_subjects IS NOT NULL 
                           AND TRIM(optional_subjects) <> ''")
  
  if (nrow(rows) == 0) return(invisible(TRUE))
  
  for (i in seq_len(nrow(rows))){
    uid <- rows$user_id[i]
    raw <- rows$optional_subjects[i]
    opts <- tryCatch(jsonlite::fromJSON(raw), error = function(e) character())
    if (length(opts)) {
      upsert_user_optionals(conn, uid, opts)
    }
  }
  
  # Remove the old column
  DBI::dbExecute(conn, "ALTER TABLE profiles DROP COLUMN optional_subjects")
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# Ensure emails are lowercase
ensure_emails_lowercased <- function(conn){
  try({ 
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "UPDATE users SET email = lower(email) WHERE email <> lower(email)") 
  }, silent = TRUE)
  invisible(TRUE)
}

`%||%` <- function(a, b) { if (!is.null(a) && !is.na(a) && length(a) > 0 && !(is.character(a) && identical(a, ""))) a else b }

      .slider-hero .inner { position:relative; z-index:2; padding: 22px 24px; }

      .slider-hero .title { display:flex; align-items:center; gap:.5rem; color:#fff; font-weight:800; letter-spacing:.2px; }

      /* Carousel sizing & text flow (responsive) */
      .info-carousel { width:100%; max-width:100%; min-width:0; }
      .info-carousel .carousel-inner { width:100%; max-width:100%; min-width:0; }
      .info-carousel .carousel-item { padding: 8px 0; max-width:100%; min-width:0; }
      .info-slide {
        display:flex; flex-direction:column; justify-content:center;
        width:100%; max-width:100%; min-width:0; min-height:150px;
        color:#fff;
      }
      .info-title {
        font-weight:800; font-size:1.22rem; line-height:1.4; margin:0;
        word-break: break-word; overflow-wrap: anywhere; white-space: normal;
      }
      .info-sub {
        font-size:.95rem; opacity:.95; margin-top:6px;
        white-space: normal; word-break: break-word; overflow-wrap: anywhere;
      }

      .chip { display:inline-flex; align-items:center; gap:.4rem; padding:.25rem .7rem; border-radius:9999px; font-weight:700; background: rgba(255,255,255,.18); }
      .chip .dot { width:8px; height:8px; border-radius:9999px; background:#fff; opacity:.9; }
      .slider-hero .carousel-indicators { margin-bottom: 0; }
      .slider-hero .carousel-indicators [data-bs-target] { background-color:#fff; }

      /* Flash 8 grid */
      .flash8root .col { display: flex; }
      .flash-card { width: 100%; min-width:0; }

      /* Flip cards */
      .flip-card { background: transparent; width: 100%; height: 190px; perspective: 1000px; cursor: pointer; min-width:0; }
      .flip-card .flip-card-inner {
        position: relative; width: 100%; height: 100%; text-align: center; min-width:0;
        transition: transform .6s; transform-style: preserve-3d; border-radius: 16px; box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,.10);
      }
      .flip-card.flipped .flip-card-inner { transform: rotateY(180deg); }

      .flip-card-front, .flip-card-back {
        position: absolute; width: 100%; height: 100%; backface-visibility: hidden; border-radius: 16px;
        display:flex; flex-direction:column; align-items:center; justify-content:center; padding: 14px;
      }
      .flip-card-front { color: #fff; }
      .flip-card-back  { background: var(--surface, #fff); color: var(--text, #0F172A); transform: rotateY(180deg);
        border: 1px solid var(--ring, #E6EBF4); }

      .flip-card.theme-vocab .flip-card-front { background: linear-gradient(135deg, #4F46E5, #8B5CF6); }
      .flip-card.theme-gk    .flip-card-front { background: linear-gradient(135deg, #22D3EE, #4F46E5); }

      .flash-tag { position:absolute; top:10px; left:12px; padding:2px 8px; font-size:.72rem; letter-spacing:.06em;
        border-radius:9999px; background: rgba(255,255,255,.22); color:#fff; border: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.35); }

      .flash-main { font-size: 1rem; line-height: 1.35; }
      .flash-main .word { font-size: 1.25rem; font-weight: 800; }

      .flash-main .subj { margin-top: 8px; font-size: .8rem; opacity: .75; }

      @media (max-width: 575.98px){
        .flip-card { height: 170px; }
        .info-title { font-size:1.06rem; }
      }

      /* === Latest Uploads (options + correct highlight + pager) === */
      .mcq-card { margin-bottom: .5rem; padding: .75rem; border: 1px solid #E6EBF4; border-radius: .75rem; }
      .mcq-head { display:flex; justify-content:space-between; gap:.5rem; font-size:.85rem; color:#64748b; margin-bottom:.25rem; }
      .mcq-q { font-weight:600; }
      .mcq-opts { margin:.4rem 0 0 0; padding-left: 1rem; }
      .mcq-opt { margin:.15rem 0; }
      .mcq-opt.correct { font-weight:700; background:#ecfdf5; border-left: 4px solid #10b981; padding:.15rem .4rem; border-radius:.3rem; }

      /* controls */
      .latest-controls { display:flex; align-items:center; gap:.5rem; flex-wrap:wrap; }
      .latest-controls .form-select { height: 31px; padding:.15rem .5rem; }
      .pager { display:flex; align-items:center; justify-content:space-between; gap:.5rem; margin-top:.75rem; flex-wrap:wrap; }
      .pager-right { display:flex; align-items:center; gap:.5rem; flex-wrap:wrap; }
      .pager .form-control { height:31px; padding:.15rem .5rem; width: 90px; }

      @media (max-width: 575.98px){
        .mcq-head { flex-direction:column; align-items:flex-start; gap:.2rem; }
      }
    ")),
    
    # JS (flip + carousel; robust 5s autoplay on first render & re-render)
    tags$script(HTML(sprintf("
      (function(inputName){
        document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
          var card = e.target.closest('.flash8root .flip-card');
          if(!card) return;
          card.classList.toggle('flipped');
          var payload = { id: card.getAttribute('data-card-id'), flipped: card.classList.contains('flipped'), t: Date.now() };
          if(window.Shiny && inputName){ Shiny.setInputValue(inputName, payload, {priority:'event'}); }
        });
      })('%s');

      (function(){
        function ensureCarousel(id){
          var el = document.getElementById(id); if(!el) return;
          var ms = parseInt(el.dataset.interval || el.getAttribute('data-bs-interval') || '5000', 10) || 5000;
          try{
            if(window.bootstrap && window.bootstrap.Carousel){
              var inst = window.bootstrap.Carousel.getOrCreateInstance(el, {
                interval: ms, ride: true, pause: false, wrap: true, touch: true
              });
              try{ inst.cycle(); }catch(e){}
              setTimeout(function(){ try{ inst.cycle(); }catch(e){} }, 100);
              setTimeout(function(){ try{ inst.next();  }catch(e){} }, ms);
            }
          }catch(e){}
          if(el._autotick){ clearInterval(el._autotick); el._autotick = null; }
          el._autotick = setInterval(function(){
            try{
              if(window.bootstrap && window.bootstrap.Carousel){
                window.bootstrap.Carousel.getOrCreateInstance(el).next();
              }
            }catch(e){}
          }, ms);
        }
        function init(){ ensureCarousel('%s'); }
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
        window.addEventListener('load', init);
        if(window.Shiny){
          Shiny.addCustomMessageHandler('cssbuddy:init-carousel', function(id){ ensureCarousel(id); });
          document.addEventListener('shiny:connected', init);
          document.addEventListener('shiny:value', function(ev){
            var t = ev && ev.target; if(!t) return;
            if(t.id && t.id.endsWith('%s')) { init(); }
          });
        }
        var mo = new MutationObserver(function(){
          var el = document.getElementById('%s');
          if(el && !el._autoinited){ el._autoinited = true; init(); }
        });
        mo.observe(document.documentElement, {childList:true, subtree:true});
      })();
    ", ns("flip_evt"), ns("infoCarousel"), ns("infoCarousel"), ns("infoCarousel")))),
    
    # Hero wrapper (slider rendered inside)
    div(class = "hero p-4 p-md-5 mb-3 rounded-3",
        div(class = "slider-hero mb-3",
            div(class = "hero-bg"),
            div(class = "hero-overlay"),
            div(class = "inner",
                div(class = "d-flex align-items-center justify-content-between mb-2",
                    div(class = "title", icon("bullhorn"), span("Today’s Highlights"))
                ),
                uiOutput(ns("promo_slider"))
            )
        )
    ),
    
    # Flash 8-Pack
    div(class = "card-soft p-3 mt-3",
        h5(icon("bolt"), " Daily Flash 8-Pack"),
        div(id = ns("flash8root"), class = "flash8root",
            div(class = "row row-cols-1 row-cols-sm-2 row-cols-lg-4 g-3",
                do.call(tagList, lapply(1:8, function(i){
                  theme_cls <- if (i <= 4) "theme-vocab" else "theme-gk"
                  div(class = "col",
                      div(class = paste("flip-card flash-card", theme_cls),
                          `data-card-id` = i,
                          div(class = "flip-card-inner",
                              div(class = "flip-card-front",
                                  span(class="flash-tag", uiOutput(ns(paste0("tag_", i)), inline = TRUE)),
                                  div(class = "flash-main", uiOutput(ns(paste0("front_", i))))
                              ),
                              div(class = "flip-card-back",
                                  div(class = "flash-main", uiOutput(ns(paste0("back_", i))))
                              )
                          )
                      )
                  )
                }))
            )
        )
    ),
    
    # Latest uploads (DB Subject filter + Go To Page in Pager + Pagination)
    div(class="card-soft p-3 mt-3",
        div(class="d-flex align-items-center justify-content-between mb-2 flex-wrap gap-2",
            h5(class="mb-0", icon("clock-rotate-left"), " Latest Uploads"),
            div(class="latest-controls",
                uiOutput(ns("subject_filter_ui"))   # Rendered from DB
            )
        ),
        uiOutput(ns("recent_list")),
        uiOutput(ns("recent_pager"))
    )
  )
}

# ---------- SERVER ----------
mod_dashboard_server <- function(id, conn,
                                 user_profile = reactive(list(name = NULL, prep_level = NULL, exam_year = NULL)),
                                 exam_date = reactive(NULL),
                                 streak_value = reactive(0L)){
  moduleServer(id, function(input, output, session){
    ns <- session$ns
    
    # Safe SQL
    safe_q <- function(sql, params = NULL){
      tryCatch({
        if (is.null(params)) DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, sql) else DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, sql, params = params)
      }, error = function(e){ message("SQL error: ", conditionMessage(e)); data.frame() })
    }
    
    # -------- Slider content --------
    news_headlines_from_db <- function(limit = 12){
      has_news <- tryCatch({
        cols <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "PRAGMA table_info(news_cache)")$name
        "title" %in% cols
      }, error = function(e) FALSE)
      if (!isTRUE(has_news)) return(list())
      
      df <- safe_q("
        SELECT title, source, url, ts
        FROM news_cache
        WHERE TRIM(IFNULL(title,'')) <> ''
        ORDER BY COALESCE(ts, datetime('now')) DESC
        LIMIT 50
      ")
      if (!nrow(df)) return(list())
      
      out <- list()
      n <- min(nrow(df), limit)
      for (i in seq_len(n)){
        title <- htmltools::htmlEscape(df$title[i] %||% "")
        src   <- htmltools::htmlEscape(df$source[i] %||% "")
        url   <- df$url[i] %||% ""
        stamp <- htmltools::htmlEscape(df$ts[i] %||% "")
        if (nzchar(url)) {
          out[[length(out)+1]] <- sprintf(
            "<div class='info-slide'><div class='chip'><span class='dot'></span>News • %s</div>
             <div class='info-title'><a href='%s' target='_blank' rel='noopener' style='color:#fff;text-decoration:underline;'>%s</a></div>
             <div class='info-sub'>%s</div></div>",
            src, htmltools::htmlEscape(url), title, stamp
          )
        } else {
          out[[length(out)+1]] <- sprintf(
            "<div class='info-slide'><div class='chip'><span class='dot'></span>News • %s</div>
             <div class='info-title'>%s</div><div class='info-sub'>%s</div></div>",
            src, title, stamp
          )
        }
      }
      out
    }
    
    # Pools (quotes/idioms)
    quotes_pool <- list(
      list(q="What we know is a drop; what we don't is an ocean.", a="Isaac Newton"),
      list(q="Well begun is half done.", a="Aristotle"),
      list(q="It always seems impossible until it’s done.", a="Nelson Mandela"),
      list(q="The secret of getting ahead is getting started.", a="Mark Twain"),
      list(q="Quality is not an act, it is a habit.", a="Aristotle"),
      list(q="A river cuts through rock not because of its power, but because of its persistence.", a="Jim Watkins"),
      list(q="You don’t have to be great to start, but you have to start to be great.", a="Zig Ziglar"),

      list(q="Genius is 1% inspiration and 99% perspiration.", a="Thomas Edison"),
      list(q="The only way to do great work is to love what you do.", a="Steve Jobs"),
      list(q="Success is the sum of small efforts, repeated day in and day out.", a="Robert Collier"),
