# ====================== SERVER ======================
mod_essay_server <- function(id, conn, is_logged_in, user = NULL, is_admin = NULL, ...){
  moduleServer(id, function(input, output, session){
    ns <- session$ns
    
    # Use session-level tracking to prevent duplicate module execution
    if (!is.null(session$userData$essay_module_initialized)) {
      return()
    }
    session$userData$essay_module_initialized <- TRUE
    
    cat("=== ESSAY MODULE INITIALIZED ===\n")
    
    # ---------- Storage path for PDFs ----------
    base_dir <- normalizePath(file.path(getwd(), "essay_uploads"), mustWork = FALSE)
    if (!dir.exists(base_dir)) dir.create(base_dir, recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)
    try(addResourcePath("essays", base_dir), silent = TRUE)
    
    # ---------- Resolve current user id / admin flag ----------
    uid_now <- reactive({
      if (!is.null(user) && is.function(user)) {
        u <- try(user(), silent = TRUE)
        id <- try(u$id, silent = TRUE)
        if (is.numeric(id) && length(id) == 1) return(as.integer(id))
      }
      u2 <- try(session$userData$auth_uid, silent = TRUE)
      if (is.numeric(u2) && length(u2) == 1) return(as.integer(u2))
      NA_integer_
    })
    
    is_admin_now <- reactive({
      if (!is.null(is_admin) && is.function(is_admin)) return(isTRUE(try(is_admin(), silent = TRUE)))
      isTRUE(try(session$userData$is_admin_flag, silent = TRUE))
    })
    
    # ---------- DB helpers ----------
    db_cols <- function(table){
      tryCatch(DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, sprintf("PRAGMA table_info(%s)", table))$name, error = function(e) character())
    }
    
    insert_pdf_once <- function(user_id, topic_id, pdf_name, pdf_type, pdf_size, pdf_relpath_or_abs, file_abs_path){
      cat("=== STARTING DATABASE INSERT ===\n")
      cat("User ID:", user_id, "\n")
      cat("Topic ID:", topic_id, "\n")
      cat("PDF Name:", pdf_name, "\n")
      
      # Use immediate transaction for better locking
      DBI::dbExecute(conn, "BEGIN IMMEDIATE TRANSACTION")
      cat("Transaction started\n")
      
      tryCatch({
        # More comprehensive duplicate check with file content
        existing <- tryCatch({
          DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, 
                          "SELECT id FROM essays WHERE user_id = ? AND pdf_name = ? AND submitted_at > datetime('now', '-30 seconds')",
                          params = list(as.integer(user_id), pdf_name)
          )
        }, error = function(e) {
          cat("Duplicate check error:", e$message, "\n")
          data.frame()
        })
        
        cat("Duplicate check found", nrow(existing), "existing records\n")
        
        if (nrow(existing) > 0) {
          DBI::dbExecute(conn, "ROLLBACK")
          cat("Duplicate detected - rolling back\n")
          showNotification("This file was already submitted recently.", type = "warning")
          return(FALSE)
        }
        
        # Insert the record
        now <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
        cols <- db_cols("essays")
        cat("Available columns:", paste(cols, collapse = ", "), "\n")
        
        values <- list(
          user_id = as.integer(user_id),
          topic_id = if (is.na(topic_id)) NA else as.integer(topic_id),
          mode = "pdf",
          pdf_name = pdf_name %||% "",
          pdf_type = pdf_type %||% "",
          pdf_size = as.integer(pdf_size %||% NA),
          started_at = now,
          submitted_at = now,
          is_marked = 0L
        )
        
        # Add pdf_path if the column exists
        if ("pdf_path" %in% cols) {
          values$pdf_path <- pdf_relpath_or_abs %||% ""
        }
        
        # Determine which columns to keep
        keep <- intersect(names(values), cols)
        cat("Columns to insert:", paste(keep, collapse = ", "), "\n")
        
        if (!length(keep)) {
          DBI::dbExecute(conn, "ROLLBACK")
          cat("No matching columns - rolling back\n")
          stop("No matching columns for PDF insert.")
        }
        
        # Build SQL and parameters
        sql <- paste0("INSERT INTO essays(", paste(keep, collapse=","), ") VALUES(",
                      paste(rep("?", length(keep)), collapse=","), ")")
        params <- lapply(keep, function(k) values[[k]])
        
        cat("Executing SQL:", sql, "\n")
        
        # Execute the insert
        result <- DBI::dbExecute(conn, sql, params = params)
        cat("Insert result:", result, "\n")
        
        # Commit transaction
        DBI::dbExecute(conn, "COMMIT")
        cat("Transaction committed successfully\n")
        return(TRUE)
        
      }, error = function(e) {
        DBI::dbExecute(conn, "ROLLBACK")
        cat("Transaction error - rolling back:", e$message, "\n")
        showNotification(paste("Database error:", e$message), type = "error")
        return(FALSE)
      })
    }
    
    db_get_categories <- function(){
      ch <- tryCatch(essay_get_categories(conn), error = function(e) character())
      unique(ch[!is.na(ch) & nzchar(ch)])
    }
    
    db_get_topics   <- function(cat = NA_character_){ 
      tryCatch(essay_get_topics(conn, category = cat), error = function(e) tibble()) 
    }
    
    db_list_user <- function(user_id){
      tryCatch({
        DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "
          SELECT DISTINCT e.*, t.title AS topic_title, t.category AS topic_category
          FROM essays e
          LEFT JOIN essay_topics t ON t.id = e.topic_id
          WHERE e.user_id = ?
          ORDER BY e.submitted_at DESC, e.id DESC
        ", params = list(as.integer(user_id)))
      }, error = function(e) tibble())
    }
    
    db_get_one <- function(essay_id, user_id){
      tryCatch({
        df <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "
          SELECT e.*, t.title AS topic_title, t.category AS topic_category
          FROM essays e
          LEFT JOIN essay_topics t ON t.id = e.topic_id
          WHERE e.id = ? AND e.user_id = ?
          LIMIT 1
        ", params = list(as.integer(essay_id), as.integer(user_id)))
        if (nrow(df)) df[1,] else NULL
      }, error = function(e) NULL)
    }
    
    db_delete_essay <- function(essay_id, user_id){
      tryCatch({
        cat("=== STARTING DELETE OPERATION ===\n")
        cat("Essay ID to delete:", essay_id, "\n")
        cat("User ID:", user_id, "\n")
        
        # First get the essay details to delete the file
        essay <- db_get_one(essay_id, user_id)
        cat("Essay found for deletion:", !is.null(essay), "\n")
        
        if (!is.null(essay) && "pdf_path" %in% names(essay) && nzchar(essay$pdf_path %||% "")) {
          # Extract filename from path and delete the file
          file_path <- file.path(base_dir, gsub("^essays/", "", essay$pdf_path))
          cat("File path to delete:", file_path, "\n")
          cat("File exists:", file.exists(file_path), "\n")
          
          if (file.exists(file_path)) {
            file.remove(file_path)
            cat("File deleted successfully\n")
          }
        }
        
        # Delete from database
        result <- DBI::dbExecute(conn, "DELETE FROM essays WHERE id = ? AND user_id = ? AND is_marked = 0",
                                 params = list(as.integer(essay_id), as.integer(user_id)))
        cat("Database delete result (rows affected):", result, "\n")
        
        success <- result > 0
        cat("Delete operation successful:", success, "\n")
        return(success)
        
      }, error = function(e) {
        cat("Delete operation error:", e$message, "\n")
        FALSE
      })
    }
    
    # --------------- UI blocks ---------------
    login_gate_ui <- div(class = "login-gate",
                         div(class = "essay-card login-card",
                             div(class = "login-icon", icon("file-pdf")),
                             h3("Essay Writing"),
                             p("Upload your handwritten essays for evaluation by our expert team."),
                             p(class = "text-muted", "Please sign in to access the essay submission system."),
                             p(class = "text-muted", "Use the login button in the top-right menu to continue.")
                         )
    )
    
    # Modern file upload block
    upload_block <- tagList(
      # Hero Section with impressive styling
      div(class = "essay-hero",
          h1(icon("pen-fancy", class = "me-3"), "Essay Writing"),
          p("Upload your handwritten essay for evaluation. Our expert team includes",
            span(class = "expert-highlight", "CSPs and Subject Specialists"),
            "who will evaluate and provide you with free assistance and feedback."
          )
      ),
      
      # Upload form in one row with two equal columns
      div(class = "essay-card mb-4",
          h4(class = "essay-subtitle", "Upload Your Essay"),
          fluidRow(
            # Category Selection Column
            column(6,
                   div(class = "mb-3",
                       tags$label(class = "form-label required-field", "Select Category"),
                       pickerInput(ns("category"), NULL,
                                   choices = character(0), 
                                   multiple = FALSE,
                                   options = list(`live-search` = TRUE, size = 8))
                   ),
                   uiOutput(ns("topic_ui"))
            ),
            
            # PDF Upload Column
            column(6,
                   div(class = "mb-3",
                       tags$label(class = "form-label required-field", "Upload PDF File"),
                       div(class = "file-input-wrapper", id = ns("file_drop_zone"),
                           div(class = "file-input-icon", icon("cloud-upload-alt")),
                           div(class = "file-input-text", "Choose PDF file or drag & drop here"),
                           div(class = "file-input-hint", "Maximum file size: 10MB • Supported format: PDF"),
                           fileInput(ns("pdf_file"), NULL, 
                                     accept = c(".pdf"), 
                                     multiple = FALSE,
                                     buttonLabel = "Browse Files", 
                                     placeholder = "No file selected",
                                     width = "100%")
                       )
                   )
            )
          ),
          
          # Submit button centered below
          div(class = "d-grid gap-2 mt-4",
              actionButton(ns("submit_pdf"), "Submit Essay for Evaluation", 
                           class = "btn btn-primary btn-lg",
                           icon = icon("paper-plane"))
          )
      )
    )
    
    main_app_ui <- tagList(
      # Upload Section
      upload_block,
      
      # History Section with buttons at top right - REMOVED REFRESH BUTTON
      div(class = "essay-card mt-4",
          div(class = "section-header",
              h4(class = "section-title", "My Submissions"),
              div(class = "section-actions",
                  actionButton(ns("open_selected"), "View Selected", 
                               class = "btn btn-outline-primary btn-sm",
                               icon = icon("eye"))
              )
          ),
          div(class = "table-responsive",
              DTOutput(ns("history_tbl"))
          )
      ),
      
      # Admin Section (if applicable)
      uiOutput(ns("admin_ui"))
    )
    
    output$main_ui <- renderUI({
      if (!isTRUE(is_logged_in())) return(login_gate_ui)
      main_app_ui
    })
    
    # --------- File upload drag & drop enhancement ---------
    observe({
      if (!isTRUE(is_logged_in())) return()
      
      # Add drag and drop functionality
      session$sendCustomMessage("addDragDrop", list(
        id = ns("file_drop_zone"),
        inputId = ns("pdf_file")
      ))
    })
    
    # --------- Categories & Topics ---------
    db_get_categories_safe <- reactive({ 
      sort(unique(db_get_categories())) 
    })
    
    observe({
      if (!isTRUE(is_logged_in())) return()
      ch <- db_get_categories_safe()
      sel <- if (nzchar(input$category %||% "") && (input$category %in% ch)) input$category else (ch[1] %||% NULL)
      updatePickerInput(session, "category", choices = ch, selected = sel)
    })
    
    topics_df <- reactive({
      cat <- input$category %||% NA_character_
      db_get_topics(cat)
    })
    
    output$topic_ui <- renderUI({
      df <- topics_df()
      if (!nrow(df)) return(p("No active topics for this category.", class = "text-muted"))
      choices <- setNames(as.character(df$id), df$title)
      selectInput(ns("topic_id"), "Select Topic",
                  choices = choices,
                  selected = if ((input$topic_id %||% "") %in% as.character(df$id)) input$topic_id else as.character(df$id[1]))
    })
    
    # --------- Submit: PDF ----------
    # Session-level submission tracking to prevent duplicates
    if (is.null(session$userData$essay_submission_state)) {
      session$userData$essay_submission_state <- reactiveValues(
        in_progress = FALSE,
        last_submit_time = 0
      )
    }
    
    observeEvent(input$submit_pdf, {
      cat("=== SUBMIT BUTTON CLICKED ===\n")
      cat("Submission in progress:", session$userData$essay_submission_state$in_progress, "\n")
      cat("Time since last submit:", Sys.time() - session$userData$essay_submission_state$last_submit_time, "seconds\n")
      
      # Debounce: prevent multiple rapid clicks
      current_time <- as.numeric(Sys.time())
      if (current_time - session$userData$essay_submission_state$last_submit_time < 3) {
        cat("SUBMISSION DEBOUNCED - Too soon after last submission\n")
        showNotification("Please wait a moment before submitting again.", type = "warning")
        return()
      }
      
      # Prevent multiple simultaneous submissions
      if (isTRUE(session$userData$essay_submission_state$in_progress)) {
        cat("SUBMISSION BLOCKED - Already in progress\n")
        showNotification("Submission in progress, please wait...", type = "warning")
        return()
      }
      
      # Set submission state
      session$userData$essay_submission_state$in_progress <- TRUE
      session$userData$essay_submission_state$last_submit_time <- current_time
      cat("Setting submission_state$in_progress to TRUE\n")
      
      # Ensure state is reset even if error occurs
      on.exit({
        session$userData$essay_submission_state$in_progress <- FALSE
        cat("Reset submission_state$in_progress to FALSE\n")
      })
      
      if (!isTRUE(is_logged_in())) { 
        cat("User not logged in\n")
        showNotification("Please sign in first.", type = "error")
        return() 
      }
      
      uid <- uid_now()
      cat("User ID:", uid, "\n")
      
      if (is.na(uid)) { 
        cat("User ID is NA\n")
        showNotification("User not resolved. Please re-login.", type = "error")
        return() 
      }
      
      # Validate category selection
      if (is.null(input$category) || input$category == "") {
        cat("Category not selected\n")
        showNotification("Please select a category.", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      # Validate topic selection
      if (is.null(input$topic_id) || input$topic_id == "") {
        cat("Topic not selected\n")
        showNotification("Please select a topic.", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      f <- input$pdf_file
      cat("File input status - null:", is.null(f), " datapath:", !is.null(f) && nzchar(f$datapath), "\n")
      
      if (is.null(f) || !nzchar(f$datapath)) { 
        cat("No file selected\n")
        showNotification("Please choose a PDF file first.", type = "warning")
        return() 
      }
      
      if (!grepl("\\.pdf$", tolower(f$name))) { 
        cat("File is not PDF:", f$name, "\n")
        showNotification("File must be a PDF document.", type = "error")
        return() 
      }
      
      # Check file size (10MB limit)
      if (f$size > 10 * 1024 * 1024) {
        cat("File too large:", f$size, "bytes\n")
        showNotification("File size exceeds 10MB limit.", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      topic_id <- suppressWarnings(as.integer(input$topic_id %||% NA))
      cat("Topic ID:", topic_id, "\n")
      
      # Create user directory
      user_dir <- file.path(base_dir, paste0("user_", uid))
      if (!dir.exists(user_dir)) dir.create(user_dir, recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)
      
      # Generate safe filename with high precision timestamp
      safe_name <- gsub("[^0-9A-Za-z_.-]+", "_", f$name)
      timestamp <- round(as.numeric(Sys.time()) * 1000)  # Millisecond precision
      random_suffix <- sample(100000:999999, 1)
      fname <- paste0(timestamp, "_", random_suffix, "_", safe_name)
      dest <- file.path(user_dir, fname)
      cat("Destination file:", dest, "\n")
      
      # Copy file with verification
      ok <- FALSE
      try({ 
        file.copy(f$datapath, dest, overwrite = FALSE)
        # Verify file was copied
        if (file.exists(dest)) {
          ok <- TRUE
        }
      }, silent = TRUE)
      
      cat("File copy successful:", ok, "\n")
      
      if (!ok) { 
        showNotification("Failed to store file on server.", type = "error")
        return() 
      }
      
      # Create relative path for web access
      rel <- paste0("essays/", paste0("user_", uid, "/", fname))
      cat("Relative path:", rel, "\n")
      
      # Insert into database with enhanced duplicate prevention
      cat("Calling insert_pdf_once...\n")
      res <- insert_pdf_once(
        user_id = uid,
        topic_id = topic_id,
        pdf_name = fname,
        pdf_type = f$type %||% "application/pdf",
        pdf_size = suppressWarnings(as.integer(f$size %||% NA)),
        pdf_relpath_or_abs = rel,
        file_abs_path = dest
      )
      
      cat("Insert result:", res, "\n")
      
      if (isTRUE(res)) {
        showNotification("Essay submitted successfully! Our expert team will evaluate it soon.", type = "message")
        # Reset file input
        reset("pdf_file")
        reload_history()
      } else {
        # Error message already shown in insert_pdf_once
        # Also delete the copied file if insertion failed
        if (file.exists(dest)) {
          file.remove(dest)
          cat("Cleaned up file after failed insertion\n")
        }
      }
      
      cat("=== SUBMISSION PROCESS COMPLETED ===\n")
    })
    
    # --------- History ----------
    history <- reactiveVal(tibble())
    
    reload_history <- function(){
      cat("=== RELOADING HISTORY ===\n")
      uid <- uid_now()
      cat("User ID for history:", uid, "\n")
      
      if (is.na(uid)) { 
        cat("User ID is NA - returning empty history\n")
        history(tibble()); return() 
      }
      
      df <- db_list_user(uid)
      cat("History records found:", nrow(df), "\n")
      
      if (!nrow(df)) { 
        cat("No history records - returning empty\n")
        history(tibble()); return() 
      }
      
      # Remove duplicates by ID
      df <- df[!duplicated(df$id), ]
      cat("Records after duplicate removal:", nrow(df), "\n")
      
      # Ensure required columns exist
      if (!"topic_title" %in% names(df) && "title" %in% names(df)) df$topic_title <- df$title
      if (!"topic_category" %in% names(df) && "category" %in% names(df)) df$topic_category <- df$category
      if (!"is_marked" %in% names(df)) df$is_marked <- 0L
      if (!"marks" %in% names(df)) df$marks <- NA_real_
      if (!"feedback" %in% names(df)) df$feedback <- NA_character_
      if (!"mode" %in% names(df)) {
        df$mode <- ifelse(!is.na(df$pdf_path) & nzchar(df$pdf_path), "pdf", "text")
      }
      
      title_col <- if ("topic_title" %in% names(df)) df$topic_title else if ("title" %in% names(df)) df$title else rep("", nrow(df))
      category_col <- if ("topic_category" %in% names(df)) df$topic_category else if ("category" %in% names(df)) df$category else rep("", nrow(df))
      
      # FIXED: Updated status logic to show marks and feedback when marked with marks > 0
      status_html <- sapply(seq_len(nrow(df)), function(i) {
        is_marked <- isTRUE(df$is_marked[i] == 1)
        has_marks <- !is.na(df$marks[i]) && df$marks[i] > 0
        
        if (is_marked && has_marks) {
          paste0("<span class='essay-status-pill-", ns(""), " pill-marked-", ns(""), "'>✓ Evaluated (", 
                 round(df$marks[i], 1), " marks)</span>")
        } else {
          paste0("<span class='essay-status-pill-", ns(""), " pill-unmarked-", ns(""), "'>Pending Review</span>")
        }
      })
      
      when_txt <- if ("submitted_at" %in% names(df)) df$submitted_at else if ("created_at" %in% names(df)) df$created_at else rep("", nrow(df))
      
      # FIXED: Create columns for marks and feedback that show when essay is marked with marks > 0
      marks_col <- sapply(seq_len(nrow(df)), function(i) {
        is_marked <- isTRUE(df$is_marked[i] == 1)
        has_marks <- !is.na(df$marks[i]) && df$marks[i] > 0
        
        if (is_marked && has_marks) {
          as.character(round(df$marks[i], 1))
        } else {
          ""
        }
      })
      
      feedback_col <- sapply(seq_len(nrow(df)), function(i) {
        is_marked <- isTRUE(df$is_marked[i] == 1)
        has_marks <- !is.na(df$marks[i]) && df$marks[i] > 0
        has_feedback <- !is.na(df$feedback[i]) && nzchar(df$feedback[i])
        
        if (is_marked && has_marks && has_feedback) {
          # Truncate long feedback for table display
          fb <- df$feedback[i]
          if (nchar(fb) > 100) {
            fb <- paste0(substr(fb, 1, 100), "...")
          }
          fb
        } else {
          ""
        }
      })
      
      # Create delete buttons only for pending submissions
      delete_buttons <- sapply(seq_len(nrow(df)), function(i) {
        is_marked <- isTRUE(df$is_marked[i] == 1)
        has_marks <- !is.na(df$marks[i]) && df$marks[i] > 0
        
        if (!is_marked || !has_marks) {
          as.character(actionButton(
            ns(paste0("delete_", df$id[i])),
            "Delete",
            class = "btn btn-danger btn-sm",
            onclick = paste0('Shiny.setInputValue("', ns('delete_click'), '", "', df$id[i], '", {priority: "event"})')
          ))
        } else {
          ""
        }
      })
      
      out <- tibble(
        ID = df$id,
        Topic = title_col,
        Category = category_col,
        `File Name` = if ("pdf_name" %in% names(df)) df$pdf_name else "N/A",
        `Submitted` = when_txt,
        `Marks` = marks_col,
        `Feedback` = feedback_col,
        Status = status_html,
        Actions = delete_buttons
      )
      
      # Final check for duplicates
      out <- out[!duplicated(out$ID), ]
      cat("Final history rows:", nrow(out), "\n")
      
      history(out)
    }
    
    observeEvent(is_logged_in(), {
      cat("Login status changed - reloading history\n")
      if (isTRUE(is_logged_in())) reload_history()
    }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
    
    # Session-level delete tracking
    if (is.null(session$userData$essay_delete_state)) {
      session$userData$essay_delete_state <- reactiveValues(
        essay_to_delete = NULL,
        last_delete_time = 0
      )
    }
    
    # Handle delete button clicks from table
    observeEvent(input$delete_click, {
      current_time <- as.numeric(Sys.time())
      if (current_time - session$userData$essay_delete_state$last_delete_time < 1) {
        cat("DELETE CLICK DEBOUNCED - Too soon after last click\n")
        return()
      }
      session$userData$essay_delete_state$last_delete_time <- current_time
      
      cat("=== DELETE BUTTON CLICKED ===\n")
      cat("Raw delete_click value:", input$delete_click, "\n")
      
      essay_id <- as.integer(input$delete_click)
      uid <- uid_now()
      
      cat("Parsed essay ID:", essay_id, "\n")
      cat("Current user ID:", uid, "\n")
      
      if (is.na(essay_id) || is.na(uid)) {
        cat("Invalid delete request - essay_id or uid is NA\n")
        showNotification("Invalid delete request.", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      # Store the essay_id and show confirmation modal
      cat("Setting delete_state$essay_to_delete to:", essay_id, "\n")
      session$userData$essay_delete_state$essay_to_delete <- essay_id
      
      # Use a custom modal with proper ID handling
      showModal(
        modalDialog(
          title = "Confirm Deletion",
          HTML(paste0(
            "Are you sure you want to delete submission #", essay_id, "?<br>",
            "This action cannot be undone."
          )),
          footer = tagList(
            modalButton("Cancel"),
            # Use actionButton with proper namespace
            actionButton(ns("modal_confirm_delete"), "Delete", class = "btn btn-danger")
          ),
          easyClose = TRUE,
          size = "m"
        )
      )
      
      cat("Confirmation modal shown for essay ID:", essay_id, "\n")
    })
    
    # Session-level modal confirmation tracking
    if (is.null(session$userData$essay_modal_state)) {
      session$userData$essay_modal_state <- reactiveValues(
        last_modal_time = 0
      )
    }
    
    observeEvent(input$modal_confirm_delete, {
      current_time <- as.numeric(Sys.time())
      if (current_time - session$userData$essay_modal_state$last_modal_time < 1) {
        cat("MODAL CONFIRM DEBOUNCED - Too soon after last confirmation\n")
        return()
      }
      session$userData$essay_modal_state$last_modal_time <- current_time
      
      cat("=== MODAL CONFIRM DELETE BUTTON CLICKED ===\n")
      
      essay_id <- session$userData$essay_delete_state$essay_to_delete
      uid <- uid_now()
      
      cat("Attempting to delete essay ID:", essay_id, "for user ID:", uid, "\n")
      
      # Remove modal immediately
      removeModal()
      
      if (!is.null(essay_id) && !is.na(uid)) {
        # Perform deletion
        success <- db_delete_essay(essay_id, uid)
        
        if (success) {
          cat("Delete operation successful\n")
          showNotification("Submission deleted successfully.", type = "message")
          reload_history()
        } else {
          cat("Delete operation failed\n")
          showNotification("Failed to delete submission. It may have already been evaluated.", type = "error")
        }
      } else {
        cat("Invalid deletion parameters\n")
        showNotification("Invalid deletion request.", type = "error")
      }
      
      # Clean up
      session$userData$essay_delete_state$essay_to_delete <- NULL
      cat("Cleaned up essay_to_delete\n")
    })
    
    output$history_tbl <- renderDT({
      df <- history()
      cat("Rendering history table with", nrow(df), "rows\n")
      
      if (!nrow(df)) {
        df <- tibble(
          ID = integer(),
          Topic = character(),
          Category = character(),
          `File Name` = character(),
          `Submitted` = character(),
          `Marks` = character(),
          `Feedback` = character(),
          Status = character(),
          Actions = character()
        )
      }
      
      status_idx <- which(names(df) == "Status") - 1L
      actions_idx <- which(names(df) == "Actions") - 1L
      
      datatable(
        df,
        escape = which(names(df) != "Status" & names(df) != "Actions"),
        rownames = FALSE,
        selection = "single",
        options = list(
          pageLength = 10,
          scrollX = TRUE,
          dom = 'lftipr',
          language = list(
            emptyTable = "No submissions yet. Upload your first essay above!",
            zeroRecords = "No matching submissions found"
          ),
          columnDefs = list(
            list(targets = status_idx, className = "dt-center"),
            list(targets = actions_idx, className = "dt-center"),
            list(targets = 0, visible = FALSE) # Hide ID column
          )
        )
      )
    })
    
    # FIXED: View Selected button - properly displays PDF in iframe and shows marks/feedback when available
    observeEvent(input$open_selected, {
      cat("=== VIEW SELECTED BUTTON CLICKED ===\n")
      
      s <- input$history_tbl_rows_selected
      df <- history()
      
      cat("Selected row:", s, "\n")
      cat("History rows:", nrow(df), "\n")
      
      if (!length(s) || !nrow(df)) { 
        cat("No row selected or empty history\n")
        showNotification("Please select a submission first.", type = "warning")
        return() 
      }
      
      rid <- df$ID[s[1]]
      uid <- uid_now()
      
      cat("Selected essay ID:", rid, "\n")
      cat("Current user ID:", uid, "\n")
      
      row <- db_get_one(rid, uid)
      cat("Essay found:", !is.null(row), "\n")
      
      if (is.null(row)) { 
        cat("Could not load essay details\n")
        showNotification("Couldn't load submission details.", type = "error")
        return() 
      }
      
      topic_t <- row$topic_title %||% row$title %||% "Uploaded Essay"
      cat("Topic title:", topic_t, "\n")
      
      # Check if essay is marked and has marks
      is_marked <- isTRUE(row$is_marked == 1)
      has_marks <- !is.na(row$marks) && row$marks > 0
      has_feedback <- !is.na(row$feedback) && nzchar(row$feedback)
      
      # Create content for modal
      modal_content <- tagList()
      
      # Add marks and feedback section if available
      if (is_marked && has_marks) {
        marks_feedback_section <- div(
          style = "background: linear-gradient(135deg, #f0f9ff 0%, #e0f2fe 100%); border-radius: 12px; padding: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; border-left: 4px solid #0ea5e9;",
          h4(icon("star", class = "me-2"), "Evaluation Results", style = "color: #0369a1; margin-top: 0;"),
          div(
            style = "display: grid; grid-template-columns: auto 1fr; gap: 15px; align-items: start;",
            div(
              style = "background: white; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; text-align: center; box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.1);",
              h5(style = "margin: 0 0 5px 0; color: #64748b; font-size: 0.9rem;", "Marks"),
              h3(style = "margin: 0; color: #0ea5e9; font-weight: bold;", round(row$marks, 1))
            ),
            if (has_feedback) div(
              style = "background: white; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.1);",
              h5(style = "margin: 0 0 10px 0; color: #64748b; font-size: 0.9rem;", "Feedback"),
              p(style = "margin: 0; line-height: 1.5;", row$feedback)
            )
          )
        )
        modal_content <- tagAppendChild(modal_content, marks_feedback_section)
      }
      
      # Display PDF
      if ("pdf_path" %in% names(row) && nzchar(row$pdf_path %||% "")) {
        pth <- row$pdf_path
        cat("PDF path from database:", pth, "\n")
        
        # Remove leading slash if present and ensure proper path
        pth <- gsub("^/", "", pth)
        pth <- gsub("^essays/", "", pth)  # Remove essays/ prefix if present
        
        # Construct the correct URL for the resource path
        pdf_url <- paste0("essays/", pth)
        cat("Final PDF URL:", pdf_url, "\n")
        
        pdf_section <- tagList(
          div(
            style = "text-align: center; margin-bottom: 10px;",
            tags$a(href = pdf_url, target = "_blank", 
                   "Open PDF in new tab", 
                   class = "btn btn-outline-primary btn-sm")
          ),
          tags$iframe(
            src = pdf_url,
            style = "width: 100%; height: 70vh; border: none; border-radius: 8px;",
            loading = "lazy"
          )
        )
        modal_content <- tagAppendChild(modal_content, pdf_section)
      } else if ("pdf_blob" %in% names(row) && length(row$pdf_blob[[1]]) > 0) {
        # Handle blob storage
        cat("Displaying PDF from blob\n")
        b64 <- tryCatch(jsonlite::base64_enc(row$pdf_blob[[1]]), error = function(e) NULL)
        if (!is.null(b64)) {
          dataurl <- paste0("data:application/pdf;base64,", b64)
          pdf_section <- tags$iframe(
            src = dataurl,
            style = "width: 100%; height: 70vh; border: none; border-radius: 8px;",
            loading = "lazy"
          )
          modal_content <- tagAppendChild(modal_content, pdf_section)
        } else {
          cat("Failed to encode blob\n")
          showNotification("PDF available but couldn't render file.", type = "error")
        }
      } else {
        cat("No PDF path or blob found\n")
        showNotification("PDF file not found for this submission.", type = "error")
      }
      
      showModal(modalDialog(
        title = paste("Essay Submission #", row$id, "-", topic_t),
        size = "xl",
        easyClose = TRUE,
        footer = modalButton("Close"),
        modal_content
      ))
    })
    
    # ---------------- Admin: Topic management ----------------
    output$admin_ui <- renderUI({
      if (!isTRUE(is_admin_now())) return(NULL)
      
      tagList(
        div(class = "essay-card mt-4",
            h4(class = "essay-section-title", "Admin — Topic Management"),
            fluidRow(
              column(4, textInput(ns("adm_title"), "New Topic Title")),
              column(3, textInput(ns("adm_cat"), "Category")),
              column(2, actionButton(ns("adm_add"), "Add Topic", class = "btn btn-primary w-100 mt-4"))
            ),
            div(class = "table-responsive",
                DTOutput(ns("adm_tbl"))
            ),
            div(class = "mt-2",
                actionButton(ns("adm_toggle"), "Toggle Active Status", 
                             class = "btn btn-outline-secondary btn-sm")
            )
        )
      )
    })
    
    admin_data <- reactiveVal(tibble())
    admin_reload <- function(){
      if (!isTRUE(is_admin_now())) { admin_data(tibble()); return() }
      df <- tryCatch(essay_list_topics(conn), error = function(e) tibble())
      admin_data(df)
    }
    
    observeEvent(is_admin_now(), {
      if (isTRUE(is_admin_now())) admin_reload()
    }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
    
    observeEvent(input$adm_add, {
      if (!isTRUE(is_admin_now())) return()
      ttl <- input$adm_title %||% ""
      cat <- input$adm_cat   %||% ""
      if (!nzchar(ttl) || !nzchar(cat)) { 
        showNotification("Both title and category are required.", type = "warning")
        return() 
      }
      ok <- try(essay_add_topic(conn, title = ttl, category = cat, created_by = uid_now()), silent = TRUE)
      if (inherits(ok, "try-error")) {
        showNotification("Failed to add topic.", type = "error")
      } else {
        showNotification("Topic added successfully.", type = "message")
        admin_reload()
        updateTextInput(session, "adm_title", value = "")
        updateTextInput(session, "adm_cat", value = "")
      }
    })
    
    output$adm_tbl <- renderDT({
      if (!isTRUE(is_admin_now())) return(DT::datatable(data.frame()))
      df <- admin_data()
      if (!nrow(df)) df <- tibble(
        id = integer(), 
        category = character(), 
        title = character(), 
        is_active = integer(), 
        created_at = character()
      )
      datatable(
        df, 
        selection = "single", 
        options = list(pageLength = 10, scrollX = TRUE), 
        rownames = FALSE
      )
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$adm_toggle, {
      if (!isTRUE(is_admin_now())) return()
      s <- input$adm_tbl_rows_selected
      df <- admin_data()
      if (!length(s) || !nrow(df)) { 
        showNotification("Please select a topic first.", type = "warning")
        return() 
      }
      tid <- df$id[s[1]]
      ok <- try(essay_toggle_active(conn, tid), silent = TRUE)
      if (inherits(ok, "try-error")) {
        showNotification("Failed to toggle topic status.", type = "error")
      } else {
        showNotification("Topic status updated.", type = "message")
        admin_reload()
      }
    })
  })
}

# ====== Schema & helpers ======

ensure_essay_schema <- function(conn){
  try(DBI::dbExecute(conn, "PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON"), silent = TRUE)
  # Topics
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS essay_topics (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    category TEXT NOT NULL,
    title TEXT NOT NULL,
    is_active INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    created_by INTEGER,
    created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
  )")
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_topics_cat ON essay_topics(category)")
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_topics_active ON essay_topics(is_active)")
  # Essays
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS essays (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    topic_id INTEGER,
    mode TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'text', -- 'text' or 'pdf'
    content_html TEXT,
    content_text TEXT,
    word_count INTEGER,
    duration_seconds INTEGER,
    wpm REAL,
    started_at TEXT,
    submitted_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    pdf_name TEXT,
    pdf_type TEXT,
    pdf_size INTEGER,
    pdf_path TEXT,
    pdf_blob BLOB,
    is_marked INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    marked_at TEXT,
    marked_by INTEGER,
    marks REAL,
    feedback TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY(topic_id) REFERENCES essay_topics(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY(marked_by) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL
  )")
  # Add any missing columns (self-healing for older DBs)
  add <- function(nm, sql) .ensure_col(conn, "essays", nm, sql)
  add("mode", "TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'text'")
  add("pdf_name", "TEXT")
  add("pdf_type", "TEXT")
  add("pdf_size", "INTEGER")
  add("pdf_path", "TEXT")
  add("pdf_blob", "BLOB")
  add("is_marked", "INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0")
  add("marked_at", "TEXT")
  add("marked_by", "INTEGER")
  add("marks", "REAL")
  add("feedback", "TEXT")
  invisible(TRUE)
}

essay_seed_topics <- function(conn){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  already <- tryCatch(dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT COUNT(*) AS n FROM essay_topics"), error = function(e) data.frame(n=0))$n
  if (isTRUE(already > 0)) return(invisible(TRUE))
  seeds <- tibble::tribble(
    ~category,                 ~title,
    "Politics",                "Democracy and Digital Disinformation",
    "Economy",                 "Is Universal Basic Income a Viable Policy for Developing Countries?",
    "Social Issues",           "The Role of Education in Social Mobility",
    "International Relations", "Great-Power Competition in the Indo-Pacific",
    "Environment",             "Climate Change: Adaptation vs. Mitigation for Pakistan",
    "Governance",              "Civil Service Reforms: Balancing Merit and Inclusion",
    "Ethics",                  "AI Ethics: Innovation versus Regulation",
    "Security",                "Cybersecurity as a National Security Imperative"
  )
  DBI::dbWithTransaction(conn, {
    for (i in seq_len(nrow(seeds))){
      dbExecute(conn,
                "INSERT INTO essay_topics(category,title,is_active) VALUES (?,?,1)",
                params = list(seeds$category[i], seeds$title[i])
      )
    }
  })
  invisible(TRUE)
}

essay_get_categories <- function(conn){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  out <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT DISTINCT category FROM essay_topics WHERE is_active=1 ORDER BY category")$category
  unique(out[!is.na(out) & nzchar(out)])
}

essay_get_topics <- function(conn, category = NA_character_){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  if (is.na(category) || !nzchar(category)){
    dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, category, title FROM essay_topics WHERE is_active=1 ORDER BY category, title")
  } else {
    dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, category, title FROM essay_topics WHERE is_active=1 AND category=? ORDER BY title",
               params = list(category))
  }
}

essay_random_topic <- function(conn, category = NA_character_){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  if (is.na(category) || !nzchar(category)){
    dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, category, title FROM essay_topics WHERE is_active=1 ORDER BY RANDOM() LIMIT 1")
  } else {
    dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, category, title FROM essay_topics WHERE is_active=1 AND category=? ORDER BY RANDOM() LIMIT 1",
               params = list(category))
  }
}

essay_add_topic <- function(conn, title, category, created_by = NA_integer_){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  if (!nzchar(title) || !nzchar(category)) return(FALSE)
  dbExecute(conn, "INSERT INTO essay_topics(category,title,is_active,created_by) VALUES (?,?,1,?)",
            params = list(category, title, created_by %||% NA))
  TRUE
}

essay_toggle_active <- function(conn, topic_id){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  dbExecute(conn, "UPDATE essay_topics SET is_active = CASE WHEN is_active=1 THEN 0 ELSE 1 END WHERE id = ?",
            params = list(as.integer(topic_id)))
  TRUE
}

essay_list_topics <- function(conn){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, category, title, is_active, created_at FROM essay_topics ORDER BY category, title")
}

essay_insert_pdf <- function(conn, user_id, topic_id = NA, pdf_name, pdf_type = NA_character_, pdf_size = NA_integer_,
                             pdf_path = NA_character_, pdf_blob = NULL, store_mode = c("path","blob")){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  store_mode <- match.arg(store_mode)
  now <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  params <- list(
    as.integer(user_id),
    if (is.na(topic_id)) NA else as.integer(topic_id),
    "pdf",
    pdf_name %||% "",
    pdf_type %||% "",
    as.integer(pdf_size %||% NA),
    if (identical(store_mode, "path")) (pdf_path %||% "") else NA,
    if (identical(store_mode, "blob")) list(pdf_blob) else NULL,
    now, now
  )
  dbExecute(conn, "
    INSERT INTO essays(user_id, topic_id, mode, pdf_name, pdf_type, pdf_size, pdf_path, pdf_blob, started_at, submitted_at)
    VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)", params = params)
  TRUE
}

.ensure_col <- function(conn, table, col, sql){
  has <- tryCatch(dbGetQuery(conn, sprintf("PRAGMA table_info(%s)", table)), error = function(e) NULL)
  if (is.null(has)) return(invisible(FALSE))
  if (tolower(col) %in% tolower(has$name)) return(invisible(TRUE))
  dbExecute(conn, sprintf("ALTER TABLE %s ADD COLUMN %s", table, sql))
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# mod_books.R — Modern Books Marketplace UI (MEMORY OPTIMIZED FOR MOBILE)
suppressPackageStartupMessages({
  library(shiny)

  library(shinyjs)
  library(DT)

  library(purrr)

  library(RSQLite)
  library(uuid)
  library(jsonlite)
})

# Database setup for books
ensure_books_db <- function(db_path) {
  if (!dir.exists(dirname(db_path))) dir.create(dirname(db_path), recursive = TRUE)
  con <- dbConnect(SQLite(), db_path)
  
  # Books table with user_email field
  dbExecute(con, "
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS books (
      id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      title TEXT NOT NULL,
      category TEXT NOT NULL,
      price REAL NOT NULL,
      condition TEXT NOT NULL,
      contact_details TEXT NOT NULL,
      description TEXT,
      image_paths TEXT,
      created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
      user_id INTEGER,
      user_email TEXT,
      is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT 1
    )
  ")
  
  # Create indices
  dbExecute(con, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_books_category ON books(category)")
  dbExecute(con, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_books_condition ON books(condition)")
  dbExecute(con, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_books_created ON books(created_at)")
  dbExecute(con, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_books_user_email ON books(user_email)")
  
  dbDisconnect(con)
}

# MEMORY-OPTIMIZED image compression function
compress_image <- function(input_path, output_path, max_width = 800, quality = 60) {
  tryCatch({
    # Check file size first - reject files larger than 10MB
    file_size <- file.info(input_path)$size
    if (file_size > 10 * 1024 * 1024) { # 10MB limit
      stop("File too large. Maximum size is 10MB.")
    }
    
    # Check if magick package is available for image processing
    if (requireNamespace("magick", quietly = TRUE)) {
      # Read the image with memory limits
      img <- tryCatch({
        magick::image_read(input_path)
      }, error = function(e) {
        # If magick fails, use simple file copy for unsupported formats
        file.copy(input_path, output_path)
        return(NULL)
      })
      
      if (!is.null(img)) {
        # Get image info
        img_info <- magick::image_info(img)
        width <- img_info$width
        height <- img_info$height
        
        # Calculate new dimensions to reduce memory usage
        if (width > max_width || height > max_width) {
          # More aggressive resizing for mobile
          scale_factor <- max_width / max(width, height)
          new_width <- floor(width * scale_factor)
          new_height <- floor(height * scale_factor)
          
          # Use scale instead of resize for better memory efficiency
          img <- magick::image_scale(img, paste0(new_width, "x", new_height))
        }
        
        # Auto-orient images from mobile devices
        img <- magick::image_orient(img)
        
        # Compress and save with lower quality for mobile
        magick::image_write(img, path = output_path, quality = quality)
        
        # Explicitly clean up magick objects to free memory
        rm(img)
        gc() # Force garbage collection
        return(TRUE)
      }
    }
    
    # Fallback: if magick is not available or failed, just copy the file
    file.copy(input_path, output_path)
    return(FALSE)
    
  }, error = function(e) {
    # If compression fails, fall back to original file
    tryCatch({
      file.copy(input_path, output_path)
      return(FALSE)
    }, error = function(e2) {
      return(FALSE)
    })
  })
}

# MEMORY-OPTIMIZED file operations
safe_file_operations <- function(book_id, uploaded_images) {
  tryCatch({
    book_dir <- file.path("db", "books", book_id)
    if (!dir.exists(book_dir)) {
      dir.create(book_dir, recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)
    }
    
    image_paths <- character()
    
    for (i in seq_along(uploaded_images)) {
      img <- uploaded_images[[i]]
      
      # Validate file exists and is accessible
      if (!file.exists(img$datapath)) {
        stop(paste("File not accessible:", img$name))
      }
      
      # Check file size before processing
      file_size <- file.info(img$datapath)$size
      if (file_size > 15 * 1024 * 1024) { # 15MB limit
        stop(paste("File too large:", img$name, "- Maximum 15MB allowed"))
      }
      
      # Create unique filename
      timestamp <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
      random_suffix <- sprintf("%04d", sample(1:1000, 1))
      safe_name <- paste0("image_", i, "_", timestamp, "_", random_suffix, ".jpg") # Force JPEG for consistency
      new_path <- file.path(book_dir, safe_name)
      
      # Use compression with aggressive settings for mobile
      compression_result <- compress_image(img$datapath, new_path, max_width = 800, quality = 60)
      
      # Verify the file was created
      if (!file.exists(new_path)) {
        # Final fallback - direct copy with unique name
        file.copy(img$datapath, new_path)
      }
      
      relative_path <- file.path("books", book_id, safe_name)
      image_paths <- c(image_paths, relative_path)
      
      # Force garbage collection after each image to free memory
      gc()
    }
    
    return(image_paths)
    
  }, error = function(e) {
    stop(paste("Error in file operations:", e$message))
  })
}

# UI for Books module - MODERN REDESIGN
mod_books_ui <- function(id) {
  ns <- NS(id)
  
  # Create JavaScript code with proper string handling
  js_code <- HTML(paste0("
    // JavaScript to reset file inputs and handle memory
    Shiny.addCustomMessageHandler('resetFileInput', function(message) {
      var input = $('#' + message);
      if (input.length) {
        input.val('');
        // Clear any previews
        input.nextAll('.image-preview').remove();
      }
    });
    
    // Limit file size on client side
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
      function setupFileInputLimit(inputId) {
        var input = document.getElementById(inputId);
        if (input) {
          input.addEventListener('change', function(e) {
            var file = e.target.files[0];
            if (file && file.size > 15 * 1024 * 1024) {
              alert('File size must be less than 15MB. Please choose a smaller file.');
              e.target.value = '';
            }
          });
        }
      }
      
      // Setup limits for both image inputs
      setupFileInputLimit('", ns("book_image_1"), "');
      setupFileInputLimit('", ns("book_image_2"), "');
    });

          outline: 2px solid var(--primary-500);
          outline-offset: 2px;
        }
      "))
    ),
    
    div(class = "books-module",
        fluidRow(
          column(12,
                 div(class = "books-card",
                     div(class = "card-header",
                         h4(icon("book-open"), "📚 Books Marketplace")
                     ),
                     div(class = "card-body",
                         # Modern header with gradient title
                         div(class = "books-header",
                             h1(class = "books-title", "Discover Your Next Read"),
                             actionButton(ns("show_sell_modal"), "Sell Your Book", 
                                          icon = icon("plus-circle"),
                                          class = "books-btn books-btn-primary")
                         ),

                         div(class = "books-filters",
                             fluidRow(
                               column(4, class = "col-md-4 col-12",
                                      div(class = "books-form-group",
                                          tags$label(class = "books-label", `for` = ns("filter_category"),
                                                     icon("folder"), " Category"),
                                          selectInput(ns("filter_category"), NULL, 
                                                      choices = c("All Categories", BOOK_CATEGORIES),

                               ),

                                      div(class = "books-form-group",
                                          tags$label(class = "books-label", `for` = ns("filter_condition"),
                                                     icon("star"), " Condition"),

                                      )
                               ),

                                          tags$label(class = "books-label", `for` = ns("filter_sort"),

                         uiOutput(ns("no_books_message"))
