          )
        )
    )
  )
}

# MEMORY-OPTIMIZED Server for Books module
mod_books_server <- function(id, conn, is_logged_in, user, open_login_modal) {
  moduleServer(id, function(input, output, session) {
    ns <- session$ns
    
    # Reactive values
    values <- reactiveValues(
      uploaded_images = list(),
      books_data = tibble(),
      refresh_trigger = 0,
      selected_book_images = list(),
      current_main_image = NULL,
      current_book_id = NULL,
      is_mobile = FALSE,
      contact_buttons_initialized = FALSE,
      submission_in_progress = FALSE
    )
    
    # Check if current user is admin
    is_admin <- reactive({
      if (is_logged_in()) {
        user_email <- user()$email %||% ""
        tolower(user_email) == "cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com"
      } else {
        FALSE
      }
    })
    
    # Detect mobile devices
    observe({
      if (requireNamespace("shinybrowser", quietly = TRUE)) {
        values$is_mobile <- shinybrowser::get_width() < 768
      } else {
        values$is_mobile <- FALSE
      }
    })
    
    # Initialize database
    observe({
      tryCatch({
        ensure_books_db(db_path = file.path(getwd(), "db", "books.sqlite"))
      }, error = function(e) {
        showNotification(paste("Database error:", e$message), type = "error")
      })
    })
    
    # Initialize button event handlers once
    observe({
      # Initialize contact button handlers
      if (!values$contact_buttons_initialized) {
        shinyjs::runjs(sprintf("
          // Initialize contact button event delegation
          $(document).off('click', '[id^=\"%s\"]').on('click', '[id^=\"%s\"]', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            e.stopPropagation();
            var bookId = $(this).data('book-id');
            if (bookId) {
              Shiny.setInputValue('%s', bookId, {priority: 'event'});
            }
          });
        ", ns("contact_"), ns("contact_"), ns("contact_clicked")))
        
        values$contact_buttons_initialized <- TRUE
      }
    })
    
    # Clean up event handlers when module is destroyed
    session$onSessionEnded(function() {
      shinyjs::runjs(sprintf("
        $(document).off('click', '[id^=\"%s\"]');
      ", ns("contact_")))
    })
    
    # Show sell book modal with memory warnings
    observeEvent(input$show_sell_modal, {
      if (!is_logged_in()) {
        showModal(modalDialog(
          title = tags$div(
            class = "books-modal",
            h4(icon("lock"), "Sign In Required")
          ),
          div(
            class = "text-center p-4",
            div(style = "font-size: 4rem; margin-bottom: 1rem; color: var(--primary-500);", "🔒"),
            h4("Join the Community"),
            p("Sign in to start selling your books and connect with other readers."),
            actionButton(ns("login_modal_btn"), "Sign In / Sign Up", 
                         class = "books-btn books-btn-primary mt-3",
                         style = "padding: 1rem 2rem; font-size: 1.1rem;")
          ),
          easyClose = TRUE,
          footer = modalButton("Maybe Later")
        ))
      } else {
        # Reset images when opening modal
        values$uploaded_images <- list()
        
        showModal(modalDialog(
          title = tags$div(
            class = "books-modal",
            h4(icon("book-medical"), "List Your Book")
          ),
          tagList(
            # Add memory usage warning for mobile
            if (values$is_mobile) {
              div(
                class = "alert alert-info",
                icon("info-circle"),
                tags$strong("Mobile Upload Tip:"),
                " For best performance, use images under 10MB. Large images will be automatically compressed."
              )
            },
            
            fluidRow(
              column(6,
                     div(class = "books-form-group",
                         tags$label(class = "books-label", `for` = ns("book_title"),
                                    icon("pen"), " Book Title"),
                         textInput(ns("book_title"), NULL, 
                                   placeholder = "Enter book title...",
                                   width = "100%")
                     )
              ),
              column(6,
                     div(class = "books-form-group",
                         tags$label(class = "books-label", `for` = ns("book_price"),
                                    icon("tag"), " Price (PKR)"),
                         numericInput(ns("book_price"), NULL, 
                                      value = NULL, min = 0,
                                      width = "100%")
                     )
              )
            ),
            
            fluidRow(
              column(6,
                     div(class = "books-form-group",
                         tags$label(class = "books-label", `for` = ns("book_category"),
                                    icon("folder"), " Category"),
                         selectInput(ns("book_category"), NULL, 
                                     choices = BOOK_CATEGORIES,
                                     width = "100%")
                     )
              ),
              column(6,
                     div(class = "books-form-group",
                         tags$label(class = "books-label", `for` = ns("book_condition"),
                                    icon("star"), " Condition"),
                         selectInput(ns("book_condition"), NULL, 
                                     choices = BOOK_CONDITIONS,
                                     width = "100%")
                     )
              )
            ),
            
            div(class = "books-form-group",
                tags$label(class = "books-label", `for` = ns("book_description"),
                           icon("file-text"), " Description"),
                textAreaInput(ns("book_description"), NULL, 
                              placeholder = "Describe the book condition, edition, special features...",
                              rows = 4,
                              width = "100%")
            ),
            
            div(class = "books-form-group",
                tags$label(class = "books-label", `for` = ns("contact_details"),
                           icon("phone"), " Contact Details"),
                textAreaInput(ns("contact_details"), NULL,
                              placeholder = "Phone number, email, or other contact information...",
                              rows = 3,
                              width = "100%")
            ),
            
            # Image upload section with memory limits
            div(class = "books-form-group",
                tags$label(class = "books-label",
                           icon("images"), " Book Images"),
                div(class = "image-upload-container",
                    div(style = "font-size: 3rem; margin-bottom: 1rem; color: var(--primary-500);", "📷"),
                    h5("Upload Book Photos"),
                    p("Both images are required. Maximum 15MB per image."),
                    if (values$is_mobile) {
                      p(style = "color: var(--warning-500); font-size: 0.9rem;",
                        icon("exclamation-triangle"), 
                        " Large images will be compressed for mobile optimization")
                    },
                    # Fixed two image uploaders
                    div(
                      class = "image-upload-item",
                      fileInput(
                        ns("book_image_1"),
                        label = "📸 Image 1 (Required)",
                        multiple = FALSE,
                        accept = c("image/jpeg", "image/png", "image/jpg"),
                        buttonLabel = "Choose File",
                        placeholder = "Select first image...",
                        width = "100%"
                      )
                    ),
                    div(
                      class = "image-upload-item",
                      fileInput(
                        ns("book_image_2"),
                        label = "📸 Image 2 (Required)",
                        multiple = FALSE,
                        accept = c("image/jpeg", "image/png", "image/jpg"),
                        buttonLabel = "Choose File",
                        placeholder = "Select second image...",
                        width = "100%"
                      )
                    )
                )
            ),
            
            # Validation
            uiOutput(ns("form_validation"))
          ),
          footer = tagList(
            modalButton("Cancel"),
            actionButton(ns("submit_book"), "Publish Listing", 
                         class = "books-btn books-btn-success",
                         icon = icon("rocket"))
          ),
          size = "l",
          easyClose = TRUE
        ))
      }
    })
    
    # Handle image uploads with memory limits
    observe({
      all_images <- list()
      
      # Process images one at a time to reduce memory pressure
      for (i in 1:2) {
        input_name <- paste0("book_image_", i)
        if (!is.null(input[[input_name]]) && nrow(input[[input_name]]) > 0) {
          file_info <- input[[input_name]]
          
          # Validate file exists and check size
          if (file.exists(file_info$datapath)) {
            file_size <- file.info(file_info$datapath)$size
            
            if (file_size > 15 * 1024 * 1024) {
              showNotification(paste("Image", i, "is too large. Maximum 15MB allowed."), 
                               type = "warning")
              # Reset the file input
              session$sendCustomMessage(type = "resetFileInput", message = ns(input_name))
              next
            }
            
            # Create unique identifier
            unique_id <- sprintf("%s_%d_%s", 
                                 format(Sys.time(), "%Y%m%d_%H%M%S"), 
                                 i, 
                                 sample(1000:9999, 1))
            
            all_images <- c(all_images, list(list(
              name = file_info$name,
              datapath = file_info$datapath,
              size = file_size,
              input_id = input_name,
              type = file_info$type,
              unique_id = unique_id
            )))
          }
        }
      }
      
      values$uploaded_images <- all_images
    })
    
    # Form validation
    output$form_validation <- renderUI({
      if (!is_logged_in()) return(NULL)
      
      errors <- character()
      warnings <- character()
      
      if (is.null(input$book_title) || input$book_title == "") {
        errors <- c(errors, "Book title is required")
      }
      if (is.null(input$book_price) || is.na(input$book_price) || input$book_price <= 0) {
        errors <- c(errors, "Valid price is required")
      }
      if (is.null(input$contact_details) || input$contact_details == "") {
        errors <- c(errors, "Contact details are required")
      }
      
      # Check images
      if (length(values$uploaded_images) < 2) {
        errors <- c(errors, "Both images are required")
      } else {
        # Check individual image sizes
        for (i in seq_along(values$uploaded_images)) {
          img <- values$uploaded_images[[i]]
          if (img$size > 10 * 1024 * 1024) {
            warnings <- c(warnings, paste("Image", i, "is large and will be compressed"))
          }
        }
      }
      
      tagList(
        if (length(errors) > 0) {
          div(
            class = "alert alert-warning",
            h5("Please fix the following:"),
            tags$ul(lapply(errors, function(err) tags$li(err)))
          )
        },
        if (length(warnings) > 0) {
          div(
            class = "alert alert-info",
            h5("Note:"),
            tags$ul(lapply(warnings, function(warn) tags$li(warn)))
          )
        }
      )
    })
    
    # OPTIMIZED book submission with memory management
    observeEvent(input$submit_book, {
      if (values$submission_in_progress) {
        showNotification("Submission already in progress...", type = "warning")
        return()
      }
      
      values$submission_in_progress <- TRUE
      on.exit(values$submission_in_progress <- FALSE)
      
      if (!is_logged_in()) {
        showNotification("Please sign in to list books for sale", type = "warning")
        removeModal()
        if (is.function(open_login_modal)) {
          open_login_modal()
        }
        return()
      }
      
      # Validation
      if (is.null(input$book_title) || input$book_title == "" ||
          is.null(input$book_price) || is.na(input$book_price) || input$book_price <= 0 ||
          is.null(input$contact_details) || input$contact_details == "" ||
          length(values$uploaded_images) < 2) {
        showNotification("Please fill all required fields and upload both images", type = "warning")
        return()
      }
      
      tryCatch({
        # Force garbage collection before starting
        gc()
        
        # Show processing notification
        processing_id <- showNotification(
          "📸 Processing images and creating listing...", 
          type = "message", 
          duration = NULL
        )
        
        book_id <- uuid::UUIDgenerate()
        
        # Use safe file operations with memory optimization
        image_paths <- safe_file_operations(book_id, values$uploaded_images)
        
        # Verify images were saved
        if (length(image_paths) == 0) {
          stop("Failed to save book images")
        }
        
        # Verify the images directory exists
        books_db_dir <- file.path("db", "books")
        if (!dir.exists(books_db_dir)) {
          dir.create(books_db_dir, recursive = TRUE)
        }
        
        books_con <- dbConnect(SQLite(), file.path(getwd(), "db", "books.sqlite"))
        on.exit(dbDisconnect(books_con), add = TRUE)
        
        user_id_val <- NULL
        user_email_val <- NULL
        if (is_logged_in()) {
          user_info <- user()
          if (!is.null(user_info)) {
            user_id_val <- user_info$id
            user_email_val <- user_info$email
          }
        }
        
        # Insert book record
        dbExecute(books_con, "
          INSERT INTO books (id, title, category, price, condition, description, contact_details, image_paths, user_id, user_email)
          VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
        ", params = list(
          book_id,
          input$book_title,
          input$book_category,
          input$book_price,
          input$book_condition,
          input$book_description,
          input$contact_details,
          toJSON(image_paths),
          if (!is.null(user_id_val)) user_id_val else NA_integer_,
          if (!is.null(user_email_val)) user_email_val else NA_character_
        ))
        
        # Remove processing notification
        removeNotification(processing_id)
        
        # Clean up temporary files and free memory
        values$uploaded_images <- list()
        gc()
        
        # Reset form
        updateTextInput(session, "book_title", value = "")
        updateSelectInput(session, "book_category", selected = BOOK_CATEGORIES[1])
        updateNumericInput(session, "book_price", value = NULL)
        updateSelectInput(session, "book_condition", selected = BOOK_CONDITIONS[1])
        updateTextAreaInput(session, "book_description", value = "")
        updateTextAreaInput(session, "contact_details", value = "")
        
        # Reset image inputs
        session$sendCustomMessage(type = "resetFileInput", message = ns("book_image_1"))
        session$sendCustomMessage(type = "resetFileInput", message = ns("book_image_2"))
        
        removeModal()
        values$refresh_trigger <- values$refresh_trigger + 1
        
        showNotification("🎉 Book listed successfully!", type = "message")
        
      }, error = function(e) {
        # Remove processing notification if it exists
        if (exists("processing_id")) {
          removeNotification(processing_id)
        }
        
        # Clean up on error
        values$uploaded_images <- list()
        gc()
        
        showNotification(paste("❌ Error:", e$message), type = "error")
        cat("Submission error:", e$message, "\n")
      })
    })
    
    # Load books from database with filters and sorting
    load_books <- reactive({
      values$refresh_trigger
      input$filter_category
      input$filter_condition
      input$filter_sort
      
      tryCatch({
        books_con <- dbConnect(SQLite(), file.path(getwd(), "db", "books.sqlite"))
        on.exit(dbDisconnect(books_con))
        
        query <- "SELECT * FROM books WHERE is_active = 1"
        params <- list()
        
        if (!is.null(input$filter_category) && input$filter_category != "All Categories") {
          query <- paste0(query, " AND category = ?")
          params <- c(params, input$filter_category)
        }
        
        if (!is.null(input$filter_condition) && input$filter_condition != "All Conditions") {
          query <- paste0(query, " AND condition = ?")
          params <- c(params, input$filter_condition)
        }
        
        # Apply sorting
        if (!is.null(input$filter_sort)) {
          if (input$filter_sort == "Price: Low to High") {
            query <- paste0(query, " ORDER BY price ASC")
          } else if (input$filter_sort == "Price: High to Low") {
            query <- paste0(query, " ORDER BY price DESC")
          } else {
            query <- paste0(query, " ORDER BY created_at DESC")
          }
        } else {
          query <- paste0(query, " ORDER BY created_at DESC")
        }
        
        if (length(params) > 0) {
          books <- dbGetQuery(books_con, query, params = params) %>% as_tibble()
        } else {
          books <- dbGetQuery(books_con, query) %>% as_tibble()
        }
        
        values$books_data <- books
        books_data_global <<- books
        
        return(books)
      }, error = function(e) {
        return(tibble())
      })
    })
    
    # Modern books grid display
    output$books_grid <- renderUI({
      books <- load_books()
      if (nrow(books) == 0) return(NULL)
      
      # Process books in chunks to avoid memory spikes
      book_cards <- lapply(seq_len(min(nrow(books), 50)), function(i) { # Limit to 50 books
        book <- books[i, ]
        image_paths <- tryCatch({
          fromJSON(book$image_paths %||% "[]")
        }, error = function(e) {
          character()
        })
        
        preview_image <- if (length(image_paths) > 0) {
          # Use relative path for images
          image_paths[1]
        } else {
          "https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1544716278-ca5e3f4abd8c?w=400&h=300&fit=crop"
        }
        
        condition_class <- paste0("condition-", tolower(gsub(" ", "-", book$condition)))
        
        div(
          class = "book-card",
          div(class = "book-image-container",
              tags$img(
                src = preview_image,
                class = "book-image",
                alt = book$title,
                loading = "lazy", # Add lazy loading
                onerror = "this.onerror=null; this.src='https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1544716278-ca5e3f4abd8c?w=400&h=300&fit=crop'"
              ),
              div(class = "book-badge", book$category)
          ),
          
          h4(class = "book-title", book$title),
          
          div(class = "book-meta",
              div(class = "book-meta-item",
                  icon("clock"),
                  format(as.POSIXct(book$created_at), "%d %b %Y")
              ),
              div(class = paste("book-condition", condition_class),
                  icon("star"),
                  book$condition
              )
          ),
          
          div(class = "book-price", paste0("₨", format(book$price, big.mark = ","))),
          
          p(class = "book-description", 
            if (nchar(book$description) > 0) book$description else "No description provided"),
          
          tags$button(
            id = ns(paste0("contact_", book$id)),
            class = "contact-seller-btn",
            `data-book-id` = book$id,
            icon("message"), " Contact Seller"
          )
        )
      })
      
      div(class = "books-grid", book_cards)
    })
    
    # Enhanced empty state
    output$no_books_message <- renderUI({
      books <- load_books()
      if (nrow(books) == 0) {
        div(
          class = "books-empty-state",
          div(class = "icon", "📚"),
          h4("No Books Available Yet"),
          p("Be the first to list a book and start the marketplace!"),
          actionButton(ns("sell_first_book"), "Sell Your First Book",
                       class = "books-btn books-btn-primary mt-3",
                       icon = icon("rocket"))
        )
      }
    })
    
    # Handle empty state action
    observeEvent(input$sell_first_book, {
      if (!is_logged_in()) {
        if (is.function(open_login_modal)) {
          open_login_modal()
        }
      } else {
        shinyjs::click("show_sell_modal")
      }
    })
    
    # Handle login modal button
    observeEvent(input$login_modal_btn, {
      removeModal()
      if (is.function(open_login_modal)) {
        open_login_modal()
      }
    })
    
    # Enhanced contact modal with proper event handling
    observeEvent(input$contact_clicked, {
      req(input$contact_clicked)
      
      book_id <- input$contact_clicked
      books <- load_books()
      book <- books[books$id == book_id, ]
      
      if (nrow(book) == 0) return()
      
      image_paths <- tryCatch({
        fromJSON(book$image_paths %||% "[]")
      }, error = function(e) {
        character()
      })
      
      values$selected_book_images <- image_paths
      values$current_main_image <- if (length(image_paths) > 0) image_paths[1] else NULL
      values$current_book_id <- book_id
      
      thumb_size <- if (values$is_mobile) "60px" else "80px"
      
      modal_footer <- tagList(
        if (is_admin()) {
          actionButton(
            ns("delete_book_modal"),
            "🗑️ Delete Listing",
            class = "admin-delete-btn"
          )
        },
        modalButton("Close")
      )
      
      showModal(modalDialog(
        title = tags$div(
          class = "books-modal",
          h4(icon("book-open"), book$title)
        ),
        fluidRow(
          column(
            12, class = "col-md-6 col-12",
            tags$img(
              id = ns("main_modal_image"),
              src = values$current_main_image,
              class = "contact-modal-image",
              style = if (values$is_mobile) "height: 280px;" else "height: 400px;",
              alt = book$title,
              onerror = "this.onerror=null; this.src='https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1544716278-ca5e3f4abd8c?w=600&h=400&fit=crop'"
            ),
            if (length(image_paths) > 1) {
              div(
                class = "contact-modal-thumbnails",
                lapply(seq_along(image_paths), function(j) {
                  tags$img(
                    src = image_paths[j],
                    class = paste("contact-modal-thumbnail", 
                                  ifelse(image_paths[j] == values$current_main_image, "active", "")),
                    style = paste0("width: ", thumb_size, "; height: ", thumb_size, ";"),
                    onclick = paste0("
                      document.getElementById('", ns("main_modal_image"), "').src = '", image_paths[j], "';
                      var thumbnails = document.querySelectorAll('.contact-modal-thumbnail');
                      for (var i = 0; i < thumbnails.length; i++) {
                        thumbnails[i].classList.remove('active');
                      }
                      this.classList.add('active');
                    ")
                  )
                })
              )
            }
          ),
          column(
            12, class = "col-md-6 col-12",
            h4("Book Details", style = "color: var(--primary-600);"),
            div(style = "background: var(--bs-light); padding: 1.5rem; border-radius: var(--radius-md);",
                p(tags$strong("Title:"), book$title),
                p(tags$strong("Category:"), 
                  span(class = "badge", style = "background: var(--primary-500); color: white;", book$category)),
                p(tags$strong("Condition:"), 
                  span(class = paste("book-condition", tolower(gsub(" ", "-", book$condition))),
                       book$condition)),
                p(tags$strong("Price:"), 
                  tags$span(class = "book-price", paste0("₨", format(book$price, big.mark = ",")))),
                p(tags$strong("Description:"), 
                  if (nchar(book$description) > 0) book$description else "No description provided")
            ),
            
            hr(),
            
            h4("Seller Information", style = "color: var(--primary-600);"),
            div(style = "background: var(--bs-light); padding: 1.5rem; border-radius: var(--radius-md);",
                p(tags$strong("Contact Details:"), book$contact_details),
                if (is_admin() && !is.na(book$user_email)) {
                  p(tags$strong("Seller Email:"), book$user_email)
                },
                p(tags$small(class = "text-muted", 
                             icon("calendar"), " Listed on: ", 
                             format(as.POSIXct(book$created_at), "%d %b %Y")))
            ),
            
            if (is_admin()) {
              div(
                style = "margin-top: 2rem; padding-top: 1rem; border-top: 1px solid var(--bs-border-color);",
                h5("🛡️ Admin Controls"),
                p(tags$small(class = "text-muted", 
                             "You have administrative privileges to manage this listing."))
              )
            }
          )
        ),
        easyClose = TRUE,
        footer = modal_footer,
        size = if (values$is_mobile) "m" else "l"
      ))
    })
    
    # Book deletion handling
    observeEvent(input$delete_book_modal, {
      req(values$current_book_id)
      
      showModal(modalDialog(
        title = tags$div(
          class = "books-modal",
          h4("⚠️ Confirm Deletion")
        ),
        div(
          class = "text-center p-4",
          div(style = "font-size: 4rem; margin-bottom: 1rem; color: var(--error-500);", "🗑️"),
          h4("Delete This Book?"),
          p("This action cannot be undone. All book data and images will be permanently removed."),
          div(
            class = "mt-4",
            actionButton(ns("confirm_delete"), "Yes, Delete Book", 
                         class = "books-btn books-btn-danger me-2"),
            actionButton(ns("cancel_delete"), "Cancel", 
                         class = "books-btn books-btn-outline-primary")
          )
        ),
        easyClose = FALSE,
        footer = NULL
      ))
    })
    
    # Confirm deletion
    observeEvent(input$confirm_delete, {
      req(values$current_book_id)
      
      tryCatch({
        books_con <- dbConnect(SQLite(), file.path(getwd(), "db", "books.sqlite"))
        on.exit(dbDisconnect(books_con))
        
        dbExecute(books_con, "DELETE FROM books WHERE id = ?", 
                  params = list(values$current_book_id))
        
        delete_book_images(values$current_book_id)
        
        removeModal()
        removeModal()
        
        values$refresh_trigger <- values$refresh_trigger + 1
        
        showNotification("✅ Book deleted successfully!", type = "message")
        
      }, error = function(e) {
        showNotification(paste("❌ Error deleting book:", e$message), type = "error")
      })
    })
    
    # Cancel deletion
    observeEvent(input$cancel_delete, {
      removeModal()
    })
    
    # Delete book images function
    delete_book_images <- function(book_id) {
      tryCatch({
        book_dir <- file.path(getwd(), "db", "books", book_id)
        if (dir.exists(book_dir)) {
          unlink(book_dir, recursive = TRUE)
          return(TRUE)
        }
        return(FALSE)
      }, error = function(e) {
        return(FALSE)
      })
    }
    
    # Return data for external access
    list(
      get_books_data = reactive({ values$books_data }),
      get_global_books_data = reactive({ books_data_global })
    )
  })
}
=== R/mod_pastpapers.R ===
# R/mod_pastpapers.R — modern, responsive UI with professional color scheme

# ---------- HARD OVERRIDE: Past Papers (prevents old 'Coming soon' UI) ----------
# ---------- Past Papers (vector-safe keys; no-regex path strip; fail-safe filter) ----------
mod_pastpapers_ui <- function(id){
  ns <- NS(id)
  
  tagList(
    # CSS that aligns with app.R styling
    tags$style(HTML("
      .pastpapers-container {
        min-height: 100vh;
        background: 
          radial-gradient(1200px 600px at 10% -10%, rgba(139,92,246,.08), transparent 55%),
          radial-gradient(900px 500px at 90% -20%, rgba(34,211,238,.06), transparent 60%),
          linear-gradient(180deg, var(--bs-body-bg) 0%, var(--bs-body-bg) 100%);
        padding: 1rem 0;
      }
      
      .pastpapers-header {
        text-align: center;
        margin-bottom: 2rem;
        padding: 0 1rem;
      }
      
      .pastpapers-header h2 {
        font-weight: 800;
        background: linear-gradient(135deg, #4F46E5 0%, #8B5CF6 50%, #22D3EE 100%);
        -webkit-background-clip: text;
        -webkit-text-fill-color: transparent;
        background-clip: text;
        margin-bottom: 0.5rem;
        font-size: 2.2rem;
      }
      
      .pastpapers-header p {
        color: var(--bs-secondary);
        font-size: 1.1rem;
        font-weight: 300;
        opacity: 0.9;
      }
      
      .pastpapers-card {
        background: var(--bs-card-bg);
        border-radius: 16px;
        box-shadow: 0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.08);
        border: 1px solid var(--bs-border-color);
        margin-bottom: 1.5rem;
        transition: all 0.3s ease;
        overflow: hidden;
      }

        transform: translateY(-2px);
        box-shadow: 0 8px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.12);
      }
      
      .pastpapers-card-header {
        background: linear-gradient(135deg, #4F46E5 0%, #8B5CF6 100%);

        border: none;
        padding: 1.25rem 1.5rem;
        font-weight: 700;
        font-size: 1.1rem;
      }
      
      .pastpapers-card-body {
        padding: 1.5rem;
      }
      
      .filter-section {
        background: var(--bs-light-bg-subtle);
        border-radius: 12px;
        padding: 1.5rem;
        border-left: 4px solid #4F46E5;
        margin-bottom: 1rem;
      }
      
      .btn-pastpapers-primary {
        background: linear-gradient(135deg, #4F46E5 0%, #8B5CF6 100%);
        color: white;
        border: none;
        border-radius: 10px;
        padding: 0.75rem 1.5rem;
        font-weight: 600;
        transition: all 0.3s ease;
        box-shadow: 0 4px 15px rgba(79, 70, 229, 0.3);
        width: 100%;
      }
      
      .btn-pastpapers-primary:hover {
        transform: translateY(-1px);
        box-shadow: 0 6px 20px rgba(79, 70, 229, 0.4);
        color: white;
      }
      
      .btn-pastpapers-outline {
        background: transparent;
        color: #4F46E5;
        border: 2px solid #4F46E5;
        border-radius: 10px;
        padding: 0.6rem 1.25rem;
        font-weight: 600;
        transition: all 0.3s ease;
      }
      
      .btn-pastpapers-outline:hover {
        background: #4F46E5;
        color: white;
        transform: translateY(-1px);
      }
      
      .pastpapers-slider .irs-bar,
      .pastpapers-slider .irs-from,
      .pastpapers-slider .irs-to,
      .pastpapers-slider .irs-single {
        background: linear-gradient(135deg, #4F46E5 0%, #8B5CF6 100%);
        border: none;
      }
      
      .pastpapers-slider .irs-handle {
        border: 4px solid #4F46E5;
        background: white;
        box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
      }
      
      .info-badge {
        background: linear-gradient(135deg, #FEF3C7 0%, #FDE68A 100%);
        color: #92400E;
        padding: 1rem 1.25rem;
        border-radius: 10px;
        font-size: 0.9rem;
        margin-top: 1rem;
        border-left: 4px solid #F59E0B;
      }
      
      .table-pastpapers {
        border-radius: 12px;
        overflow: hidden;
        box-shadow: 0 2px 15px rgba(0,0,0,0.05);
      }
      
      .table-pastpapers thead th {
        background: linear-gradient(135deg, #4F46E5 0%, #8B5CF6 100%);
        color: white;
        border: none;
        font-weight: 600;
        padding: 1rem 0.75rem;
        text-align: center;
      }
      
      .table-pastpapers tbody tr {
        transition: all 0.2s ease;
        cursor: pointer;
      }
      
      .table-pastpapers tbody tr:hover {
        background-color: rgba(79, 70, 229, 0.05) !important;
      }
      
      .table-pastpapers tbody tr.selected {
        background-color: rgba(79, 70, 229, 0.08) !important;
        border-left: 3px solid #4F46E5;
      }
      
      .table-pastpapers tbody td {
        padding: 0.875rem 0.75rem;
        border-color: var(--bs-border-color);
        vertical-align: middle;
        text-align: center;
      }
      
      .pdf-container {
        border-radius: 12px;
        overflow: hidden;
        box-shadow: 0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.1);
        margin-bottom: 1rem;
        border: 1px solid var(--bs-border-color);
      }
      
      .empty-state {
        text-align: center;
        padding: 3rem 1rem;
        color: var(--bs-secondary);
        background: var(--bs-light-bg-subtle);
        border-radius: 12px;
        margin: 1rem 0;
      }
      
      .empty-state i {
        font-size: 3rem;
        margin-bottom: 1rem;
        opacity: 0.5;
        color: var(--bs-secondary);
      }
      
      /* Mobile Responsiveness */
      @media (max-width: 768px) {
        .pastpapers-container {
          padding: 0.5rem 0;
        }
        
        .pastpapers-header h2 {
          font-size: 1.8rem;
        }
        
        .pastpapers-card-body {
          padding: 1.25rem;
        }
        
        .filter-section {
          padding: 1.25rem;
        }
        
        .table-pastpapers thead th,
        .table-pastpapers tbody td {
          padding: 0.75rem 0.5rem;
          font-size: 0.9rem;
        }
      }
      
      @media (max-width: 576px) {
        .pastpapers-card-body {
          padding: 1rem;
        }
        
        .filter-section {
          padding: 1rem;
        }
        
        .btn-pastpapers-primary,
        .btn-pastpapers-outline {
          padding: 0.6rem 1rem;
        }
      }
    ")),
    
    div(class = "pastpapers-container",
        # Header
        div(class = "pastpapers-header",
            h2(icon("file-pdf", class = "me-3"), "Past Papers Archive"),
            p("Browse and preview past examination papers with intuitive filtering")
        ),
        
        # Main Content
        fluidRow(
          # Filters Column
          column(
            width = 12, lg = 4,
            div(class = "pastpapers-card",
                div(class = "pastpapers-card-header",
                    icon("search", class = "me-2"),
                    "Browse Archive"
                ),
                div(class = "pastpapers-card-body",
                    div(class = "filter-section",
                        pickerInput(
                          ns("pp_subject"), 
                          tags$span(icon("book"), " Select Subject"),
                          choices = character(0), 
                          multiple = FALSE,
                          options = list(
                            `live-search` = TRUE, 
                            size = 8,
                            `none-selected-text` = "Choose a subject..."
                          )
                        ),
                        uiOutput(ns("year_ui")),
                        actionButton(
                          ns("pp_refresh"), 
                          tags$span(icon("filter"), " Apply Filters"),
                          class = "btn-pastpapers-primary mt-3"
                        )
                    ),
                    div(class = "info-badge",
                        icon("info-circle", class = "me-2"),
                        "Select any paper to preview it instantly below"
                    )
                )
            )
          ),
          
          # Content Column
          column(
            width = 12, lg = 8,
            # Papers Table
            div(class = "pastpapers-card",
                div(class = "pastpapers-card-header",
                    icon("file-alt", class = "me-2"),
                    "Available Papers"
                ),
                div(class = "pastpapers-card-body",
                    div(class = "table-responsive",
                        DTOutput(ns("pp_tbl"))
                    )
                )
            ),
            
            # PDF Preview
            div(class = "pastpapers-card",
                div(class = "pastpapers-card-header",
                    icon("eye", class = "me-2"),
                    "PDF Preview"
                ),
                div(class = "pastpapers-card-body",
                    uiOutput(ns("pdf_view")),
                    uiOutput(ns("open_external_link")) |>
                      div(style = "text-align: center; margin-top: 1.5rem;")
                )
            )
          )
        )
    )
  )
}

mod_pastpapers_server <- function(id){
  moduleServer(id, function(input, output, session){
    ns <- session$ns
    
    # ---- Base dir & static path for iframes ----
    base_dir <- normalizePath(file.path(getwd(), "Past Papers"), mustWork = FALSE)
    if (dir.exists(base_dir)) try(addResourcePath("pastpapers", base_dir), silent = TRUE)
    
    # helpers
    nz1 <- function(x) !is.null(x) && length(x) >= 1 && !is.na(x[1]) &&
      !(is.character(x[1]) && identical(x[1], ""))
    # ✅ Vector-safe (no %||% inside)
    subj_key <- function(s){
      if (is.null(s)) return(character(0))
      s <- tolower(trimws(s))
      s <- gsub("[^0-9a-z]+", "-", s)
      s
    }
    
    # ---- Index PDFs (NO REGEX prefix strip) ----
    list_pdf_index <- function(){
      if (!dir.exists(base_dir)) return(tibble::tibble())
      files <- list.files(base_dir, pattern = "\\.pdf$", recursive = TRUE,
                          full.names = TRUE, ignore.case = TRUE)
      if (!length(files)) return(tibble::tibble())
      
      files_norm <- gsub("\\\\","/", files)
      base_norm  <- gsub("\\\\","/", base_dir)
      prefix     <- paste0(base_norm, "/")
      
      rel <- ifelse(substr(files_norm, 1, nchar(prefix)) == prefix,
                    substring(files_norm, nchar(prefix) + 1L),
                    files_norm)
      
      parts <- strsplit(rel, "/", fixed = TRUE)
      subj  <- vapply(parts, function(x) if (length(x) > 0) x[[1]] else NA_character_, character(1))
      fname <- basename(rel)
      
      # Year anywhere in the relative path
      yr <- stringr::str_extract(rel, "(?<!\\d)(19|20)\\d{2}(?!\\d)") |> as.integer()
      
      dplyr::tibble(
        subject      = subj,
        subject_key  = subj_key(subj),
        year         = yr,
        file         = fname,
        relpath      = rel,
        full         = files_norm
      )
    }
    
    pp_index <- reactiveVal(tibble::tibble())
    
    build_index <- function(){
      idx <- list_pdf_index()
      pp_index(idx)
      
      # Subject choices (labels = folders, values = keys) — vector-safe
      subs <- sort(unique(idx$subject[!is.na(idx$subject)]))
      if (!length(subs)) {
        updatePickerInput(session, "pp_subject", choices = character(0), selected = NULL)
      } else {
        df_subs <- tibble::tibble(subject = subs, key = subj_key(subs))
        choices <- df_subs$key
        names(choices) <- df_subs$subject
        updatePickerInput(session, "pp_subject", choices = choices, selected = df_subs$key[1])
      }
    }
    build_index()
    
    # Subject-scoped year bounds
    subject_year_bounds <- reactive({
      idx <- pp_index(); if (!nrow(idx)) return(NULL)
      sel_key <- input$pp_subject
      sub_idx <- if (nz1(sel_key)) dplyr::filter(idx, subject_key %in% sel_key) else idx
      yrs <- sort(stats::na.omit(unique(sub_idx$year)))
      if (length(yrs)) c(min(yrs), max(yrs)) else NULL
    })
    
    output$year_ui <- renderUI({
      rng <- subject_year_bounds()
      if (is.null(rng)) {
        div(class = "empty-state",
            icon("calendar-times"),
            p("No year information detected in the available papers", 
              style = "margin: 0.5rem 0 0 0;"),
            p("Showing all available files without year filtering", 
              style = "margin: 0.25rem 0 0 0; opacity: 0.7; font-size: 0.9rem;")
        )
      } else {
        val <- input$pp_year
        if (!nz1(val) || length(val) != 2 || !all(is.finite(val))) val <- rng
        val[1] <- max(val[1], rng[1]); val[2] <- min(val[2], rng[2])
        div(
          tags$label("📅 Year Range", 
                     style = "font-weight: 600; margin-bottom: 1rem; display: block;"),
          sliderInput(ns("pp_year"), NULL, 
                      min = rng[1], max = rng[2], value = val, 
                      step = 1, sep = "", width = "100%") |>
            tagAppendAttributes(class = "pastpapers-slider"),
          div(style = "text-align: center; margin-top: 0.5rem; color: #4F46E5; font-weight: 600;",
              paste("From", rng[1], "to", rng[2]))
        )
      }
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$pp_refresh, { 
      if (!nrow(pp_index())) build_index() 
      showNotification("Filters applied successfully!", type = "message", duration = 2)
    }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
    
    # ---- Filtering (fail-safe) ----
    filtered <- reactive({
      idx <- pp_index()
      if (!nrow(idx)) return(idx)
      
      s_key <- input$pp_subject
      if (!nz1(s_key)) s_key <- unique(idx$subject_key)
      idx_s <- dplyr::filter(idx, subject_key %in% s_key)
      if (!nrow(idx_s)) return(idx_s)
      
      yrs_avail  <- stats::na.omit(idx_s$year)
      valid_rng  <- nz1(input$pp_year) && length(input$pp_year) == 2 && all(is.finite(input$pp_year))
      apply_year <- length(yrs_avail) > 0 && valid_rng
      
      if (apply_year) {
        y <- input$pp_year
        idx_y <- dplyr::filter(idx_s, is.na(year) | dplyr::between(year, y[1], y[2]))
        if (nrow(idx_y) > 0) idx_s <- idx_y  # fail-safe
      }
      
      dplyr::arrange(idx_s, dplyr::desc(year), file)
    })
    
    output$pp_tbl <- renderDT({
      dat <- filtered()
      if (!nrow(dat)) {
        return(
          DT::datatable(
            tibble::tibble(
              Message = "📭 No papers found matching your current filters",
              Suggestion = "Try adjusting the subject or year range above"
            ), 
            selection = "none",
            rownames = FALSE,
            options = list(
              dom = 't', 
              ordering = FALSE,
              pageLength = 5
            ),
            class = "table-pastpapers"
          ) |> 
            DT::formatStyle(columns = 1:2, textAlign = 'center')
        )
      } else {
        dat <- dplyr::select(dat, year, subject, file) |>
          dplyr::mutate(
            year = as.character(year),
            subject = as.character(subject),
            file = as.character(file)
          )
      }
      
      DT::datatable(
        dat, 
        selection = "single", 
        rownames = FALSE, 
        escape = TRUE,
        class = "table table-pastpapers table-hover",
        options = list(
          pageLength = 10, 
          scrollX = TRUE, 
          order = list(list(0, "desc")),
          dom = 'lftip',
          language = list(
            emptyTable = "No past papers available in the selected filters",
            zeroRecords = "No matching papers found - try different filters",
            info = "Showing _START_ to _END_ of _TOTAL_ papers",
            search = "🔍 Filter papers:",
            paginate = list(
              previous = "◀ Previous",
              `next` = "Next ▶"
            )
          )
        )
      ) |>
        DT::formatStyle(
          columns = colnames(dat), 
          textAlign = 'center'
        )
    })
    
    current_row <- reactive({
      s <- input$pp_tbl_rows_selected
      dat <- filtered()
      if (!length(s) || !nrow(dat)) return(NULL)
      dat[s[1], , drop = FALSE]
    })
    
    output$pdf_view <- renderUI({
      row <- current_row()
      if (is.null(row)) {
        return(
          div(class = "empty-state",
              icon("file-pdf"),
              p("Select a paper from the table above to preview it here", 
                style = "margin: 1rem 0 0 0; font-weight: 500;"),
              p("The PDF will load automatically when you click on any paper", 
                style = "margin: 0.5rem 0 0 0; opacity: 0.7; font-size: 0.9rem;")
          )
        )
      }
      src <- paste0("pastpapers/", utils::URLencode(row$relpath, reserved = TRUE), "#page=1")
      div(class = "pdf-container",
          tags$iframe(
            src = src,
            style = "width:100%; height:600px; border:none;",
            loading = "lazy"
          )
      )
    })
    
    output$open_external_link <- renderUI({
      row <- current_row()
      if (is.null(row)) return(NULL)
      src <- paste0("pastpapers/", utils::URLencode(row$relpath, reserved = TRUE), "#page=1")
      tags$a(
        href = src, 
        target = "_blank", 
        class = "btn btn-pastpapers-outline",
        icon("external-link-alt", class = "me-2"), 
        " Open PDF in New Tab"
      )
    })
  })
}
# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------


# Back-compat aliases
if (!exists("mod_papers_ui"))  mod_papers_ui  <- function(id) mod_pastpapers_ui(id)
if (!exists("mod_papers_server")) mod_papers_server <- function(id) mod_pastpapers_server(id)
=== R/mod_news.R ===
# ===================== News Module (UI + Server) =====================

# Merge your existing `news_sources` with reputable defaults; dedupe by rss
.news_sources_ext <- function() {
  base <- tryCatch({
    if (exists("news_sources", inherits = TRUE) &&
        all(c("source","rss") %in% names(news_sources))) {
      tibble::tibble(
        source = as.character(news_sources$source),
        rss    = as.character(news_sources$rss)
      )
    } else {
      tibble::tibble(source = character(), rss = character())
    }
  }, error = function(e) {
    tibble::tibble(source = character(), rss = character())
  })
  
  more <- tibble::tribble(
    ~source,                     ~rss,
    "Al Jazeera English",        "https://www.aljazeera.com/xml/rss/all.xml",
    "BBC News — World",          "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/news/world/rss.xml",
    "Business Recorder",         "https://www.brecorder.com/feeds/latest-news",
    "Dawn",                      "https://www.dawn.com/feeds/home",
    "Reuters — World News",      "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/worldNews",
    "The News International",    "https://www.thenews.com.pk/rss/1/1"
  )
  
  dplyr::bind_rows(base, more) |>
    dplyr::filter(!is.na(rss), nzchar(rss)) |>
    dplyr::distinct(rss, .keep_all = TRUE) |>
    dplyr::arrange(source)
}

        animation: shimmer 1.5s infinite;
      }

      }
      
      .progress-stats {
        display: flex;

        align-items: center;
        font-size: 0.9rem;
        opacity: 0.9;
        position: relative;
        z-index: 1;
      }
      
      /* ===== INFO PANEL ===== */
      .info-panel {
        background: linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(254, 243, 199, 0.8) 0%, rgba(253, 230, 138, 0.8) 100%);
        color: #92400E;
        padding: 1.25rem; /* Reduced padding */
        border-radius: var(--element-radius);
        font-size: 0.9rem; /* Slightly smaller font */
        margin-top: 2rem;
        border-left: 4px solid var(--warning-color);
        display: flex;
        align-items: flex-start;
        gap: 0.75rem;
        backdrop-filter: blur(10px);
        position: relative;
        z-index: 1;
      }
      
      [data-bs-theme='dark'] .info-panel {
        background: linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(120, 53, 15, 0.8) 0%, rgba(180, 83, 9, 0.8) 100%);
        color: #FEF3C7;
        border-left-color: #D97706;
      }
      
      /* ===== ENHANCED TABLE STYLES WITH DROPDOWN SUMMARIES ===== */
      .table-container {
        border-radius: var(--element-radius);
        overflow: hidden;
        box-shadow: 0 8px 40px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08);
        background: var(--glass-bg);
        backdrop-filter: blur(20px);
      }
      
      .news-table {

        line-height: 1.5 !important;
        background: transparent !important;
      }
      
      /* ENHANCED: Adjusted column widths for better content fitting */
      .news-table tbody td:nth-child(1) { /* Source column - smaller */
        white-space: nowrap;

      }
      
      /* Summary dropdown styles */
      .summary-toggle {

      }

    # JavaScript for summary dropdown functionality
    tags$script(HTML("
      $(document).on('click', '.summary-toggle', function() {
        var $this = $(this);
        var $content = $this.closest('td').find('.summary-content');
        var isVisible = $content.hasClass('show');
        
        // Close all other open summaries
        $('.summary-content').removeClass('show');
        $('.summary-toggle').html('<i class=\"fas fa-chevron-down\"></i> Summary');
        
        if (!isVisible) {
          $content.addClass('show');
          $this.html('<i class=\"fas fa-chevron-up\"></i> Summary');
        }
      });
    ")),
    
    # UI Structure
    div(class = "news-dashboard",
        # Hero Section
        div(class = "news-hero",
            h1(icon("newspaper", class = "me-3"), "Global News Dashboard"),
            p("Stay informed with real-time headlines from trusted international sources")
        ),
        
        # Main Content Grid
        div(class = "news-grid",
            # Left Column - Sources Panel (Now smaller)
            div(
              div(class = "news-card",
                  div(class = "news-card-header",
                      icon("rss", class = "me-2"),

                  ),

                      div(class = "sources-panel",

                              shinyWidgets::checkboxGroupButtons(
                                inputId  = ns("news_src"),
                                label    = NULL,
                                choices  = setNames(srcs$rss, srcs$source),
                                selected = unname(preselected),
                                direction = "vertical",
                                justified = FALSE,
                                size = "normal",
                                checkIcon = list(yes = NULL, no = NULL),
                                width = "100%"
                              )
                          )
                      ),

                      div(id = ns("progress_container"), class = "progress-container",
                          div(class = "progress-header",
                              span(icon("rotate"), "Fetching headlines..."),
                              span(id = ns("progress_percent"), "0%")
                          ),
                          div(class = "progress-bar-modern",
                              div(id = ns("progress_fill"), class = "progress-fill")
                          ),
                          div(class = "progress-stats",
                              span(id = ns("progress_current"), "Starting..."),
                              span(id = ns("progress_total"), "Total: 0 sources")
                          )
                      ),
                      
                      # Refresh Button
                      actionButton(ns("news_refresh"), 
                                   icon = icon("rotate"), 
                                   label = "Refresh Headlines",
                                   class = "btn-news-primary"),
                      
                      # Info Panel
                      div(class = "info-panel",
                          icon("lightbulb", class = "mt-1"),
                          div(
                            tags$strong("Pro Tip:"),
                            " Select your preferred sources and click Refresh to fetch the latest headlines instantly."
                          )
                      )
                  )
              )
            ),
            
            # Right Column - News Table (Now larger)
            div(
              div(class = "news-card",
                  div(class = "news-card-header",
                      icon("newspaper", class = "me-2"),
                      "Latest Headlines"
                  ),
                  div(class = "news-card-body",
                      div(class = "table-container",
                          DT::DTOutput(ns("news_tbl"))
                      )
                  ),
                  # Stats Bar
                  uiOutput(ns("news_stats"))
              )
            )
        )
    )
  )
}

# --------------------- Server ---------------------
mod_news_server <- function(id){
  moduleServer(id, function(input, output, session){
    ns <- session$ns
    
    # rss -> Source map (includes your original + added sources)
    src_map <- .news_sources_ext() |>
      dplyr::transmute(src = rss, Source = source)
    
    # robust, no-throw parser (handles RFC822/ISO/various; returns POSIXct or NA)
    .safe_parse_pub <- function(x) {
      if (inherits(x, "POSIXt")) return(x)
      x <- as.character(x)
      orders <- c(
        "a, d b Y H:M:S z", "a, d b Y H:M:S Z",
        "Y-m-d H:M:S z", "Y-m-d H:M:S",
        "Y-m-dTH:M:S z", "Y-m-dTH:M:S",
        "Ymd HMS", "Ymd HM", "Ymd",
        "d b Y H:M:S z", "d b Y H:M:S"
      )
      dt <- tryCatch(
        suppressWarnings(lubridate::parse_date_time(x, orders = orders, tz = "UTC", quiet = TRUE)),
        error = function(e) {
          as.POSIXct(rep(NA, length(x)), origin = "1970-01-01", tz = "UTC")
        }
      )
      if (!inherits(dt, "POSIXt")) {
        dt <- as.POSIXct(rep(NA, length(x)), origin = "1970-01-01", tz = "UTC")
      }
      lubridate::with_tz(dt, tzone = Sys.timezone())
    }
    
    # Hide progress bar initially
    shinyjs::hide("progress_container")
    
    # ---- Enhanced Fetch logic with modern progress bar ----
    news_df <- eventReactive(input$news_refresh, {
      req(input$news_src)
      sources <- input$news_src
      
      if (length(sources) == 0) {
        showNotification("📰 Please select at least one news source", type = "warning")
        return(tibble::tibble())
      }
      
      # Disable the button + show progress while fetching
      shinyjs::disable("news_refresh")
      shinyjs::show("progress_container")
      
      # Update progress bar initial state using proper shinyjs methods
      shinyjs::html("progress_percent", "0%")
      shinyjs::runjs(paste0("$('#", ns("progress_fill"), "').css('width', '0%')"))
      shinyjs::html("progress_current", "Initializing...")
      shinyjs::html("progress_total", paste("Total:", length(sources), "sources"))
      
      on.exit({
        # Restore button and hide progress after delay
        shinyjs::enable("news_refresh")
        shinyjs::delay(1500, shinyjs::hide("progress_container"))
      }, add = TRUE)
      
      all_data <- list()
      n <- length(sources)
      
      # Use progress bar for better UX
      withProgress(message = 'Fetching headlines', value = 0, {
        for (i in seq_along(sources)) {
          u <- sources[i]
          source_name <- src_map$Source[src_map$src == u] %||% u
          
          # Update progress
          progress_pct <- round((i / n) * 100)
          shinyjs::html("progress_percent", paste0(progress_pct, "%"))
          shinyjs::runjs(paste0("$('#", ns("progress_fill"), "').css('width', '", progress_pct, "%')"))
          shinyjs::html("progress_current", paste("Processing:", source_name))
          
          # Update Shiny progress
          incProgress(1/n, detail = paste("Reading:", source_name))
          
          # Fetch RSS with error handling
          res <- try(fetch_rss(u, n = 10), silent = TRUE)
          
          if (inherits(res, "try-error") || is.null(res)) {
            # Silently skip failed sources
            next
          }
          
          if (!is.data.frame(res)) {
            res <- tibble::as_tibble(res)
          }
          
          # Ensure required columns exist
          if (!"title"     %in% names(res)) res$title     <- NA_character_
          if (!"link"      %in% names(res)) res$link      <- NA_character_
          if (!"published" %in% names(res)) res$published <- NA
          if (!"summary"   %in% names(res)) res$summary   <- NA_character_
          
          res$src <- u
          all_data[[i]] <- res
          
          # Small delay to show progress animation
          Sys.sleep(0.3)
        }
      })
      
      # Combine all data
      dat <- dplyr::bind_rows(all_data)
      
      if (nrow(dat) == 0) {
        showNotification("❌ No articles could be fetched from selected sources", type = "warning")
        return(tibble::tibble(
          Source=character(), Title=character(), Published=character(),
          Link=character(), Summary=character()
        ))
      }
      
      # Process data
      tmp <- dat |>
        dplyr::left_join(src_map, by = "src") |>
        dplyr::mutate(Source = dplyr::coalesce(.data$Source, .data$src))
      
      ord <- .safe_parse_pub(tmp$published)
      pub_display <- ifelse(!is.na(ord),
                            format(ord, "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M"),
                            as.character(tmp$published))
      
      result <- tibble::tibble(
        Source   = tmp$Source,
        Title    = tmp$title,
        Published= pub_display,
        Link     = dplyr::if_else(is.na(tmp$link) | tmp$link == "", "",
                                  paste0('<a class="news-link-btn" href="', tmp$link,
                                         '" target="_blank" rel="noopener">', 
                                         '<i class="fas fa-external-link-alt"></i> Read</a>')),
        Summary  = tmp$summary,
        .ord     = as.numeric(ord)
      ) |>
        dplyr::arrange(dplyr::desc(.ord), dplyr::desc(Published)) |>
        dplyr::select(-.ord)
      
      # Show success notification
      showNotification(
        paste("✅ Fetched", nrow(result), "articles from", length(unique(result$Source)), "sources"), 
        type = "message", 
        duration = 4
      )
      
      result
    }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
    
    # News stats output
    output$news_stats <- renderUI({
      dat <- news_df()
      total_articles <- nrow(dat)
      total_sources <- length(unique(dat$Source))
      selected_count <- length(input$news_src)
      latest_update <- if(total_articles > 0) format(Sys.time(), "%H:%M") else "Never"
      
      div(class = "stats-bar",
          span(class = "stats-item",
               icon("chart-bar"), 
               paste(total_articles, "articles")
          ),
          span(class = "stats-item",
               icon("globe"), 
               paste(total_sources, "/", selected_count, "sources")
          ),
          span(class = "stats-item",
               icon("clock"), 
               paste("Updated:", latest_update)
          )
      )
    })
    
    output$news_tbl <- DT::renderDT({
      dat <- news_df()
      
      if (nrow(dat) == 0) {
        return(
          DT::datatable(
            tibble::tibble(
              Message = "No headlines available",
              Instruction = "Select news sources and click 'Refresh Headlines' to load articles"
            ), 
            selection = "none",
            rownames = FALSE,
            options = list(
              dom = 't', 
              ordering = FALSE,
              pageLength = 5,
              autoWidth = TRUE
            ),
            class = "news-table"
          ) |> 
            DT::formatStyle(columns = 1:2, textAlign = 'center', fontSize = '16px')
        )
      }
      
      # Create the data table with dropdown summaries
      dat_display <- dat |>
        dplyr::mutate(
          Summary = purrr::map2_chr(Summary, 1:n(), function(summary, i) {
            if (is.na(summary) || summary == "") {
              return("")
            }
            # Truncate long summaries for the dropdown button
            summary_preview <- ifelse(nchar(summary) > 100, 
                                      paste0(substr(summary, 1, 100), "..."), 
                                      summary)
            
            paste0(
              '<button class="summary-toggle" data-id="', i, '">',
              '<i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i> Summary',
              '</button>',
              '<div class="summary-content" id="summary-', i, '">',
              '<strong>Summary:</strong><br>',
              summary_preview,
              '</div>'
            )
          })
        )
      
      # Escape only the columns that don't contain HTML (Source, Title, Published)
      # Don't escape Link and Summary columns as they contain HTML
      esc_idx <- which(names(dat_display) %in% c("Source", "Title", "Published"))
      
      DT::datatable(
        dat_display,
        escape = esc_idx,  # Only escape non-HTML columns
        rownames = FALSE,
        class = "news-table compact stripe hover",
        extensions = c("Buttons", "Scroller", "Responsive"),
        options = list(
          pageLength = 15,
          deferRender = TRUE,
          scrollY = "70vh",
          scroller = TRUE,
          scrollX = FALSE,  # Disable horizontal scrolling
          autoWidth = TRUE,
          responsive = TRUE,
          searchHighlight = TRUE,
          dom = 'Bfrtip',
          buttons = list(
            list(extend = "copy", title = "News Headlines"),
            list(extend = "csv", title = "News Headlines"),
            list(extend = "excel", title = "News Headlines"),
            list(
              extend = "pdfHtml5",
              title = "News Headlines",
              orientation = "landscape",
              pageSize = "A4"
            ),
            list(extend = "print", title = "News Headlines")
          ),
          # ===== Column widths (ADJUSTED FOR MAXIMUM HEADLINES SPACE) =====
          columnDefs = list(
            list(className = "dt-center", targets = which(names(dat_display) == "Link") - 1L),
            list(className = "dt-left", targets = which(names(dat_display) %in% c("Title", "Summary")) - 1L),
            list(className = "dt-nowrap", targets = which(names(dat_display) %in% c("Source", "Published")) - 1L),
            list(width = '6%',  targets = which(names(dat_display) == "Source")    - 1L),  # Smaller
            list(width = '65%', targets = which(names(dat_display) == "Title")     - 1L),  # Much wider for headlines and summaries
            list(width = '8%',  targets = which(names(dat_display) == "Published") - 1L),  # Smaller
            list(width = '6%',  targets = which(names(dat_display) == "Link")      - 1L),  # Smaller
            list(width = '15%', targets = which(names(dat_display) == "Summary")   - 1L)   # Adjusted to fit better
          ),
          language = list(
            emptyTable = "No headlines available. Select sources and click Refresh.",
            zeroRecords = "No matching headlines found.",
            info = "Showing _START_ to _END_ of _TOTAL_ headlines",
            infoEmpty = "No headlines available",
            search = "🔍 Search headlines:",
            paginate = list(
              previous = "‹ Previous",
              `next` = "Next ›"
            )
          )
        )
      ) |>
        DT::formatStyle(columns = colnames(dat_display), fontSize = '14px', lineHeight = '1.4')
    })
  })
}

# tiny helper for %||%
`%||%` <- function(x, y) if (is.null(x) || length(x) == 0) y else x
=== R/mod_premium.R ===
# ============================
# mod_premium.R  —  Enhanced Premium Notes Interface (Render-safe text)
# ============================

suppressPackageStartupMessages({
  library(shiny)
  library(bslib)
  library(shinyWidgets)
  library(shinyjs)
  library(DT)
})

# ---- global rendering safety (helps on Render/servers) ----
options(bitmapType = "cairo")        # force Cairo for raster devices
if (tryCatch(.Platform$OS.type == "windows", error = function(e) FALSE)) {
  # Leave locale alone on Windows unless you want to set it explicitly
} else {
  # UTF-8 locale on Linux/macOS (best-effort, quietly ignore failures)
  try(Sys.setlocale("LC_CTYPE", "en_US.UTF-8"), silent = TRUE)
}

# ---- helpers ----
`%||%` <- function(a, b) if (!is.null(a) && length(a)>0 && !is.na(a[1]) && (!is.character(a[1]) || !identical(a[1], ""))) a[1] else b

# Pick a good sans font available on the server, register with showtext, return family alias
.pick_render_font <- function(alias = "ui") {
  if (!requireNamespace("systemfonts", quietly = TRUE)) return("sans")
  if (!requireNamespace("showtext", quietly = TRUE))    return("sans")
  
  # Common, widely-available, Unicode-friendly choices on Linux containers
  preferred <- c(
    "DejaVu Sans", "Noto Sans", "Liberation Sans",
    "Arial", "Segoe UI", "Ubuntu", "Cantarell", "Roboto"
  )
  
  sys <- try(systemfonts::system_fonts(), silent = TRUE)
  if (inherits(sys, "try-error")) return("sans")
  
  families <- unique(sys$family)
  chosen <- preferred[preferred %in% families][1] %||% "sans"
  
  # Map family -> file path(s)
  fm <- sys[sys$family == chosen & sys$weight == 400 & sys$style == "normal", , drop = FALSE]
  if (nrow(fm) == 0) {
    fm <- sys[sys$family == chosen, , drop = FALSE]
  }
  regular_path <- fm$path[1] %||% NA_character_
  
  # Register with showtext if we found a file
  if (!is.na(regular_path)) {
    try({
      showtext::font_add(family = alias, regular = regular_path)
      showtext::showtext_auto()
      return(alias)
    }, silent = TRUE)
  }
  
  "sans"
}

.get_available_notes <- function() {
  notes_dir <- file.path(getwd(), "db", "notes")
  
  if (!dir.exists(notes_dir)) {
    dir.create(notes_dir, recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)
    return(data.frame(
      file_name = character(),
      display_name = character(),
      stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    ))
  }
  
  pdf_files <- list.files(notes_dir, pattern = "\\.pdf$", full.names = FALSE, ignore.case = TRUE)
  
  if (length(pdf_files) == 0) {
    return(data.frame(
      file_name = character(),
      display_name = character(),
      stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    ))
  }
  
  data.frame(
    file_name = pdf_files,
    display_name = gsub("\\.pdf$", "", pdf_files, ignore.case = TRUE),
    stringsAsFactors = FALSE
  )
}

.create_demo_pdf <- function(input_pdf_path, output_pdf_path, max_pages = 3) {
  tryCatch({
    if (!requireNamespace("pdftools", quietly = TRUE)) {
      return(list(success = FALSE, error = "pdftools package required for preview"))
    }
    if (!requireNamespace("showtext", quietly = TRUE)) {
      return(list(success = FALSE, error = "showtext package required for Unicode text on server"))
    }
    
    # Font setup (robust on minimal Linux images)
    family <- .pick_render_font("ui")
    
    pdf_info_result <- pdftools::pdf_info(input_pdf_path)
    total_pages <- pdf_info_result$pages
    pages_to_show <- min(max_pages, total_pages)
    
    # ---- Create a cover page as PDF with Cairo + showtext ----
    cover_path <- tempfile(fileext = ".pdf")
    grDevices::cairo_pdf(cover_path, width = 8.5, height = 11)  # <- key change
    par(mar = c(0, 0, 0, 0), bg = "#f8f9fa", family = family)
    plot(0, 0, type = "n", xlim = c(0, 1), ylim = c(0, 1),
         xlab = "", ylab = "", axes = FALSE, xaxs = "i", yaxs = "i")
    
    # Title
    text(0.5, 0.85, "CSS BUDDY", cex = 2.5, font = 2, col = "#2c3e50")
    text(0.5, 0.78, "Premium MCQs Notes", cex = 1.5, col = "#3498db")
    
    # Package Type
    text(0.5, 0.68, "CSS MPT/CCE Screening/One Paper MCQs", cex = 1.1, font = 2, col = "#e74c3c")
    
    # Page Information
    text(0.5, 0.60, paste("Total Pages in Full Notes:", total_pages), cex = 1.1, col = "#7f8c8d")
    text(0.5, 0.55, paste("Preview Showing:", pages_to_show, "pages"), cex = 1.1, col = "#7f8c8d")
    
    # Syllabus Coverage (use explicit Unicode escape for bullet)
    text(0.5, 0.45, "Complete MCQs Coverage For:", cex = 1, font = 2, col = "#2c3e50")
    text(0.5, 0.40, "\u2022 CSS MPT (Modified Preliminary Test)", cex = 0.9, col = "#34495e")
    text(0.5, 0.36, "\u2022 CCE Screening Test", cex = 0.9, col = "#34495e")
    text(0.5, 0.32, "\u2022 One Paper MCQs Based Exams", cex = 0.9, col = "#34495e")
    
    # Demo Warning
    text(0.5, 0.22, "DEMO PREVIEW - LIMITED CONTENT", cex = 1.2, font = 2, col = "#e74c3c")
    text(0.5, 0.16, "Purchase full notes to access complete content", cex = 0.9, col = "#95a5a6")
    
    # Contact Info
    text(0.5, 0.10, "Email: cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com", cex = 0.8, col = "#3498db")
    text(0.5, 0.06, "WhatsApp: +92-328-2769211", cex = 0.8, col = "#3498db")
    
    dev.off()
    
    # ---- Subset original & combine with cover ----
    demo_pages_path <- tempfile(fileext = ".pdf")
    pdftools::pdf_subset(input_pdf_path, demo_pages_path, pages = 1:pages_to_show)
    pdftools::pdf_combine(c(cover_path, demo_pages_path), output = output_pdf_path)
    
    unlink(cover_path)
    unlink(demo_pages_path)
    
    return(list(
      success = TRUE,
      pages_shown = pages_to_show,
      total_pages = total_pages
    ))
  }, error = function(e) {
    return(list(
      success = FALSE,
      error = e$message
    ))
  })
}

# ---------- ENHANCED SERVER LOGIC ----------
mod_premium_server <- function(id, user_email = reactive(NULL)){
  moduleServer(id, function(input, output, session){
    ns <- session$ns
    
    # Ensure fonts/showtext initialized for any renderPlot/graphics in this session
    if (requireNamespace("showtext", quietly = TRUE)) {
      .pick_render_font("ui")
    }
    
    # Reactive for available notes
    available_notes <- reactive({
      notes <- .get_available_notes()
      return(notes)
    })
    
    # Enhanced demo preview section
    output$demo_preview_section <- renderUI({
      notes <- available_notes()
      if (nrow(notes) == 0) {
        notes_dir <- file.path(getwd(), "db", "notes")
        return(
          div(class = "premium-card",
              div(class = "premium-card-body text-center",
                  h5("📚 Demo Preview", class = "text-primary-custom"),
                  div(class = "premium-alert premium-alert-warning",
                      icon("exclamation-triangle", class = "me-2"),
                      div(
                        strong("Setup Required"),
                        tags$br(),
                        "Add PDF files to:",
                        tags$code(notes_dir)
                      )
                  )
              )
          )
        )
      }
      
      div(class = "premium-card",
          div(class = "premium-card-body",
              h5(class = "mb-4 text-center text-primary-custom", "👀 Preview Demo Notes"),
              div(class = "mb-4",
                  pickerInput(
                    ns("selected_note"),
                    label = "Choose subject to preview:",
                    choices = setNames(notes$file_name, notes$display_name),
                    selected = if (nrow(notes) > 0) notes$file_name[1] else NULL,
                    options = list(
                      style = "btn-primary",
                      size = 5
                    )
                  )
              ),
              uiOutput(ns("pdf_preview_ui"))
          )
      )
    })
    
    # Enhanced PDF Preview
    output$pdf_preview_ui <- renderUI({
      req(input$selected_note)
      
      note_file <- input$selected_note
      notes <- available_notes()
      
      if (nrow(notes) == 0) return(NULL)
      
      # Create demo PDF path
      demo_pdf_path <- file.path(tempdir(), paste0("demo_", note_file))
      original_pdf_path <- file.path(getwd(), "db", "notes", note_file)
      
      if (!file.exists(original_pdf_path)) {
        return(div(class = "premium-alert premium-alert-warning text-center", 
                   icon("times-circle", class = "me-2"),
                   "Notes file not found."))
      }
      
      # Create demo PDF (now using cairo_pdf + showtext internally)
      demo_result <- .create_demo_pdf(original_pdf_path, demo_pdf_path, max_pages = 3)
      
      if (demo_result$success) {
        # Encode the PDF for display
        pdf_data <- readBin(demo_pdf_path, "raw", file.info(demo_pdf_path)$size)
        if (!requireNamespace("base64enc", quietly = TRUE)) {
          return(div(class = "premium-alert premium-alert-warning text-center",
                     icon("exclamation-circle", class = "me-2"),
                     "Package 'base64enc' is required to preview PDF inline."))
        }
        pdf_b64 <- base64enc::base64encode(pdf_data)
        
        tagList(
          div(class = "pdf-viewer-premium",
              div(class = "p-3 bg-primary text-white d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center",
                  tags$span(icon("eye"), " Demo Preview"),
                  tags$span(class = "badge bg-light text-primary",
                            paste("Showing", demo_result$pages_shown, "of", demo_result$total_pages, "pages"))
              ),
              tags$iframe(
                style = "width: 100%; height: 450px; border: none;",
                src = paste0("data:application/pdf;base64,", pdf_b64)
              )
          ),
          div(class = "text-center mt-4",
              actionButton(ns("get_full_notes"), "🚀 Get Full Notes →", 
                           class = "btn-premium btn-premium-primary btn-lg")
          )
        )
      } else {
        div(class = "premium-alert premium-alert-warning text-center",
            icon("exclamation-circle", class = "me-2"),
            "Error loading preview: ", 
            tags$br(),
            tags$small(demo_result$error))
      }
    })
    
    # Enhanced button handlers with animations
    observeEvent(input$get_full_notes, {
      runjs("$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $('.step-indicator-premium').offset().top - 100 }, 600);")
      showNotification(
        div(icon("rocket"), "Great choice! Proceed with payment and contact us for instant delivery."),
        type = "message",
        duration = 5
      )
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$buy_now, {
      runjs("$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $('.step-indicator-premium').offset().top - 100 }, 600);")
      showNotification(
        div(icon("credit-card"), "Please complete payment and share receipt for instant delivery."),
        type = "message", 
        duration = 5
      )
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$view_demo, {
      if (nrow(available_notes()) > 0) {
        runjs("$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $('#demo_preview_section').offset().top - 100 }, 600);")
      } else {
        showNotification(
          div(icon("exclamation-triangle"), "No demo notes available. Please check setup."),
          type = "warning"
        )
      }
    })
    
    # Contact buttons
    observeEvent(input$direct_whatsapp, {
      runjs("window.open('https://wa.me/923282769211?text=Hello! I want to purchase CSS MCQs notes and have made the payment.', '_blank');")
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$direct_email, {
      runjs("window.open('mailto:cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com?subject=CSS MCQs Notes Purchase&body=Hello! I have made the payment for CSS MCQs notes. Here are my details:', '_blank');")
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$quick_whatsapp, {
      runjs("window.open('https://wa.me/923282769211', '_blank');")
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$quick_email, {
      runjs("window.open('mailto:cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com', '_blank');")
    })
  })
}

=== R/mod_partner.R ===

# --- local helper to avoid scoping issues
clear_existing_requests_safe__local <- function(conn, user_a, user_b) {
  if (!exists("ensure_study_partner_schema")) return(invisible(TRUE))
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  try({
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "
          DELETE FROM study_partner_connections
           WHERE ((user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?) OR (user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?))
             AND status <> 'accepted'
        ", params = list(as.integer(user_a), as.integer(user_b),
                         as.integer(user_b), as.integer(user_a)))
  }, silent = TRUE)
  invisible(TRUE)
}
# R/mod_partner.R - Complete Study Partner Module with Delete Features

# ---------------------------------------------------------------------
# Helper: partner_extra_injections(ns)
# Adds CSS and JS to make the "progress-step" circles behave like buttons
# (hover, focus outline, ripple) and sends input$goto_step on click.
partner_extra_injections <- function(ns) {
  tagList(
    tags$style(HTML("
      .progress-step {
        cursor: pointer;
        position: relative;
        transition: transform .08s ease, box-shadow .15s ease, filter .15s ease;
        outline: none;
      }
      .progress-step:focus-visible {
        box-shadow: 0 0 0 3px rgba(59,130,246,.45);
        border-radius: 9999px;
      }
      .progress-step:hover {
        transform: translateY(-1px);
        filter: brightness(1.02);
      }
      .progress-step::after {
        content: '';
        position: absolute;
        inset: 0;
        border-radius: 9999px;
        opacity: 0;
        transform: scale(0.8);
        transition: transform .2s ease, opacity .2s ease;
        background: currentColor;
        mix-blend-mode: multiply;
        pointer-events: none;
      }
      .progress-step:active::after {
        opacity: .08;
        transform: scale(1.05);
      }
    ")),
    tags$script(HTML(sprintf("
      (function() {
        function enableStepClicks(root) {
          if (!root) return;
          var nodes = root.querySelectorAll('.progress-step');
          nodes.forEach(function(n) {
            if (n._sp_bound) return;
            n._sp_bound = true;
            n.addEventListener('click', function() {
              var step = n.getAttribute('data-step') || n.dataset.step;
              if (!step) return;
              Shiny.setInputValue('%s', step, {priority: 'event'});
            });
          });
        }
        document.addEventListener('shiny:connected', function() {
          enableStepClicks(document);
        });
        new MutationObserver(function(muts) {
          muts.forEach(function(m) {
            if (m.addedNodes) m.addedNodes.forEach(function(node) {
              if (node.querySelector) enableStepClicks(node);
            });
          });
        }).observe(document.documentElement, {subtree:true, childList:true});
      })();", ns('goto_step'))))
  )
}
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------
