                                            textAreaInput(ns("topics_of_interest"), 
                                                          "Specific Topics of Interest",
                                                          placeholder = "Enter specific topics you want to focus on (comma separated)\nExample: Microeconomics, Constitutional Law, International Relations",
                                                          rows = 3)
                                     )
                                   )
                            )
                          ),
                          
                          div(class = "text-center mt-4",
                              actionButton(ns("save_preferences"), "Save Preferences & Continue", 
                                           class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary", icon = icon("save"))
                          )
                      ),
                      
                      # Navigation Controls
                      div(class = "navigation-controls",
                          # No back button on first step
                          div(),
                          div(
                            actionButton(ns("next_to_step2"), "Next: Discover Partners →", 
                                         class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary", icon = icon("arrow-right"))
                          )
                      )
                  )
                ),
                
                # Tab 2: Find Partners
                tabPanel(
                  "Find Partners",
                  icon = icon("search"),
                  div(class = "card-soft p-4 my-3",
                      h4("🔍 Step 2: Discover Study Partners", class = "mb-3"),
                      p("Connect with fellow students who share your optional subjects and learning goals.", class = "text-muted"),
                      
                      # Quick Actions
                      div(class = "partner-step-card",
                          h5("🚀 Quick Actions", class = "mb-3"),
                          fluidRow(
                            column(12,
                                   div(class = "action-buttons",
                                       actionButton(ns("refresh_partners"), "Refresh Partner List", 
                                                    class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary", icon = icon("sync")),
                                       actionButton(ns("view_my_profile"), "View My Profile", 
                                                    class = "btn-modern btn-outline-primary", icon = icon("eye")),
                                       actionButton(ns("how_matching_works"), "How Matching Works", 
                                                    class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary", icon = icon("info-circle"))
                                   )
                            )
                          )
                      ),
                      
                      # Filters
                      div(class = "partner-step-card",
                          h5("🎛️ Filter Partners", class = "mb-3"),
                          fluidRow(
                            column(3,
                                   selectizeInput(ns("filter_goals"), "Learning Goals",
                                                  choices = c("All Goals" = "all",
                                                              "Exam Preparation" = "exam_prep",
                                                              "Conceptual Understanding" = "concepts",
                                                              "Project Collaboration" = "projects",
                                                              "Discussion & Debate" = "discussion"),
                                                  selected = "all")
                            ),
                            column(3,
                                   selectizeInput(ns("filter_style"), "Interaction Style",
                                                  choices = c("All Styles" = "all",
                                                              "One-on-One" = "one_on_one",
                                                              "Small Group" = "small_group",
                                                              "Large Group" = "large_group"),
                                                  selected = "all")
                            ),
                            column(3,
                                   selectizeInput(ns("filter_level"), "Proficiency Level",
                                                  choices = c("All Levels" = "all",
                                                              "Beginner" = "beginner",
                                                              "Intermediate" = "intermediate",
                                                              "Advanced" = "advanced"),
                                                  selected = "all")
                            ),
                            column(3,
                                   selectizeInput(ns("filter_subjects"), "Optional Subjects",
                                                  choices = c("All Subjects" = "all"),
                                                  selected = "all")
                            )
                          )
                      ),
                      
                      # Partners List
                      uiOutput(ns("partners_list")),
                      
                      # Empty State
                      div(id = ns("no_partners_message"), 
                          class = "empty-state",
                          style = "display: none;",
                          div(class = "empty-state-icon", icon("users")),
                          h5("No potential partners found"),
                          p("Try adjusting your filters or check back later for new matches."),
                          actionButton(ns("setup_preferences_first"), "Setup Preferences First", 
                                       class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary mt-3")
                      ),
                      
                      # Navigation Controls
                      div(class = "navigation-controls",
                          div(
                            actionButton(ns("back_to_step1"), "← Back: Setup", 
                                         class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary", icon = icon("arrow-left"))
                          ),
                          div(
                            actionButton(ns("next_to_step3"), "Next: My Connections →", 
                                         class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary", icon = icon("arrow-right"))
                          )
                      )
                  )
                ),
                
                # Tab 3: Connection Requests
                tabPanel(
                  "Connection Requests",
                  icon = icon("envelope"),
                  div(class = "card-soft p-4 my-3",
                      h4("📩 Step 3: Manage Connection Requests",
                         uiOutput(ns("pending_requests_badge"))),
                      p("Review incoming requests and track your sent connection invitations.", class = "text-muted"),
                      
                      tabsetPanel(
                        tabPanel("Incoming Requests",
                                 icon = icon("inbox"),
                                 uiOutput(ns("incoming_requests")),
                                 
                                 div(id = ns("no_incoming_requests"), 
                                     class = "empty-state",
                                     style = "display: none;",
                                     div(class = "empty-state-icon", icon("inbox")),
                                     h5("No incoming requests"),
                                     p("When other users send you connection requests, they'll appear here.")
                                 )
                        ),
                        
                        tabPanel("Sent Requests",
                                 icon = icon("paper-plane"),
                                 uiOutput(ns("sent_requests")),
                                 
                                 div(id = ns("no_sent_requests"), 
                                     class = "empty-state",
                                     style = "display: none;",
                                     div(class = "empty-state-icon", icon("paper-plane")),
                                     h5("No sent requests"),
                                     p("Requests you send to other users will appear here.")
                                 )
                        )
                      ),
                      
                      # Navigation Controls
                      div(class = "navigation-controls",
                          div(
                            actionButton(ns("back_to_step2"), "← Back: Discover", 
                                         class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary", icon = icon("arrow-left"))
                          ),
                          div(
                            actionButton(ns("next_to_step4"), "Next: Collaborate →", 
                                         class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary", icon = icon("arrow-right"))
                          )
                      )
                  )
                ),
                
                # Tab 4: My Connections
                tabPanel(
                  "My Connections",
                  icon = icon("users"),
                  div(class = "card-soft p-4 my-3",
                      h4("🤝 Step 3: Your Study Partners", class = "mb-3"),
                      p("Manage your connected partners and start studying together.", class = "text-muted"),
                      
                      # Progress Navigation
                      uiOutput(ns("progress_navigation")),
                      
                      uiOutput(ns("connections_header")),
                      uiOutput(ns("connections_list")),
                      
                      div(id = ns("no_connections_message"), 
                          class = "empty-state",
                          style = "display: none;",
                          div(class = "empty-state-icon", icon("user-friends")),
                          h5("No connections yet"),
                          p("Start by finding and connecting with potential partners in the 'Find Partners' tab."),
                          actionButton(ns("find_partners_now"), "Find Partners Now", 
                                       class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary mt-3")
                      ),
                      
                      # Navigation Controls
                      div(class = "navigation-controls",
                          div(
                            actionButton(ns("back_to_step2a"), "← Back: Discover", 
                                         class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary", icon = icon("arrow-left"))
                          ),
                          div(
                            actionButton(ns("next_to_step4a"), "Next: Collaborate →", 
                                         class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary", icon = icon("arrow-right"))
                          )
                      )
                  )
                ),
                
                # Tab 5: Messaging
                tabPanel(
                  "Messages",
                  icon = icon("comments"),
                  div(class = "card-soft p-4 my-3",
                      h4("💬 Study Partner Messages", class = "mb-3"),
                      p("Chat with your connected study partners about shared topics and study plans.", class = "text-muted"),
                      
                      fluidRow(
                        column(4,
                               div(class = "partner-step-card",
                                   h5("Your Study Partners", class = "mb-3"),
                                   uiOutput(ns("message_connections_list"))
                               )
                        ),
                        column(8,
                               uiOutput(ns("chat_interface"))
                        )
                      ),
                      
                      # Navigation Controls
                      div(class = "navigation-controls",
                          div(
                            actionButton(ns("back_to_step3"), "← Back: Connections", 
                                         class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary", icon = icon("arrow-left"))
                          ),
                          div(
                            actionButton(ns("next_to_step4b"), "Next: Collaborate →", 
                                         class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary", icon = icon("arrow-right"))
                          )
                      )
                  )
                ),
                
                # NEW TAB: Collaboration Hub
                tabPanel(
                  "Collaboration Hub",
                  icon = icon("rocket"),
                  div(class = "card-soft p-4 my-3",
                      h4("🚀 Step 4: Collaboration Hub", class = "mb-3"),
                      p("Work together with your study partners on shared goals and subjects.", class = "text-muted"),
                      
                      # Quick Actions Grid
                      uiOutput(ns("collaboration_quick_actions")),
                      
                      # Collaboration Features Grid
                      fluidRow(
                        column(6,
                               div(class = "collaboration-card",
                                   h4(icon("bullseye"), "Shared Study Goals"),
                                   uiOutput(ns("shared_goals_list")),
                                   actionButton(ns("create_shared_goal"), "Create Shared Goal", 
                                                class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary mt-3", icon = icon("plus"))
                               ),
                               
                               div(class = "collaboration-card",
                                   h4(icon("file"), "Resource Sharing"),
                                   uiOutput(ns("shared_resources_list")),
                                   actionButton(ns("share_resource"), "Share Resource", 
                                                class = "btn-modern btn-modern-success mt-3", icon = icon("upload"))
                               )
                        ),
                        column(6,
                               div(class = "collaboration-card",
                                   h4(icon("calendar"), "Study Sessions"),
                                   uiOutput(ns("upcoming_sessions")),
                                   actionButton(ns("schedule_session"), "Schedule Session", 
                                                class = "btn-modern btn-modern-info mt-3", icon = icon("calendar-plus"))
                               ),
                               
                               div(class = "collaboration-card",
                                   h4(icon("chart-line"), "Progress Tracking"),
                                   uiOutput(ns("collaboration_progress")),
                                   actionButton(ns("update_progress"), "Update Progress", 
                                                class = "btn-modern btn-modern-warning mt-3", icon = icon("chart-bar"))
                               )
                        )
                      ),
                      
                      # Active Collaborations
                      div(class = "partner-step-card mt-4",
                          h4(icon("users"), "Active Collaborations", class = "mb-3"),
                          uiOutput(ns("active_collaborations_list"))
                      ),
                      
                      # Navigation Controls
                      div(class = "navigation-controls",
                          div(
                            actionButton(ns("back_to_step3a"), "← Back: Connections", 
                                         class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary", icon = icon("arrow-left"))
                          )
                          # No next button on final step
                      )
                  )
                ),
                
                # Tab 6: Study Groups
                tabPanel(
                  "Study Groups",
                  icon = icon("layer-group"),
                  div(class = "card-soft p-4 my-3",
                      h4("👥 Study Groups", class = "mb-3"),
                      div(class = "partner-step-card",
                          div(class = "alert alert-info",
                              icon("rocket"), 
                              strong(" Enhanced Collaboration Features Coming Soon:"),
                              tags$ul(class = "mt-2",
                                      tags$li("Create and join subject-specific study groups"),
                                      tags$li("Schedule group study sessions with calendar integration"),
                                      tags$li("Shared notes and resource libraries"),
                                      tags$li("Real-time collaborative whiteboard"),
                                      tags$li("Group progress tracking and milestones")
                              )
                          )
                      )
                  )
                )
              )
          )
  )
}

mod_partner_server <- function(id, user_id, conn) {
  
  
  # ----- Override: always consider steps completed so navigation is never blocked -----
  if (exists("rv") && is.list(rv) && !is.null(rv$step_completion_status)) {
    rv$step_completion_status$step1 <- TRUE
    rv$step_completion_status$step2 <- TRUE
    rv$step_completion_status$step3 <- TRUE
    rv$step_completion_status$step4 <- TRUE
  }
  # --------------------------------------------------------------------
  
  
  
  
  
  
  moduleServer(id, function(input, output, session) {
    ns <- session$ns
    
    # Ensure schema is complete when module starts
    ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
    
    # Reactive values
    rv <- reactiveValues(
      preferences = NULL,
      potential_partners = NULL,
      incoming_requests = NULL,
      sent_requests = NULL,
      connections = NULL,
      current_step = 1,
      selected_connection = NULL,
      messages = NULL,
      unread_count = 0,
      pending_requests_count = 0,
      connection_modal_shown = FALSE,
      selected_partner = NULL,
      # Collaboration reactive values
      shared_goals = NULL,
      shared_resources = NULL,
      study_sessions = NULL,
      collaboration_progress = NULL,
      active_collaborations = NULL,
      selected_partner_for_session = NULL,
      # Auto-progression tracking
      has_connections = FALSE,
      has_started_collaboration = FALSE,
      # Navigation tracking
      step_completion_status = list(
        step1 = FALSE,
        step2 = FALSE,
        step3 = FALSE,
        step4 = FALSE
      ),
      # FIXED: Improved modal state tracking with timestamps
      modal_states = list(
        connection_modal_active = FALSE,
        connection_modal_time = NULL,
        session_modal_active = FALSE,
        session_modal_time = NULL,
        goal_modal_active = FALSE,
        goal_modal_time = NULL,
        resource_modal_active = FALSE,
        resource_modal_time = NULL,
        progress_modal_active = FALSE,
        progress_modal_time = NULL,
        delete_modal_active = FALSE,
        delete_modal_time = NULL
      ),
      # FIXED: Track button clicks to prevent multiple triggers
      button_clicks = list(),
      last_click_time = NULL,
      # NEW: Track items to delete
      item_to_delete = NULL,
      delete_type = NULL
    )
    
    # ----- Free navigation observers (unconditional) -----
    observeEvent(input$next_to_step2, ignoreInit = TRUE, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Find Partners")
    })
    observeEvent(input$next_to_step3, ignoreInit = TRUE, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "My Connections")
    })
    observeEvent(input$next_to_step4, ignoreInit = TRUE, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
    })
    observeEvent(input$next_to_step4a, ignoreInit = TRUE, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
    })
    observeEvent(input$next_to_step4b, ignoreInit = TRUE, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
    })
    observeEvent(input$goto_step, ignoreInit = TRUE, {
      target_tab <- switch(as.character(input$goto_step),
                           "1" = "Setup Preferences",
                           "2" = "Find Partners",
                           "3" = "My Connections",
                           "4" = "Collaboration Hub",
                           "Setup Preferences"
      )
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = target_tab)
    })
    # --------------------------------------------------------------------
    # Helper function to check if modal can be shown
    can_show_modal <- function(modal_type) {
      current_time <- Sys.time()
      
      # Check if modal is already active
      if (rv$modal_states[[paste0(modal_type, "_modal_active")]]) {
        return(FALSE)
      }
      
      # Check rate limiting - prevent multiple modals within 500ms
      if (!is.null(rv$last_click_time)) {
        time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, rv$last_click_time, units = "secs")) * 1000
        if (time_diff < 500) {
          return(FALSE)
        }
      }
      
      rv$last_click_time <- current_time
      return(TRUE)
    }
    
    # Helper function to set modal state
    set_modal_state <- function(modal_type, state) {
      rv$modal_states[[paste0(modal_type, "_modal_active")]] <- state
      if (state) {
        rv$modal_states[[paste0(modal_type, "_modal_time")]] <- Sys.time()
      }
      
      # --- CLEAR ANY EXISTING REQUESTS BETWEEN TWO USERS ---------------------------
      # Remove any non-accepted requests between user_a and user_b (both directions)
      clear_existing_requests_safe <- function(conn, user_a, user_b) {
        ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
        try({
          DBI::dbExecute(conn, "
          DELETE FROM study_partner_connections
           WHERE ((user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?) OR (user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?))
             AND status <> 'accepted'
        ", params = list(as.integer(user_a), as.integer(user_b), as.integer(user_b), as.integer(user_a)))
        }, silent = TRUE)
        invisible(TRUE)
      }
      
    }
    
    # NEW: Database functions for delete operations - FIXED VERSION
    delete_shared_goal_db <- function(conn, goal_id, user_id) {
      tryCatch({
        # First check if the user owns this goal - FIXED: Use user_id column instead of created_by
        check_query <- "SELECT user_id FROM shared_goals WHERE id = ?"
        check_result <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, check_query, params = list(goal_id))
        
        if (nrow(check_result) == 0) {
          return(list(success = FALSE, message = "Goal not found"))
        }
        
        # FIXED: Compare as integers to avoid type mismatch
        if (as.integer(check_result$user_id[1]) != as.integer(user_id)) {
          return(list(success = FALSE, message = "You can only delete goals you created"))
        }
        
        # Delete the goal
        delete_query <- "DELETE FROM shared_goals WHERE id = ?"
        DBI::dbExecute(conn, delete_query, params = list(goal_id))
        
        return(list(success = TRUE, message = "Goal deleted successfully"))
      }, error = function(e) {
        return(list(success = FALSE, message = paste("Database error:", e$message)))
      })
    }
    
    delete_study_session_db <- function(conn, session_id, user_id) {
      tryCatch({
        # First check if the user owns this session - FIXED: Use created_by column
        check_query <- "SELECT created_by FROM study_sessions WHERE id = ?"
        check_result <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, check_query, params = list(session_id))
        
        if (nrow(check_result) == 0) {
          return(list(success = FALSE, message = "Session not found"))
        }
        
        # FIXED: Compare as integers
        if (as.integer(check_result$created_by[1]) != as.integer(user_id)) {
          return(list(success = FALSE, message = "You can only delete sessions you created"))
        }
        
        # Delete the session
        delete_query <- "DELETE FROM study_sessions WHERE id = ?"
        DBI::dbExecute(conn, delete_query, params = list(session_id))
        
        return(list(success = TRUE, message = "Study session deleted successfully"))
      }, error = function(e) {
        return(list(success = FALSE, message = paste("Database error:", e$message)))
      })
    }
    
    delete_shared_resource_db <- function(conn, resource_id, user_id) {
      tryCatch({
        # First check if the user owns this resource - FIXED: Use user_id column instead of shared_by
        check_query <- "SELECT user_id FROM shared_resources WHERE id = ?"
        check_result <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, check_query, params = list(resource_id))
        
        if (nrow(check_result) == 0) {
          return(list(success = FALSE, message = "Resource not found"))
        }
        
        # FIXED: Compare as integers
        if (as.integer(check_result$user_id[1]) != as.integer(user_id)) {
          return(list(success = FALSE, message = "You can only delete resources you shared"))
        }
        
        # Get file path if exists
        file_query <- "SELECT file_path FROM shared_resources WHERE id = ?"
        file_result <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, file_query, params = list(resource_id))
        
        # Delete the file from filesystem if it exists
        if (nrow(file_result) > 0 && !is.na(file_result$file_path) && file.exists(file_result$file_path)) {
          file.remove(file_result$file_path)
        }
        
        # Delete the resource record
        delete_query <- "DELETE FROM shared_resources WHERE id = ?"
        DBI::dbExecute(conn, delete_query, params = list(resource_id))
        
        return(list(success = TRUE, message = "Resource deleted successfully"))
      }, error = function(e) {
        return(list(success = FALSE, message = paste("Database error:", e$message)))
      })
    }
    
    # NEW: Show delete confirmation modal
    show_delete_confirmation_modal <- function(item_type, item_id, item_name) {
      if (can_show_modal("delete")) {
        set_modal_state("delete", TRUE)
        rv$item_to_delete <- item_id
        rv$delete_type <- item_type
        
        showModal(modalDialog(
          title = tags$div(icon("exclamation-triangle"), " Confirm Deletion"),
          easyClose = TRUE,
          footer = NULL,
          size = "m",
          div(
            h4("Are you sure you want to delete this item?"),
            p("This action cannot be undone."),
            tags$div(
              class = "alert alert-warning",
              icon("warning"),
              strong("Item: "), item_name
            ),
            div(class = "action-buttons mt-4",
                actionButton(ns("cancel_delete"), "Cancel", 
                             class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary"),
                actionButton(ns("confirm_delete"), "Yes, Delete", 
                             class = "btn-modern btn-modern-danger", icon = icon("trash"))
            )
          )
        ))
      }
    }
    
    # NEW: Handle delete confirmation
    observeEvent(input$confirm_delete, {
      req(rv$item_to_delete, rv$delete_type, user_id())
      
      result <- NULL
      
      if (rv$delete_type == "goal") {
        result <- delete_shared_goal_db(conn, rv$item_to_delete, user_id())
      } else if (rv$delete_type == "session") {
        result <- delete_study_session_db(conn, rv$item_to_delete, user_id())
      } else if (rv$delete_type == "resource") {
        result <- delete_shared_resource_db(conn, rv$item_to_delete, user_id())
      }
      
      if (!is.null(result) && result$success) {
        showNotification(paste("✅", result$message), type = "message")
        
        # Refresh the relevant data
        if (rv$delete_type == "goal") {
          rv$shared_goals <- get_shared_goals(conn, user_id())
        } else if (rv$delete_type == "session") {
          rv$study_sessions <- get_study_sessions_fixed(conn, user_id())
        } else if (rv$delete_type == "resource") {
          rv$shared_resources <- get_shared_resources(conn, user_id())
        }
      } else if (!is.null(result)) {
        showNotification(paste("❌", result$message), type = "error")
      }
      
      removeModal()
      set_modal_state("delete", FALSE)
      rv$item_to_delete <- NULL
      rv$delete_type <- NULL
    })
    
    # NEW: Handle delete cancellation
    observeEvent(input$cancel_delete, {
      removeModal()
      set_modal_state("delete", FALSE)
      rv$item_to_delete <- NULL
      rv$delete_type <- NULL
    })
    
    
    # --- Remove an accepted connection between two users (both directions) ---
    remove_connection_fixed <- function(conn, current_user_id, partner_id) {
      ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
      try({
        # Delete accepted connections both directions
        DBI::dbExecute(conn, "
          DELETE FROM study_partner_connections
           WHERE status = 'accepted'
             AND ((user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?) OR (user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?))
        ",
                       params = list(as.integer(current_user_id), as.integer(partner_id),
                                     as.integer(partner_id), as.integer(current_user_id)))
      }, silent = TRUE)
      # Optionally, keep messages/history; do not delete messages to preserve chat history
      return(list(success = TRUE, message = "Connection removed"))
    }
    
    
    
    # --- Helper: check live connection status from DB (accepted both directions) ---
    is_connected_between <- function(conn, user_a, user_b) {
      ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
      tryCatch({
        res <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "
          SELECT 1 FROM study_partner_connections
           WHERE status = 'accepted'
             AND ((user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?) OR (user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?))
           LIMIT 1",
                               params = list(as.integer(user_a), as.integer(user_b),
                                             as.integer(user_b), as.integer(user_a)))
        nrow(res) > 0
      }, error = function(e) FALSE)
    }
    
    # --- Helper: get latest request status between two users ---
    # Returns one of: 'mutual','incoming','outgoing','none'
    get_pair_request_status <- function(conn, user_a, user_b) {
      ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
      reqs <- tryCatch({
        DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "
          SELECT user_id, partner_id, status
            FROM study_partner_connections
           WHERE status <> 'accepted'
             AND ((user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?) OR (user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?))",
                        params = list(as.integer(user_a), as.integer(user_b),
                                      as.integer(user_b), as.integer(user_a)))
      }, error = function(e) data.frame())
      
      if (nrow(reqs) == 0) return("none")
      has_a_to_b <- any(reqs$user_id == as.integer(user_a) & reqs$partner_id == as.integer(user_b))
      has_b_to_a <- any(reqs$user_id == as.integer(user_b) & reqs$partner_id == as.integer(user_a))
      if (has_a_to_b && has_b_to_a) return("mutual")
      if (has_b_to_a) return("incoming")
      if (has_a_to_b) return("outgoing")
      "none"
    }
    
    # Step validation functions
    is_step_completed <- function(step) {
      switch(step,
             "1" = !is.null(rv$preferences),
             "2" = !is.null(rv$preferences), # Step 2 is accessible once preferences are set
             "3" = !is.null(rv$connections) && nrow(rv$connections) > 0,
             "4" = TRUE, # Collaboration hub is always accessible
             FALSE
      )
    }
    
    # Step validation alert
    output$step_validation_alert <- renderUI({
      req(input$partner_tabs)
      
      current_tab <- input$partner_tabs
      current_step <- switch(current_tab,
                             "Setup Preferences" = 1,
                             "Find Partners" = 2,
                             "Connection Requests" = 3,
                             "My Connections" = 3,
                             "Messages" = 3,
                             "Collaboration Hub" = 4,
                             1
      )
      
      if (current_step > 1 && !is_step_completed(current_step - 1)) {
        div(class = "step-validation-alert",
            icon("exclamation-triangle"),
            strong(" Step Not Completed: "),
            "Please complete the previous step before proceeding. ",
            actionLink(ns("go_to_previous_step"), "Go back and complete it now.")
        )
      }
    })
    
    # Navigate to previous step when validation alert is clicked
    observeEvent(input$go_to_previous_step, {
      current_tab <- input$partner_tabs
      current_step <- switch(current_tab,
                             "Setup Preferences" = 1,
                             "Find Partners" = 2,
                             "Connection Requests" = 3,
                             "My Connections" = 3,
                             "Messages" = 3,
                             "Collaboration Hub" = 4,
                             1
      )
      
      if (current_step > 1) {
        target_tab <- switch(current_step - 1,
                             "1" = "Setup Preferences",
                             "2" = "Find Partners",
                             "3" = "My Connections"
        )
        updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = target_tab)
      }
    })
    
    # Navigation button handlers
    observeEvent(input$next_to_step2, {
      if (is_step_completed(1)) {
        updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Find Partners")
      } else {
        showNotification("Please save your study preferences first.", type = "warning")
      }
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$next_to_step3, {
      if (is_step_completed(2)) {
        updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "My Connections")
      } else {
        showNotification("Please set up your preferences first.", type = "warning")
      }
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$next_to_step4, {
      if (is_step_completed(3)) {
        updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
      } else {
        showNotification("You need to have at least one connection to collaborate.", type = "warning")
      }
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$next_to_step4a, {
      if (is_step_completed(3)) {
        updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
      } else {
        showNotification("You need to have at least one connection to collaborate.", type = "warning")
      }
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$next_to_step4b, {
      if (is_step_completed(3)) {
        updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
      } else {
        showNotification("You need to have at least one connection to collaborate.", type = "warning")
      }
    })
    
    # Back button handlers
    observeEvent(input$back_to_step1, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Setup Preferences")
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$back_to_step2, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Find Partners")
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$back_to_step2a, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Find Partners")
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$back_to_step3, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "My Connections")
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$back_to_step3a, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "My Connections")
    })
    
    # Progress step click handlers
    observe({
      # Add click handlers for progress steps
      for (i in 1:4) {
        local({
          step <- i
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("step", step)]], {
            if (is_step_completed(step) || step < rv$current_step) {
              # Allow navigation to completed steps or previous steps
              target_tab <- switch(step,
                                   "1" = "Setup Preferences",
                                   "2" = "Find Partners", 
                                   "3" = "My Connections",
                                   "4" = "Collaboration Hub"
              )
              updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = target_tab)
            } else {
              showNotification(
                paste("Please complete step", step - 1, "first before moving to step", step),
                type = "warning"
              )
            }
          })
        })
      }
    })
    
    # Unread messages badge
    output$unread_messages_badge <- renderUI({
      if (rv$unread_count > 0) {
        div(style = "position: relative; display: inline-block;",
            icon("comments", class = "text-white", style = "font-size: 1.5em;"),
            div(class = "unread-badge", rv$unread_count)
        )
      } else {
        icon("comments", class = "text-white", style = "font-size: 1.5em;")
      }
    })
    
    # Pending requests badge for tab
    output$pending_requests_badge <- renderUI({
      if (rv$pending_requests_count > 0) {
        span(class = "notification-badge", rv$pending_requests_count)
      }
    })
    
    # Update counts periodically
    observe({
      req(user_id())
      invalidateLater(10000)  # Update every 10 seconds
      
      # Update unread message count
      rv$unread_count <- get_unread_message_count(conn, user_id())
      
      # Update pending requests count
      pending_req <- get_connection_requests(conn, user_id(), "incoming")
      if (!is.null(pending_req) && nrow(pending_req) > 0) {
        rv$pending_requests_count <- nrow(pending_req)
      } else {
        rv$pending_requests_count <- 0
      }
    })
    
    # AUTO-PROGRESSION LOGIC - Check user progress and update steps
    observe({
      req(user_id())
      
      # Check if user has preferences (Step 1 completed)
      has_prefs <- !is.null(rv$preferences)
      rv$step_completion_status$step1 <- has_prefs
      
      # Check if user has connections (Step 3 completed)
      has_conns <- !is.null(rv$connections) && nrow(rv$connections) > 0
      rv$has_connections <- has_conns
      rv$step_completion_status$step3 <- has_conns
      
      # Step 2 is considered completed if preferences are set
      rv$step_completion_status$step2 <- has_prefs
      
      # Step 4 is always accessible but marked completed if user has collaborations
      has_collab <- has_conns && (
        (!is.null(rv$study_sessions) && nrow(rv$study_sessions) > 0) ||
          (!is.null(rv$shared_goals) && nrow(rv$shared_goals) > 0) ||
          (!is.null(rv$shared_resources) && nrow(rv$shared_resources) > 0)
      )
      rv$has_started_collaboration <- has_collab
      rv$step_completion_status$step4 <- has_collab
      
      # Update current step based on progress
      new_step <- 1
      if (has_prefs) new_step <- 2
      if (has_conns) new_step <- 3
      if (has_collab) new_step <- 4
      
      if (new_step != rv$current_step) {
        rv$current_step <- new_step
        update_progress_ui()
      }
    })
    
    # Helper function to update progress indicator UI
    update_progress_ui <- function() {
      for (i in 1:4) {
        step_id <- paste0("step", i)
        if (i < rv$current_step) {
          shinyjs::runjs(paste0("$('#", ns(step_id), "').addClass('completed').removeClass('active');"))
        } else if (i == rv$current_step) {
          shinyjs::runjs(paste0("$('#", ns(step_id), "').addClass('active').removeClass('completed');"))
        } else {
          shinyjs::runjs(paste0("$('#", ns(step_id), "').removeClass('active completed');"))
        }
      }
    }
    
    # Enhanced tab switching with validation
    observeEvent(input$partner_tabs, {
      # Map tabs to steps for validation
      steps <- list(
        "Setup Preferences" = 1,
        "Find Partners" = 2,
        "Connection Requests" = 3,
        "My Connections" = 3,
        "Messages" = 3,
        "Collaboration Hub" = 4
      )
      
      requested_step <- steps[[input$partner_tabs]] %||% 1
      
      # Check if user is trying to navigate forward without completing previous steps
      if (requested_step > rv$current_step) {
        showNotification(
          paste("💡 Complete step", rv$current_step, "first to unlock this feature!"),
          type = "warning", duration = 3
        )
        # Revert to current step tab
        current_tab <- switch(rv$current_step,
                              "1" = "Setup Preferences",
                              "2" = "Find Partners",
                              "3" = "My Connections",
                              "4" = "Collaboration Hub"
        )
        if (current_tab != input$partner_tabs) {
          updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = current_tab)
        }
      }
      
      # Refresh data when switching to relevant tabs
      if (input$partner_tabs == "Connection Requests") {
        refresh_connection_requests()
      } else if (input$partner_tabs == "My Connections") {
        refresh_connections()
      } else if (input$partner_tabs == "Messages") {
        refresh_connections()
      } else if (input$partner_tabs == "Collaboration Hub") {
        refresh_collaboration_data()
      }
    })
    
    # Helper function to refresh connection requests
    refresh_connection_requests <- function() {
      req(user_id())
      rv$incoming_requests <- get_connection_requests(conn, user_id(), "incoming")
      rv$sent_requests <- get_connection_requests(conn, user_id(), "sent")
      
      # Update pending count
      if (!is.null(rv$incoming_requests) && nrow(rv$incoming_requests) > 0) {
        rv$pending_requests_count <- nrow(rv$incoming_requests)
      } else {
        rv$pending_requests_count <- 0
      }
    }
    
    # Helper function to refresh connections
    refresh_connections <- function() {
      req(user_id())
      rv$connections <- get_connections(conn, user_id())
      # Ensure all connections are shown (dedupe by partner_id & keep all rows)
      if (!is.null(rv$connections) && 'partner_id' %in% names(rv$connections)) {
        rv$connections <- rv$connections[!duplicated(rv$connections$partner_id), , drop = FALSE]
      }
    }
    
    # Helper function to refresh collaboration data
    refresh_collaboration_data <- function() {
      req(user_id())
      
      # Load shared goals
      rv$shared_goals <- get_shared_goals(conn, user_id())
      
      # Load shared resources
      rv$shared_resources <- get_shared_resources(conn, user_id())
      
      # Load study sessions
      rv$study_sessions <- get_study_sessions_fixed(conn, user_id())
      
      # Load progress data
      rv$collaboration_progress <- get_collaboration_progress(conn, user_id())
      
      # Load active collaborations
      rv$active_collaborations <- get_active_collaborations(conn, user_id())
    }
    
    # Progress Navigation
    output$progress_navigation <- renderUI({
      if (rv$current_step >= 3) {
        div(class = "progress-navigation",
            h5("Ready for the Next Step?"),
            p("You've made connections! Now it's time to start collaborating with your study partners."),
            actionButton(ns("nav_to_collaboration"), 
                         "Go to Collaboration Hub →", 
                         class = "btn-modern btn-modern-success",
                         icon = icon("rocket"))
        )
      }
    })
    
    # Collaboration Quick Actions
    output$collaboration_quick_actions <- renderUI({
      if (rv$has_connections) {
        div(class = "quick-action-grid",
            div(class = "quick-action-card", 
                onclick = paste0("Shiny.setInputValue('", ns("quick_schedule"), "', Math.random())"),
                div(class = "quick-action-icon", icon("calendar")),
                h5("Schedule Session"),
                p("Plan a study session")
            ),
            div(class = "quick-action-card",
                onclick = paste0("Shiny.setInputValue('", ns("quick_goal"), "', Math.random())"),
                div(class = "quick-action-icon", icon("bullseye")),
                h5("Set Shared Goal"),
                p("Create learning objectives")
            ),
            div(class = "quick-action-card",
                onclick = paste0("Shiny.setInputValue('", ns("quick_resource"), "', Math.random())"),
                div(class = "quick-action-icon", icon("file")),
                h5("Share Resources"),
                p("Exchange study materials")
            ),
            div(class = "quick-action-card",
                onclick = paste0("Shiny.setInputValue('", ns("quick_progress"), "', Math.random())"),
                div(class = "quick-action-icon", icon("chart-line")),
                h5("Track Progress"),
                p("Monitor learning journey")
            )
        )
      }
    })
    
    # FIXED: Quick action handlers with proper modal state tracking
    observeEvent(input$quick_schedule, {
      if (!is.null(rv$connections) && nrow(rv$connections) > 0 && can_show_modal("session")) {
        set_modal_state("session", TRUE)
        show_study_session_modal(rv$connections$partner_id[1])
      } else if (is.null(rv$connections) || nrow(rv$connections) == 0) {
        showNotification("❌ You need to connect with partners first", type = "error")
      }
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$quick_goal, {
      if (can_show_modal("goal")) {
        set_modal_state("goal", TRUE)
        show_shared_goal_modal()
      }
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$quick_resource, {
      if (can_show_modal("resource")) {
        set_modal_state("resource", TRUE)
        show_share_resource_modal()
      }
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$quick_progress, {
      if (can_show_modal("progress")) {
        set_modal_state("progress", TRUE)
        show_progress_tracking_modal()
      }
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$nav_to_collaboration, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
    })
    
    
    # Safety: reset modal state flags periodically to avoid stuck states if a modal was closed externally
    observe({
      invalidateLater(3000)
      # If no modal is visible in DOM, clear flags
      shinyjs::runjs(sprintf("Shiny.setInputValue('%s', !!$('.modal:visible').length)", ns('.__modal_visible_check__')))
    })
    observeEvent(input$.__modal_visible_check__, {
      if (isTRUE(input$.__modal_visible_check__ == 0)) {
        # Clear all modal flags
        rv$modal_states$connection_modal_active <- FALSE
        rv$modal_states$session_modal_active <- FALSE
        rv$modal_states$goal_modal_active <- FALSE
        rv$modal_states$resource_modal_active <- FALSE
        rv$modal_states$progress_modal_active <- FALSE
        rv$modal_states$delete_modal_active <- FALSE
      }
    }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
    
    # Preferences status card
    output$preferences_status_card <- renderUI({
      if (is.null(rv$preferences)) {
        div(class = "partner-step-card",
            div(class = "alert alert-warning",
                icon("exclamation-triangle"),
                strong(" Setup Required:"),
                " Complete your study preferences to start finding partners."
            )
        )
      } else {
        div(class = "partner-step-card",
            div(class = "d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center",
                div(
                  h5("✅ Preferences Saved", class = "text-success mb-1"),
                  p("Your study profile is complete and ready for matching.", class = "text-muted mb-0")
                ),
                span(class = "success-badge", "Ready")
            )
        )
      }
    })
    
    # Load user preferences
    observe({
      req(user_id())
      rv$preferences <- get_study_preferences(conn, user_id())
      
      # Update UI with existing preferences
      if (!is.null(rv$preferences)) {
        updateSelectizeInput(session, "learning_goals", selected = rv$preferences$learning_goals)
        updateSelectizeInput(session, "interaction_style", selected = rv$preferences$interaction_style)
        updateSelectizeInput(session, "proficiency_level", selected = rv$preferences$proficiency_level)
        updateSelectizeInput(session, "timezone", selected = rv$preferences$timezone)
        
        # Parse availability JSON
        if (!is.na(rv$preferences$availability) && nzchar(rv$preferences$availability)) {
          availability_list <- tryCatch(
            jsonlite::fromJSON(rv$preferences$availability),
            error = function(e) character()
          )
          if (length(availability_list) > 0) {
            updateSelectizeInput(session, "availability", selected = availability_list)
          }
        }
        
        # Parse topics JSON
        if (!is.na(rv$preferences$topics_of_interest) && nzchar(rv$preferences$topics_of_interest)) {
          topics_list <- tryCatch(
            jsonlite::fromJSON(rv$preferences$topics_of_interest),
            error = function(e) character()
          )
          if (length(topics_list) > 0) {
            updateTextAreaInput(session, "topics_of_interest", 
                                value = paste(topics_list, collapse = ", "))
          }
        }
      }
    })
    
    # Save preferences
    observeEvent(input$save_preferences, {
      req(user_id())
      
      # Parse topics of interest
      topics <- if (nzchar(input$topics_of_interest)) {
        strsplit(input$topics_of_interest, "\\s*,\\s*")[[1]]
      } else {
        character()
      }
      topics <- topics[nzchar(topics)]
      
      tryCatch({
        result <- upsert_study_preferences(
          conn,
          user_id(),
          learning_goals = input$learning_goals,
          interaction_style = input$interaction_style,
          availability = input$availability,
          timezone = input$timezone,
          topics_of_interest = topics,
          proficiency_level = input$proficiency_level
        )
        
        if (!is.null(result)) {
          showNotification("✅ Preferences saved successfully! You can now discover partners.", type = "message")
          rv$preferences <- result
          
          # Auto-switch to Find Partners tab
          updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Find Partners")
        } else {
          stop("Failed to save preferences")
        }
      }, error = function(e) {
        showNotification("❌ Error saving preferences", type = "error")
      })
    })
    
    # Find potential partners
    observeEvent(input$refresh_partners, {
      req(user_id())
      rv$potential_partners <- find_potential_partners(conn, user_id(), limit = 50)
    })
    
    # Load potential partners on tab activation
    observe({
      if (input$partner_tabs == "Find Partners") {
        req(user_id())
        rv$potential_partners <- find_potential_partners(conn, user_id(), limit = 50)
      }
    })
    
    # Display potential partners - FIXED VERSION
    output$partners_list <- renderUI({
      req(rv$potential_partners)
      
      if (nrow(rv$potential_partners) == 0) {
        shinyjs::show("no_partners_message")
        return(NULL)
      } else {
        shinyjs::hide("no_partners_message")
      }
      
      # Apply filters
      filtered <- rv$potential_partners
      
      if (input$filter_goals != "all") {
        filtered <- filtered[filtered$learning_goals == input$filter_goals | is.na(filtered$learning_goals), ]
      }
      
      if (input$filter_style != "all") {
        filtered <- filtered[filtered$interaction_style == input$filter_style | is.na(filtered$interaction_style), ]
      }
      
      if (input$filter_level != "all") {
        filtered <- filtered[filtered$proficiency_level == input$filter_level | is.na(filtered$proficiency_level), ]
      }
      
      if (nrow(filtered) == 0) {
        return(div(class = "alert alert-warning", 
                   icon("filter"),
                   " No partners match your current filters. Try adjusting your filter settings."))
      }
      
      # Header with match count
      tagList(
        div(class = "partner-step-card",
            h5(sprintf("🎯 Found %d Potential Partners", nrow(filtered))),
            p("These users share your optional subjects and match your preferences.")
        ),
        
        # Partner cards with scenario handling - FIXED: Proper text handling
        lapply(seq_len(nrow(filtered)), function(i) {
          partner <- filtered[i, ]
          
          # Determine connection status safely
          # Recompute live status from DB to avoid stale flags (especially after removals)
          live_connected <- is_connected_between(conn, user_id(), partner$id)
          pair_req_status <- get_pair_request_status(conn, user_id(), partner$id)
          
          # Override flags based on live DB check
          is_connected_val <- isTRUE(live_connected)
          req_direction <- switch(pair_req_status,
                                  "mutual" = "mutual",
                                  "incoming" = "incoming",
                                  "outgoing" = "outgoing",
                                  "none" = "none",
                                  "none")
          
          # Prepare a subtle status badge for the card
          status_badge <- NULL
          if (is_connected_val) {
            status_badge <- span(class = "success-badge", "Connected")
          } else if (req_direction == "outgoing") {
            status_badge <- span(class = "pending-badge", "Request Sent")
          } else if (req_direction == "incoming") {
            status_badge <- span(class = "info-badge", "Incoming Request")
          } else if (req_direction == "mutual") {
            status_badge <- span(class = "mutual-badge", "Mutual Interest")
          } else {
            status_badge <- span(class = "warning-badge", "Not Connected")
          }
          
          is_connected_val <- if (!is.null(partner$is_connected) && length(partner$is_connected) > 0) {
            as.logical(partner$is_connected)
          } else {
            FALSE
          }
          
          has_pending_val <- if (!is.null(partner$has_pending_request) && length(partner$has_pending_request) > 0) {
            as.logical(partner$has_pending_request)
          } else {
            FALSE
          }
          
          has_incoming_val <- if (!is.null(partner$has_incoming_request) && length(partner$has_incoming_request) > 0) {
            as.logical(partner$has_incoming_request)
          } else {
            FALSE
          }
          
          req_direction <- partner$request_direction %||% "none"
          
          # FIXED: Handle common subjects list with proper character vector handling
          common_subjects_display <- "No subjects"
          if (!is.null(partner$common_subjects_list) && length(partner$common_subjects_list) > 0) {
            if (is.list(partner$common_subjects_list)) {
              # Extract the first element if it's a list
              subjects_vector <- partner$common_subjects_list[[1]]
              if (is.character(subjects_vector) && length(subjects_vector) > 0) {
                common_subjects_display <- paste(subjects_vector, collapse = ", ")
              }
            } else if (is.character(partner$common_subjects_list)) {
              common_subjects_display <- as.character(partner$common_subjects_list)
            }
          } else if (!is.null(partner$subjects) && nzchar(partner$subjects)) {
            common_subjects_display <- as.character(partner$subjects)
          }
          
          # Ensure it's a length-one character vector
          common_subjects_display <- as.character(common_subjects_display[1])
          
          # Safely extract other text fields
          partner_name <- as.character(partner$name %||% "Unknown User")[1]
          learning_goals <- as.character(partner$learning_goals %||% "Not specified")[1]
          interaction_style <- as.character(partner$interaction_style %||% "Not specified")[1]
          proficiency_level <- as.character(partner$proficiency_level %||% "Not specified")[1]
          city <- as.character(partner$city %||% "Not specified")[1]
          match_score <- round((partner$match_score %||% 0.8) * 100)
          
          # Determine card class based on connection status
          card_class <- "partner-card"
          if (req_direction == "mutual") {
            card_class <- paste(card_class, "mutual-interest-card")
          }
          
          div(class = card_class,
              fluidRow(
                column(8,
                       h5(partner_name),
                       div(class = "mb-2",
                           strong("Subjects: "), 
                           tags$span(class = "text-primary", common_subjects_display)
                       ),
                       div(class = "row text-muted small",
                           column(6,
                                  icon("bullseye"), " ", learning_goals
                           ),
                           column(6,
                                  icon("users"), " ", interaction_style
                           )
                       ),
                       div(class = "row text-muted small mt-1",
                           column(6,
                                  icon("chart-line"), " ", proficiency_level
                           ),
                           column(6,
                                  icon("map-marker-alt"), " ", city
                           )
                       )
                ),
                column(4, class = "text-right",
                       
                       div(class = "mb-3",
                           span(class = "match_score", 
                                match_score, "% Match")
                       ),
                       
                       # SCENARIO HANDLING: Different UI based on connection status
                       if (is_connected_val) {
                         tagList(
                           span(class = "success-badge", "Already Connected"),
                           br(), br(),
                           actionButton(ns(paste0("collaborate_", partner$id)), "Collaborate Now", 
                                        class = "btn-modern btn-modern-success btn-sm",
                                        icon = icon("rocket"))
                         )
                       } else if (req_direction == "mutual") {
                         # SCENARIO 1: Mutual Interest
                         div(
                           span(class = "mutual-badge mb-2", "Mutual Interest!"),
                           div(class = "action-buttons",
                               actionButton(ns(paste0("connect_mutual_", partner$id)), "Connect Now", 
                                            class = "btn-modern btn-modern-success btn-sm", 
                                            icon = icon("handshake")),
                               actionButton(ns(paste0("cancel_mine_", partner$id)), "Cancel Mine", 
                                            class = "btn-modern btn-outline-warning btn-sm", 
                                            icon = icon("times"))
                           )
                         )
                       } else if (req_direction == "incoming") {
                         # Incoming request only
                         {
                           # Map this partner to the actual connection request id
                           req_id_for_partner <- {
                             df <- rv$incoming_requests
                             rid <- NA
                             if (!is.null(df) && nrow(df) > 0) {
                               # Try join by common id columns
                               cols <- intersect(c("partner_id","from_id","requester_id","sender_id","user_id"), names(df))
                               for (cc in cols) {
                                 idx <- which(df[[cc]] == partner$id)
                                 if (length(idx) > 0) { rid <- df$id[idx[1]]; break }
                               }
                               # Fallback: try by name
                               if (is.na(rid) && "name" %in% names(df) && !is.null(partner$name)) {
                                 idx <- which(df$name == partner$name)
                                 if (length(idx) > 0) rid <- df$id[idx[1]]
                               }
                             }
                             rid
                           }
                           
                           div(class = "action-buttons",
                               actionButton(ns(paste0("accept_", req_id_for_partner %||% partner$id)), "Accept", 
                                            class = "btn-modern btn-modern-success btn-sm", icon = icon("check")),
                               actionButton(ns(paste0("reject_", req_id_for_partner %||% partner$id)), "Decline", 
                                            class = "btn-modern btn-outline-danger btn-sm", icon = icon("times"))
                           )
                         }
                       } else if (req_direction == "outgoing") {
                         # SCENARIO 3: Regular outgoing request
                         div(class = "action-buttons",
                             span(class = "pending-badge mb-2", "Request Sent"),
                             actionButton(ns(paste0("cancel_sent_", partner$id)), "Cancel",
                                          class = "btn-modern btn-outline-warning btn-sm", icon = icon("times"))
                         )
                       } else {
                         # No existing requests - can send new one
                         actionButton(ns(paste0("connect_", partner$id)), "Send Request",
                                      class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary btn-sm",
                                      icon = icon("user-plus"))
                       }
                )
              )
          )
        })
      )
    })
    
    # FIXED: Handle regular connection requests with proper modal state tracking
    observe({
      req(rv$potential_partners)
      
      for (partner_id in rv$potential_partners$id) {
        local({
          local_partner_id <- partner_id
          
          # FIXED: Use proper observer with unique tracking
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("connect_", local_partner_id)]], {
            # Check if this button was recently clicked
            button_key <- paste0("connect_", local_partner_id)
            current_time <- Sys.time()
            
            if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
              last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
              time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
              if (time_diff < 1) { # Prevent multiple clicks within 1 second
                return()
              }
            }
            
            rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
            
            # Check if there's an incoming request first (SCENARIO 2: Auto-accept)
            partner <- rv$potential_partners[rv$potential_partners$id == local_partner_id, ]
            has_incoming_val <- as.logical(partner$has_incoming_request)
            
            if (has_incoming_val) {
              # SCENARIO 2: Auto-accept when sending to someone who already sent you a request
              result <- accept_mutual_connection(conn, user_id(), local_partner_id)
              if (result$success) {
                showNotification("✅ Connection established! You both wanted to connect.", type = "message")
                # Refresh data
                rv$potential_partners <- find_potential_partners(conn, user_id(), limit = 50)
                refresh_connection_requests()
                refresh_connections()
                
                # AUTO-NAVIGATE to Collaboration Hub
                updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
              } else {
                showNotification(paste("❌", result$message), type = "error")
              }
            } else {
              # Regular connection request - show modal for icebreaker
              if (can_show_modal("connection")) {
                set_modal_state("connection", TRUE)
                
                showModal(modalDialog(
                  title = "Send Connection Request",
                  easyClose = TRUE,
                  footer = NULL,
                  size = "m",
                  div(
                    h5("🤝 Connect with Study Partner"),
                    p("Send a friendly message to introduce yourself and start studying together."),
                    textAreaInput(ns("icebreaker_message"), 
                                  "Icebreaker Message (optional)",
                                  placeholder = "Hi! I noticed we're both studying [subject]. Would you like to connect and study together?",
                                  rows = 4),
                    div(class = "action-buttons mt-4",
                        actionButton(ns("cancel_connect"), "Cancel", 
                                     class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary"),
                        actionButton(ns("confirm_connect"), "Send Connection Request", 
                                     class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary", icon = icon("paper-plane"))
                    )
                  )
                ))
                
                # Store the partner ID for the confirmation
                rv$selected_partner <- local_partner_id
              }
            }
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
        })
      }
    })
    
    # SCENARIO 1: Handle mutual connection - Connect Now
    observe({
      req(rv$potential_partners)
      
      for (partner_id in rv$potential_partners$id) {
        local({
          local_partner_id <- partner_id
          
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("connect_mutual_", local_partner_id)]], {
            # Check for recent clicks
            button_key <- paste0("connect_mutual_", local_partner_id)
            current_time <- Sys.time()
            
            if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
              last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
              time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
              if (time_diff < 1) {
                return()
              }
            }
            
            rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
            
            # Accept the incoming request and connect both users
            result <- accept_mutual_connection(conn, user_id(), local_partner_id)
            if (result$success) {
              showNotification("✅ Connection established! Taking you to collaborate...", type = "message")
              
              # Refresh data
              rv$potential_partners <- find_potential_partners(conn, user_id(), limit = 50)
              refresh_connection_requests()
              refresh_connections()
              
              # AUTO-NAVIGATE to Collaboration Hub
              updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
              
              # Show collaboration features
              showNotification(
                "🚀 Start collaborating! Schedule study sessions, set shared goals, and track progress.",
                type = "message", duration = 6
              )
            } else {
              showNotification(paste("❌", result$message), type = "error")
            }
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
        })
      }
    })
    
    # Handle collaborate now for already connected partners - FIXED
    observe({
      req(rv$potential_partners)
      
      for (partner_id in rv$potential_partners$id) {
        local({
          local_partner_id <- partner_id
          
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("collaborate_", local_partner_id)]], {
            button_key <- paste0("collaborate_", local_partner_id)
            current_time <- Sys.time()
            
            if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
              last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
              time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))

            rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time

            updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
            
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
        })
      }
    })
    
    # SCENARIO 1: Handle mutual connection - Cancel Mine
    observe({
      req(rv$potential_partners)
      
      for (partner_id in rv$potential_partners$id) {
        local({
          local_partner_id <- partner_id
          
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("cancel_mine_", local_partner_id)]], {
            button_key <- paste0("cancel_mine_", local_partner_id)
            current_time <- Sys.time()
            
            if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
              last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
              time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
              if (time_diff < 1) {
                return()
              }
            }
            
            rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
            
            # Cancel the user's outgoing request, keeping the incoming one
            result <- cancel_connection_request(conn, user_id(), local_partner_id)
            if (result$success) {
              showNotification("✅ Your request cancelled. You still have their incoming request.", type = "message")
              # Refresh data
              rv$potential_partners <- find_potential_partners(conn, user_id(), limit = 50)
              refresh_connection_requests()
            } else {
              showNotification(paste("❌", result$message), type = "error")
            }
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
        })
      }
    })
    
    # Handle cancel sent requests - FIXED
    observe({
      req(rv$potential_partners)
      
      for (partner_id in rv$potential_partners$id) {
        local({
          local_partner_id <- partner_id
          
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("cancel_sent_", local_partner_id)]], {
            button_key <- paste0("cancel_sent_", local_partner_id)
            current_time <- Sys.time()
            
            if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
              last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]

              if (time_diff < 1) {
                return()
              }
            }
            
            rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
            
            # Cancel the sent request
            result <- cancel_connection_request(conn, user_id(), local_partner_id)
            if (result$success) {
              showNotification("✅ Connection request cancelled", type = "message")
              # Refresh data
              rv$potential_partners <- find_potential_partners(conn, user_id(), limit = 50)
              refresh_connection_requests()
            } else {
              showNotification(paste("❌", result$message), type = "error")
            }
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
        })
      }
    })
    
    # Cancel connection request modal - FIXED: Reset modal state
    observeEvent(input$cancel_connect, {
      removeModal()
      set_modal_state("connection", FALSE)
      rv$selected_partner <- NULL
    })
    
    # Confirm connection request from modal - FIXED: Reset modal state
    observeEvent(input$confirm_connect, {
      req(rv$selected_partner, user_id())
      
      # Pre-clear any stale requests between the pair
      clear_existing_requests_safe__local(conn, user_id(), rv$selected_partner)
      # Send new request
      result <- send_connection_request(
        conn,
        user_id(),
        rv$selected_partner,
        input$icebreaker_message
      )
      
      if (result$success) {
        showNotification("✅ Connection request sent! They'll see your request in their inbox.", type = "message")
      } else {
        showNotification(paste("❌", result$message), type = "error")
      }
      
      removeModal()
      set_modal_state("connection", FALSE)
      rv$selected_partner <- NULL
      
      # Refresh the partners list and requests
      rv$potential_partners <- find_potential_partners(conn, user_id(), limit = 50)
      refresh_connection_requests()
    })
    
    # Load connection requests initially and periodically
    observe({
      req(user_id())
      refresh_connection_requests()
    })
    
    # Display incoming requests
    output$incoming_requests <- renderUI({
      req(rv$incoming_requests)
      
      if (nrow(rv$incoming_requests) == 0) {
        shinyjs::show("no_incoming_requests")
        return(NULL)
      } else {
        shinyjs::hide("no_incoming_requests")
      }
      
      tagList(
        div(class = "partner-step-card",
            h5(sprintf("📥 You have %d incoming request(s)", nrow(rv$incoming_requests))),
            p("Review and respond to connection requests from other users.")
        ),
        
        lapply(seq_len(nrow(rv$incoming_requests)), function(i) {
          req <- rv$incoming_requests[i, ]
          
          div(class = "partner-card connection-pending",
              h5(req$name),
              div(class = "mb-2",
                  strong("Subjects: "), 
                  tags$span(class = "text-primary", req$subjects)
              ),
              div(class = "text-muted small",
                  icon("graduation-cap"), " ", req$exam_type %||% "Not specified",
                  " • ",
                  icon("chart-line"), " ", req$prep_level %||% "Not specified"
              ),
              if (!is.na(req$icebreaker_message) && nzchar(req$icebreaker_message)) {
                div(class = "icebreaker-message", 
                    icon("quote-left", class = "me-1"),
                    req$icebreaker_message)
              },
              fluidRow(
                column(6,
                       p(class = "text-muted", 
                         icon("clock"),
                         " Received: ", format(as.POSIXct(req$created_at), "%b %d, %Y"))
                ),
                column(6, class = "text-right",
                       div(class = "action-buttons",
                           actionButton(ns(paste0("accept_", req$id)), "Accept", 
                                        class = "btn-modern btn-modern-success", icon = icon("check")),
                           actionButton(ns(paste0("reject_", req$id)), "Decline", 
                                        class = "btn-modern btn-outline-danger", icon = icon("times"))
                       )
                )
              )
          )
        })
      )
    })
    
    # Display sent requests
    output$sent_requests <- renderUI({
      req(rv$sent_requests)
      
      if (nrow(rv$sent_requests) == 0) {
        shinyjs::show("no_sent_requests")

      tagList(

                    "You: ", req$icebreaker_message)

                         span(class = "pending-badge ms-2", "Pending Response")
                       )
                ),
                column(6, class = "text-right",
                       actionButton(ns(paste0("cancel_sent_tab_", req$id)), "Cancel Request",
                                    class = "btn-modern btn-outline-warning btn-sm", icon = icon("times"))
                )
              )
          )
        })
      )
    })
    
    # Handle cancel sent requests from sent requests tab - FIXED
    observe({
      req(rv$sent_requests)
      
      for (req_id in rv$sent_requests$id) {

            button_key <- paste0("cancel_sent_tab_", local_req_id)
            current_time <- Sys.time()
            
            if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
              last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
              time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
              if (time_diff < 1) {
                return()
              }
            }
            
            rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
            
            result <- cancel_connection_request_by_id(conn, local_req_id, user_id())
            if (result$success) {

              refresh_connection_requests()
              rv$potential_partners <- find_potential_partners(conn, user_id(), limit = 50)
            } else {
              showNotification(paste("❌", result$message), type = "error")
            }
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
        })
      }
    })
    
    # Enhanced connection acceptance with auto-navigation - FIXED
    observe({
      req(rv$incoming_requests)
      
      for (req_id in rv$incoming_requests$id) {
        local({
          local_req_id <- req_id
          
          # Accept request
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("accept_", local_req_id)]], {
            button_key <- paste0("accept_", local_req_id)
            current_time <- Sys.time()
            
            if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
              last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
              time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
              if (time_diff < 1) {
                return()
              }
            }
            
            rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
            
            result <- update_connection_status(conn, local_req_id, user_id(), "accepted")
            if (result$success) {
              showNotification("✅ Connection accepted! Taking you to your connections...", type = "message")
              
              # Refresh data
              refresh_connection_requests()
              refresh_connections()
              rv$potential_partners <- find_potential_partners(conn, user_id(), limit = 50)
              rv$pending_requests_count <- max(0, rv$pending_requests_count - 1)

              updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "My Connections")
