              )
            }
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
          
          # Reject request
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("reject_", local_req_id)]], {
            button_key <- paste0("reject_", local_req_id)
            current_time <- Sys.time()
            
            if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
              last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
              time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
              if (time_diff < 1) {
                return()
              }
            }
            
            rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
            
            result <- update_connection_status(conn, local_req_id, user_id(), "rejected")
            if (result$success) {
              showNotification("❌ Connection declined", type = "warning")
              refresh_connection_requests()
              rv$potential_partners <- find_potential_partners(conn, user_id(), limit = 50)
              rv$pending_requests_count <- max(0, rv$pending_requests_count - 1)
            }
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
        })
      }
    })
    
    # Load connections initially
    observe({

      refresh_connections()
    })

    output$connections_header <- renderUI({

    output$connections_list <- renderUI({
      req(rv$connections)
      
      if (nrow(rv$connections) == 0) {
        shinyjs::show("no_connections_message")

      } else {
        shinyjs::hide("no_connections_message")
      }
      
      # Header with collaboration prompt
      header_card <- div(class = "partner-step-card",
                         h5("🎉 You're Connected! Ready to Collaborate?"),

                         fluidRow(

                           )
                         )
      )
      
      # Individual connection cards
      connection_cards <- lapply(seq_len(nrow(rv$connections)), function(i) {
        conn <- rv$connections[i, ]
        
        div(class = "partner-card",
            fluidRow(
              column(8,
                     h5(conn$name),
                     div(class = "mb-2",
                         strong("Email: "),

                     ),
                     div(class = "mb-2",
                         strong("Subjects: "), 
                         tags$span(class = "text-primary", conn$subjects)
                     ),
                     div(class = "row text-muted small",
                         column(6,
                                icon("bullseye"), " ", conn$learning_goals %||% "Not specified"
                         ),
                         column(6,
                                icon("users"), " ", conn$interaction_style %||% "Not specified"
                         )
                     ),
                     div(class = "row text-muted small mt-1",
                         column(6,
                                icon("chart-line"), " ", conn$proficiency_level %||% "Not specified"
                         ),
                         column(6,
                                icon("map-marker-alt"), " ", conn$city %||% "Not specified"
                         )
                     )
              ),
              column(4, class = "text-right",
                     span(class = "success-badge", "Connected"),
                     br(), br(),
                     div(class = "action-buttons",
                         actionButton(ns(paste0("message_conn_", conn$partner_id)), "Message",
                                      class = "btn-modern btn-outline-primary btn-sm", icon = icon("envelope")),
                         actionButton(ns(paste0("study_session_", conn$partner_id)), "Study Session",
                                      class = "btn-modern btn-modern-success btn-sm", icon = icon("video")),
                         actionButton(ns(paste0("share_resources_", conn$partner_id)), "Share Notes",
                                      class = "btn-modern btn-outline-info btn-sm", icon = icon("file")),
                         actionButton(ns(paste0("progress_tracking_", conn$partner_id)), "Track Progress",
                                      class = "btn-modern btn-outline-warning btn-sm", icon = icon("chart-bar"))
                     ),
                     actionButton(ns(paste0("remove_connection_", conn$partner_id)), "Remove Connection",
                                  class = "btn-modern btn-modern-danger btn-sm", icon = icon("user-times"))
              )
            )
        )
      })
      
      # Return header and cards
      div(class = "connections-list", do.call(tagList, c(list(header_card), connection_cards)))
    })
    
    # Quick action buttons - FIXED
    observeEvent(input$quick_schedule_main, {
      button_key <- "quick_schedule_main"
      current_time <- Sys.time()
      
      if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
        last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
        time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
        if (time_diff < 1) {
          return()
        }
      }
      
      rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
      
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
      # Trigger schedule session modal after a brief delay
      shinyjs::delay(500, {
        if (!is.null(rv$connections) && nrow(rv$connections) > 0 && can_show_modal("session")) {
          set_modal_state("session", TRUE)
          show_study_session_modal(rv$connections$partner_id[1])
        }
      })
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$quick_goal_main, {
      button_key <- "quick_goal_main"
      current_time <- Sys.time()
      
      if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
        last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
        time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
        if (time_diff < 1) {
          return()
        }
      }
      
      rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
      
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
      shinyjs::delay(500, {
        if (can_show_modal("goal")) {
          set_modal_state("goal", TRUE)
          show_shared_goal_modal()
        }
      })
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$go_to_collaboration, {
      button_key <- "go_to_collaboration"
      current_time <- Sys.time()
      
      if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
        last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
        time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
        if (time_diff < 1) {
          return()
        }
      }
      
      rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
      
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Collaboration Hub")
    })
    
    # Enhanced empty state for connections
    output$no_connections_message <- renderUI({
      div(class = "empty-state",
          div(class = "empty-state-icon", icon("user-friends")),
          h5("No connections yet"),
          p("Start by finding and connecting with potential partners in the 'Find Partners' tab."),
          actionButton(ns("find_partners_now"), "Find Partners Now", 
                       class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary mt-3"),
          br(),
          div(class = "mt-3",
              p("Once you have connections, you'll be able to:"),
              tags$ul(
                tags$li("Schedule study sessions"),
                tags$li("Set shared learning goals"), 
                tags$li("Share study resources"),
                tags$li("Track progress together")
              )
          )
      )
    })
    
    # MESSAGING SYSTEM
    
    # Message connections list - FIXED: Use proper connection object
    output$message_connections_list <- renderUI({
      req(rv$connections)
      
      if (nrow(rv$connections) == 0) {
        return(div(class = "empty-state",
                   div(class = "empty-state-icon", icon("user-friends")),
                   h5("No connections yet"),
                   p("Connect with partners to start messaging")))
      }
      
      # Get unread counts for each connection
      connection_items <- lapply(seq_len(nrow(rv$connections)), function(i) {
        conn_partner <- rv$connections[i, ]
        
        # Get connection ID using FIXED function
        connection_info <- get_connection_by_users_fixed(conn, user_id(), conn_partner$partner_id)
        if (nrow(connection_info) == 0) return(NULL)
        
        connection_id <- connection_info$id[1]
        
        # Get unread count for this connection
        unread_count <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "
          SELECT COUNT(*) as unread_count
          FROM study_partner_messages 
          WHERE connection_id = ? AND sender_id != ? AND is_read = 0
        ", params = list(connection_id, user_id()))$unread_count
        
        connection_class <- "list-group-item list-group-item-action"
        if (unread_count > 0) {
          connection_class <- paste(connection_class, "connection-with-unread")
        }
        
        if (!is.null(rv$selected_connection) && rv$selected_connection$partner_id == conn_partner$partner_id) {
          connection_class <- paste(connection_class, "active")
        }
        
        tags$button(
          class = connection_class,
          onclick = sprintf("Shiny.setInputValue('%s', %d)", ns("select_connection"), conn_partner$partner_id),
          style = "text-align: left; border: none; width: 100%; padding: 12px 15px;",
          div(
            h6(conn_partner$name, class = "mb-1"),
            p(class = "mb-1 text-muted small", 
              "Subjects: ", tags$span(class = "text-primary", conn_partner$subjects)),
            if (unread_count > 0) {
              span(class = "badge bg-danger", unread_count)
            }
          )
        )
      })
      
      tagList(connection_items)
    })
    
    # Select connection for messaging - UPDATED WITH FIXED FUNCTION
    observeEvent(input$select_connection, {
      req(input$select_connection, rv$connections)
      
      partner_id <- input$select_connection
      selected_conn <- rv$connections[rv$connections$partner_id == partner_id, ]
      
      if (nrow(selected_conn) > 0) {
        # Get the actual connection record using FIXED function
        connection_info <- get_connection_by_users_fixed(conn, user_id(), partner_id)
        if (nrow(connection_info) > 0) {
          rv$selected_connection <- list(
            connection_id = connection_info$id[1],
            partner_id = partner_id,
            partner_name = selected_conn$name[1],
            partner_subjects = selected_conn$subjects[1]
          )
          
          # Load messages for this connection
          rv$messages <- get_messages(conn, connection_info$id[1])
          
          # Mark messages as read
          mark_messages_as_read(conn, connection_info$id[1], user_id())
          rv$unread_count <- get_unread_message_count(conn, user_id())
        }
      }
    })
    
    # Chat interface
    output$chat_interface <- renderUI({
      if (is.null(rv$selected_connection)) {
        return(div(class = "empty-state",
                   div(class = "empty-state-icon", icon("comments")),
                   h5("Select a connection to start chatting"),
                   p("Choose a study partner from the list to begin your discussion")))
      }
      
      tagList(
        div(class = "chat-container",

                tags$small(class = "ms-2", 
                           "Subjects: ", rv$selected_connection$partner_subjects)
            ),
            
            div(class = "chat-messages", id = ns("chat_messages"),
                uiOutput(ns("chat_messages_content"))
            ),
            
            div(class = "chat-input-container",
                fluidRow(
                  column(10,
                         textAreaInput(ns("new_message"), NULL,
                                       placeholder = "Type your message here... Discuss your shared subjects and study plans!",
                                       rows = 2)
                  ),
                  column(2,
                         actionButton(ns("send_message"), "Send",
                                      class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary",
                                      style = "height: 100%;")
                  )
                )
            )
        )
      )
    })
    
    # Render chat messages content
    output$chat_messages_content <- renderUI({
      req(!is.null(user_id()))
      
      req(rv$messages, rv$selected_connection)
      
      if (nrow(rv$messages) == 0) {
        return(
          div(class = "empty-state",
              style = "height: 100%; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;",
              div(
                div(icon("comments", class = "empty-state-icon"),
                    h5("No messages yet"),
                    p("Start the conversation about your shared subjects!")
                )
              )
          )
        )
      }
      
      # Auto-scroll to bottom
      shinyjs::runjs(sprintf('
        var container = document.getElementById("%s");
        if (container) {
          container.scrollTop = container.scrollHeight;
        }
      ', ns("chat_messages")))
      
      # Create message bubbles
      message_list <- lapply(seq_len(nrow(rv$messages)), function(i) {
        msg <- rv$messages[i, ]
        current_uid <- suppressWarnings(as.integer(user_id() %||% NA))
        is_own <- isTRUE(as.integer(msg$sender_id) == current_uid)
        
        div(class = ifelse(is_own, "message own", "message other"),
            div(class = "message-bubble",
                if (!is_own) div(class = "message-sender", msg$sender_name),
                div(class = "message-text", msg$message_text),
                div(class = "message-time", 
                    format(as.POSIXct(msg$sent_at), "%H:%M"))
            )
        )
      })
      
      tagList(message_list)
    })
    
    # Send message
    observeEvent(input$send_message, {
      req(rv$selected_connection, input$new_message, nzchar(input$new_message))
      
      result <- send_message(conn, rv$selected_connection$connection_id, user_id(), input$new_message)
      
      if (result$success) {
        # Clear input
        updateTextAreaInput(session, "new_message", value = "")
        
        # Reload messages
        rv$messages <- get_messages(conn, rv$selected_connection$connection_id)
      } else {
        showNotification(paste("❌", result$message), type = "error")
      }
    })
    
    # Auto-refresh messages every 5 seconds when chat is open
    observe({
      if (!is.null(rv$selected_connection) && input$partner_tabs == "Messages") {
        invalidateLater(5000)
        rv$messages <- get_messages(conn, rv$selected_connection$connection_id)
        rv$unread_count <- get_unread_message_count(conn, user_id())
      }
    })
    
    # COLLABORATION FEATURES
    
    # FIXED: Shared Goals UI with proper NULL/empty data handling AND DELETE BUTTONS
    output$shared_goals_list <- renderUI({
      # Safely check if data exists and has rows
      if (is.null(rv$shared_goals) || !is.data.frame(rv$shared_goals) || nrow(rv$shared_goals) == 0) {
        return(div(class = "empty-state",
                   div(class = "empty-state-icon", icon("bullseye")),
                   h5("No shared goals yet"),
                   p("Create shared study goals with your partners")))
      }
      
      # Safely iterate through goals
      tryCatch({
        lapply(seq_len(nrow(rv$shared_goals)), function(i) {
          goal <- rv$shared_goals[i, ]
          
          # Safely extract goal properties with defaults
          goal_id <- goal$id %||% 0
          goal_title <- goal$title %||% "Untitled Goal"
          goal_description <- goal$description %||% "No description"
          goal_progress <- as.numeric(goal$progress %||% 0)
          partner_name <- goal$partner_name %||% "Unknown Partner"
          
          # Safely format deadline
          deadline_display <- "No deadline"
          if (!is.null(goal$deadline) && !is.na(goal$deadline) && nzchar(goal$deadline)) {
            tryCatch({
              if (is.numeric(goal$deadline)) {
                deadline_display <- as.character(as.Date(goal$deadline, origin = "1899-12-30"))
              } else {
                deadline_display <- as.character(as.Date(goal$deadline))
              }
            }, error = function(e) {
              deadline_display <- "Invalid date"
            })
          }
          
          # FIXED: Check if current user is the creator of this goal - use user_id instead of created_by
          is_creator <- identical(as.integer(goal$user_id), as.integer(user_id()))
          
          # Debug output
          cat("DEBUG Goal ID:", goal_id, "User ID (creator):", goal$user_id, "Current User ID:", user_id(), "Is owner:", is_creator, "\n")
          
          div(class = "partner-card",
              # DELETE BUTTON ADDED - only show if user is creator
              if (is_creator) {
                div(class = "delete-btn",
                    title = "Delete this goal",
                    onclick = sprintf("Shiny.setInputValue('%s', %d)", 
                                      ns("delete_goal"), goal_id),
                    icon("times"))
              },
              
              h6(goal_title),
              p(goal_description, class = "text-muted small"),
              div(class = "progress-bar-container",
                  div(class = "progress-bar-fill", 
                      style = sprintf("width: %d%%", min(max(goal_progress, 0), 100)))),
              div(class = "d-flex justify-content-between mt-2",
                  tags$small(class = "text-muted", 
                             icon("users"), " With: ", partner_name),
                  tags$small(class = "text-muted", 
                             icon("calendar"), " Due: ", deadline_display))
          )
        })
      }, error = function(e) {
        div(class = "alert alert-warning",
            icon("exclamation-triangle"),
            " Error displaying shared goals: ", e$message)
      })
    })
    
    # FIXED: Handle goal deletion
    observeEvent(input$delete_goal, {
      req(input$delete_goal, user_id())
      
      goal_id <- input$delete_goal
      
      # Safely find the goal
      if (!is.null(rv$shared_goals) && is.data.frame(rv$shared_goals)) {
        goal <- rv$shared_goals[rv$shared_goals$id == goal_id, ]
        if (nrow(goal) > 0) {
          goal_name <- goal$title[1] %||% "Unknown Goal"
          show_delete_confirmation_modal("goal", goal_id, goal_name)
        }
      }
    })
    
    # FIXED: Shared Resources UI with proper NULL/empty data handling AND DELETE BUTTONS
    output$shared_resources_list <- renderUI({
      # Safely check if data exists and has rows
      if (is.null(rv$shared_resources) || !is.data.frame(rv$shared_resources) || nrow(rv$shared_resources) == 0) {
        return(div(class = "empty-state",
                   div(class = "empty-state-icon", icon("file")),
                   h5("No shared resources"),
                   p("Share study materials with your partners")))
      }
      
      # Safely iterate through resources
      tryCatch({
        lapply(seq_len(nrow(rv$shared_resources)), function(i) {
          resource <- rv$shared_resources[i, ]
          
          # Safely extract resource properties with defaults
          resource_id <- resource$id %||% 0
          resource_title <- resource$title %||% "Untitled Resource"
          resource_description <- resource$description %||% "No description"
          resource_file_name <- resource$file_name %||% ""
          resource_file_size <- resource$file_size %||% 0
          shared_by <- resource$shared_by %||% "Unknown User"
          
          # Determine if resource has a file
          has_file <- !is.null(resource_file_name) && nzchar(resource_file_name)
          
          # FIXED: Check if current user is the sharer of this resource - use user_id instead of shared_by_id
          is_sharer <- identical(as.integer(resource$user_id), as.integer(user_id()))
          
          # Debug output
          cat("DEBUG Resource ID:", resource_id, "User ID (sharer):", resource$user_id, "Current User ID:", user_id(), "Is owner:", is_sharer, "\n")
          
          div(class = "partner-card",
              # DELETE BUTTON ADDED - only show if user is sharer
              if (is_sharer) {
                div(class = "delete-btn",
                    title = "Delete this resource",
                    onclick = sprintf("Shiny.setInputValue('%s', %d)", 
                                      ns("delete_resource"), resource_id),
                    icon("times"))
              },
              
              h6(resource_title),
              p(resource_description, class = "text-muted small"),
              
              # File info if available
              if (has_file) {
                div(class = "file-info mb-2",
                    icon("paperclip", class = "text-primary"),
                    tags$small(class = "text-muted", 
                               resource_file_name,
                               " (", format_file_size(resource_file_size), ")")
                )
              },
              
              div(class = "d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mt-2",
                  tags$small(class = "text-muted", 
                             icon("user"), " Shared by: ", shared_by),
                  
                  # Download button for files, view button for text resources
                  if (has_file) {
                    downloadButton(ns(paste0("download_resource_", resource_id)), 
                                   "Download", 
                                   class = "btn-sm btn-outline-primary")
                  } else {
                    actionButton(ns(paste0("view_resource_", resource_id)), 
                                 "View", 
                                 class = "btn-sm btn-outline-secondary")
                  }
              )
          )
        })
      }, error = function(e) {
        div(class = "alert alert-warning",
            icon("exclamation-triangle"),
            " Error displaying shared resources: ", e$message)
      })
    })
    
    # FIXED: Handle resource deletion
    observeEvent(input$delete_resource, {
      req(input$delete_resource, user_id())
      
      resource_id <- input$delete_resource
      
      # Safely find the resource
      if (!is.null(rv$shared_resources) && is.data.frame(rv$shared_resources)) {
        resource <- rv$shared_resources[rv$shared_resources$id == resource_id, ]
        if (nrow(resource) > 0) {
          resource_name <- resource$title[1] %||% "Unknown Resource"
          show_delete_confirmation_modal("resource", resource_id, resource_name)
        }
      }
    })
    
    # FIXED: Format file size helper function
    format_file_size <- function(bytes) {
      if (is.null(bytes) || is.na(bytes) || !is.numeric(bytes)) return("Unknown size")
      
      units <- c("B", "KB", "MB", "GB")
      size <- as.numeric(bytes)
      unit_index <- 1
      
      while (size >= 1024 && unit_index < length(units)) {
        size <- size / 1024
        unit_index <- unit_index + 1
      }
      
      paste0(round(size, 1), " ", units[unit_index])
    }
    
    # FIXED: Handle resource downloads with proper error handling
    observe({
      req(rv$shared_resources)
      
      if (!is.data.frame(rv$shared_resources) || nrow(rv$shared_resources) == 0) return()
      
      for (resource_id in rv$shared_resources$id) {
        local({
          local_resource_id <- resource_id
          
          output[[paste0("download_resource_", local_resource_id)]] <- downloadHandler(
            filename = function() {
              if (!is.null(rv$shared_resources) && is.data.frame(rv$shared_resources)) {
                resource <- rv$shared_resources[rv$shared_resources$id == local_resource_id, ]
                if (nrow(resource) > 0) {
                  return(resource$file_name %||% "download")
                }
              }
              return("download")
            },
            content = function(file) {
              tryCatch({
                if (!is.null(rv$shared_resources) && is.data.frame(rv$shared_resources)) {
                  resource <- rv$shared_resources[rv$shared_resources$id == local_resource_id, ]
                  if (nrow(resource) > 0 && !is.null(resource$file_path) && file.exists(resource$file_path)) {
                    file.copy(resource$file_path, file)
                  } else {
                    # Fallback: create a simple text file
                    writeLines(
                      c(
                        paste("Title:", resource$title %||% ""),
                        paste("Description:", resource$description %||% ""),
                        paste("Type:", resource$resource_type %||% ""),
                        paste("Shared by:", resource$shared_by %||% ""),
                        paste("Date:", resource$created_at %||% ""),
                        "",
                        "File not available for download."
                      ), 
                      file
                    )
                  }
                }
              }, error = function(e) {
                writeLines(paste("Error downloading file:", e$message), file)
              })
            }
          )
        })
      }
    })
    
    # FIXED: Study Sessions UI with proper NULL/empty data handling AND PROPER REFRESHING
    output$upcoming_sessions <- renderUI({
      # Use the reactive value instead of direct database call
      sessions <- rv$study_sessions
      
      # Safely check if data exists and has rows
      if (is.null(sessions) || !is.data.frame(sessions) || nrow(sessions) == 0) {
        return(div(class = "empty-state",
                   div(class = "empty-state-icon", icon("calendar")),
                   h5("No upcoming sessions"),
                   p("Schedule study sessions with your partners")))
      }
      
      # Safely iterate through sessions
      tryCatch({
        lapply(seq_len(nrow(sessions)), function(i) {
          session <- sessions[i, ]
          
          # Safely extract session properties with defaults
          session_id <- session$id %||% 0
          session_title <- session$title %||% "Untitled Session"
          session_description <- session$description %||% "No description"
          partner_name <- session$partner_name %||% "Unknown Partner"
          
          # Safely handle session time
          session_time <- "Time not set"
          if (!is.null(session$scheduled_datetime) && !is.na(session$scheduled_datetime) && nzchar(session$scheduled_datetime)) {
            session_time <- session$scheduled_datetime
          } else if (!is.null(session$scheduled_for) && !is.na(session$scheduled_for) && nzchar(session$scheduled_for)) {
            session_time <- session$scheduled_for
          }
          
          # FIXED: Check if current user is the creator of this session - use created_by column
          is_creator <- identical(as.integer(session$created_by), as.integer(user_id()))
          
          # Debug output
          cat("DEBUG Session ID:", session_id, "Created by:", session$created_by, "Current User ID:", user_id(), "Is owner:", is_creator, "\n")
          
          div(class = "partner-card",
              # Delete button (only show if user is creator)
              if (is_creator) {
                div(class = "delete-btn",
                    title = "Delete this session",
                    onclick = sprintf("Shiny.setInputValue('%s', %d)", 
                                      ns("delete_session"), session_id),
                    icon("times"))
              },
              
              h6(session_title),
              p(session_description, class = "text-muted small"),
              div(class = "d-flex justify-content-between mt-2",
                  tags$small(class = "text-muted", 
                             icon("clock"), " ", 
                             tryCatch({
                               format(as.POSIXct(session_time), "%b %d, %H:%M")
                             }, error = function(e) {
                               "Invalid date"
                             })),
                  tags$small(class = "text-muted", 
                             icon("users"), " ", partner_name))
          )
        })
      }, error = function(e) {
        div(class = "alert alert-warning",
            icon("exclamation-triangle"),
            " Error displaying study sessions: ", e$message)
      })
    })

        div(class = "alert alert-warning",
            icon("exclamation-triangle"),
            " Error displaying active collaborations: ", e$message)
      })
    })
    
    # FIXED: Add handlers for Resume and Details buttons in Active Collaborations
    observe({
      req(rv$active_collaborations)
      
      if (!is.data.frame(rv$active_collaborations) || nrow(rv$active_collaborations) == 0) return()
      
      for (i in seq_len(nrow(rv$active_collaborations))) {
        local({
          local_partner_id <- rv$active_collaborations$partner_id[i] %||% 0
          local_partner_name <- rv$active_collaborations$partner_name[i] %||% "Unknown Partner"
          
          # Resume button handler
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("resume_collab_", local_partner_id)]], {
            button_key <- paste0("resume_collab_", local_partner_id)
            current_time <- Sys.time()
            
            if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
              last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
              time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
              if (time_diff < 1) {
                return()
              }
            }
            
            rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
            
            showNotification(paste("Resuming collaboration with", local_partner_name), type = "message")
            # Navigate to messages with this partner
            updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Messages")
            # Trigger connection selection
            shinyjs::runjs(sprintf("Shiny.setInputValue('%s', %d)", ns("select_connection"), local_partner_id))
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
          
          # Details button handler - FIXED: Changed button ID to avoid conflict
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("view_collab_details_", local_partner_id)]], {
            button_key <- paste0("view_collab_details_", local_partner_id)
            current_time <- Sys.time()
            
            if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
              last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
              time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
              if (time_diff < 1) {
                return()
              }
            }
            
            rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
            
            showModal(modalDialog(
              title = paste("Collaboration Details -", local_partner_name),
              size = "l",
              easyClose = TRUE,
              footer = modalButton("Close"),
              div(
                h5("Collaboration Overview"),
                p("Subjects: ", tags$strong(rv$active_collaborations$subjects[i] %||% "Not specified")),
                p("Current Focus: ", tags$strong(rv$active_collaborations$current_focus[i] %||% "Not specified")),
                p("Last Activity: ", tags$strong(rv$active_collaborations$last_activity[i] %||% "No activity")),
                hr(),
                h5("Quick Actions"),
                div(class = "action-buttons",
                    actionButton(ns(paste0("message_from_modal_", local_partner_id)), "Send Message",
                                 class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary", icon = icon("envelope")),
                    actionButton(ns(paste0("session_from_modal_", local_partner_id)), "Schedule Session",
                                 class = "btn-modern btn-modern-success", icon = icon("calendar")),
                    actionButton(ns(paste0("goal_from_modal_", local_partner_id)), "Set Shared Goal",
                                 class = "btn-modern btn-modern-warning", icon = icon("bullseye"))
                )
              )
            ))
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
          
          # Modal button handlers
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("message_from_modal_", local_partner_id)]], {
            removeModal()
            updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Messages")
            shinyjs::runjs(sprintf("Shiny.setInputValue('%s', %d)", ns("select_connection"), local_partner_id))
          })
          
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("session_from_modal_", local_partner_id)]], {
            removeModal()

              set_modal_state("session", TRUE)

          })
          
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("goal_from_modal_", local_partner_id)]], {
            removeModal()
            if (can_show_modal("goal")) {
              set_modal_state("goal", TRUE)
              show_shared_goal_modal()
            }
          })
        })
      }
    })
    
    # Handle collaboration actions from connections list - FIXED
    
    # Handle "Remove Connection" button clicks for each connection
    observe({
      req(rv$connections)
      if (!is.data.frame(rv$connections) || nrow(rv$connections) == 0) return()
      for (pid in rv$connections$partner_id) {
        local({
          local_pid <- pid
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("remove_connection_", local_pid)]], {
            button_key <- paste0("remove_connection_", local_pid)
            current_time <- Sys.time()
            if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
              last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
              time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
              if (time_diff < 1) return()
            }
            rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
            
            showModal(modalDialog(
              title = "Remove Connection",
              easyClose = TRUE, footer = NULL,
              size = "m",
              div(
                p("Are you sure you want to remove this connection? You can always reconnect later."),
                div(class = "action-buttons mt-3",
                    actionButton(ns(paste0("cancel_remove_", local_pid)), "Cancel",
                                 class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary"),
                    actionButton(ns(paste0("confirm_remove_", local_pid)), "Remove Connection",
                                 class = "btn-modern btn-modern-danger", icon = icon("user-times"))
                )
              )
            ))
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
          
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("cancel_remove_", local_pid)]], {
            removeModal()
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
          
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("confirm_remove_", local_pid)]], {
            removeModal()
            res <- remove_connection_fixed(conn, user_id(), local_pid)
            if (isTRUE(res$success)) {
              showNotification("✅ Connection removed. You can reconnect anytime.", type = "message")
              # Refresh lists so the user shows up again as a potential partner
              refresh_connections()
              rv$potential_partners <- find_potential_partners(conn, user_id(), limit = 50)
              # If currently chatting with this partner, clear the chat selection
              if (!is.null(rv$selected_connection) && rv$selected_connection$partner_id == local_pid) {
                rv$selected_connection <- NULL
                rv$messages <- NULL
              }
              # Navigate user to "Find Partners" so they see the update
              updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Find Partners")
            } else {
              showNotification(paste("❌", res$message %||% "Failed to remove connection"), type = "error")
            }
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
        })
      }
    })
    
    observe({
      req(rv$connections)
      
      if (!is.data.frame(rv$connections) || nrow(rv$connections) == 0) return()
      
      for (conn_id in rv$connections$partner_id) {
        local({

    # Study Session Modal - FIXED VERSION with proper time picker and modal state tracking
    show_study_session_modal <- function(partner_id) {
      partner <- rv$connections[rv$connections$partner_id == partner_id, ]
      rv$selected_partner_for_session <- partner_id
      
      showModal(modalDialog(
        title = div(icon("video"), " Schedule Study Session"),
        easyClose = TRUE,
        footer = NULL,
        size = "l",
        div(
          h5(paste("Schedule with:", partner$name)),
          p("Plan a study session to work on your shared subjects"),
          
          fluidRow(
            column(6,
                   textInput(ns("session_title"), "Session Title", 
                             placeholder = "e.g., Microeconomics Chapter 3 Review"),
                   textAreaInput(ns("session_description"), "Description",
                                 placeholder = "What will you focus on in this session?",
                                 rows = 3),
                   selectizeInput(ns("session_subject"), "Primary Subject",
                                  choices = strsplit(partner$subjects, ",")[[1]])
            ),
            column(6,
                   dateInput(ns("session_date"), "Date", 
                             value = Sys.Date() + 1,
                             min = Sys.Date(),
                             format = "yyyy-mm-dd"),
                   # FIXED: Replace text input with proper time input
                   div(class = "form-group",
                       tags$label(`for` = ns("session_time"), "Time"),
                       tags$input(id = ns("session_time"), type = "time", 
                                  value = "19:00", class = "form-control")
                   ),
                   numericInput(ns("session_duration"), "Duration (minutes)", 
                                value = 60, min = 30, max = 240, step = 30),
                   textInput(ns("session_platform"), "Platform",
                             placeholder = "Zoom, Google Meet, Discord, etc.")
            )
          ),
          
          div(class = "action-buttons mt-4",
              actionButton(ns("cancel_session"), "Cancel", 
                           class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary"),
              actionButton(ns("confirm_session"), "Schedule Session", 
                           class = "btn-modern btn-modern-success", icon = icon("calendar-check"))
          )
        )
      ))
    }
    
    # Handle session scheduling - COMPLETELY FIXED VERSION with proper refresh
    observeEvent(input$confirm_session, {
      req(user_id(), input$session_title, rv$selected_partner_for_session)
      
      # Validate inputs
      if (is.null(input$session_date)) {
        showNotification("❌ Please select a date for the session", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      # Get time from the time input (this will be in HH:MM format)
      session_time <- if (!is.null(input$session_time) && nzchar(input$session_time)) {
        input$session_time
      } else {
        "19:00" # Default time
      }
      
      # Combine date and time into a single datetime string
      scheduled_datetime <- paste(input$session_date, session_time)
      
      # Validate the datetime
      if (is.na(as.POSIXct(scheduled_datetime, format = "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M"))) {
        showNotification("❌ Invalid date/time combination", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      # Use the FIXED function with proper parameters
      result <- schedule_study_session_fixed(
        conn,
        user_id(),
        rv$selected_partner_for_session,
        input$session_title,
        input$session_description %||% "",
        input$session_subject %||% "General",
        as.character(input$session_date),  # Ensure it's character
        session_time,                      # Already in HH:MM format
        input$session_duration %||% 60,
        input$session_platform %||% "Zoom"
      )
      
      if (result$success) {
        showNotification("✅ Study session scheduled successfully!", type = "message")
        removeModal()
        # Reset modal state
        set_modal_state("session", FALSE)
        # Refresh sessions list using FIXED function
        rv$study_sessions <- get_study_sessions_fixed(conn, user_id())
      } else {
        showNotification(paste("❌", result$message), type = "error")
      }
    })
    
    # Cancel session modal - FIXED: Reset modal state
    observeEvent(input$cancel_session, {
      removeModal()
      set_modal_state("session", FALSE)
      rv$selected_partner_for_session <- NULL
    })
    
    # Schedule session from collaboration hub - FIXED
    observeEvent(input$schedule_session, {
      button_key <- "schedule_session"
      current_time <- Sys.time()
      
      if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
        last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
        time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
        if (time_diff < 1) {
          return()
        }
      }
      
      rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
      
      if (is.null(rv$connections) || nrow(rv$connections) == 0) {
        showNotification("❌ You need to connect with partners first", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      # Show partner selection modal
      showModal(modalDialog(
        title = "Select Partner for Study Session",
        easyClose = TRUE,
        footer = NULL,
        size = "m",
        div(
          h5("Choose a partner to schedule with:"),
          selectizeInput(ns("session_partner_select"), "Study Partner",
                         choices = setNames(rv$connections$partner_id, rv$connections$name)),
          div(class = "action-buttons mt-4",
              actionButton(ns("cancel_partner_select"), "Cancel", 
                           class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary"),
              actionButton(ns("confirm_partner_select"), "Continue", 
                           class = "btn-modern btn-modern-primary")
          )
        )
      ))
    })

    # ENHANCED: Share Resource Modal with file upload
    show_share_resource_modal <- function() {
      if (is.null(rv$connections) || nrow(rv$connections) == 0) {
        showNotification("❌ You need to connect with partners first", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      showModal(modalDialog(
        title = "Share Study Resource",
        easyClose = TRUE,
        footer = NULL,
        size = "m",
        div(
          selectizeInput(ns("resource_partner"), "Share With Partner",
                         choices = setNames(rv$connections$partner_id, rv$connections$name)),
          textInput(ns("resource_title"), "Resource Title",
                    placeholder = "e.g., Constitutional Law Notes"),
          textAreaInput(ns("resource_description"), "Description",
                        placeholder = "Describe what this resource contains",
                        rows = 3),
          selectizeInput(ns("resource_type"), "Resource Type",
                         choices = c("Notes", "Book", "Article", "Video", "Practice Questions", "Other")),
          
          # NEW: File upload field
          div(class = "file-input-wrapper",
              tags$label(`for` = ns("resource_file"), "Upload File (Optional)", class = "font-weight-bold"),
              fileInput(ns("resource_file"), NULL, 
                        accept = c(".pdf", ".doc", ".docx", ".txt", ".rtf", ".jpg", ".png", ".mp4", ".mp3"),
                        buttonLabel = "Choose File",
                        placeholder = "No file selected"),
              tags$small("Supported formats: PDF, Word, Text, Images, Video, Audio"),
              tags$small("Maximum file size: 10MB")
          ),
          
          div(class = "action-buttons mt-4",
              actionButton(ns("cancel_resource"), "Cancel", 
                           class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary"),
              actionButton(ns("confirm_resource"), "Share Resource", 
                           class = "btn-modern btn-modern-success", icon = icon("upload"))
          )
        )
      ))
    }
    
    # ENHANCED: Handle resource sharing with file upload - FIXED VERSION
    observeEvent(input$confirm_resource, {
      req(user_id(), input$resource_partner, input$resource_title)
      
      # Get file info if uploaded
      file_info <- list(
        file_name = "",
        file_type = "",
        file_size = NA_integer_,
        file_path = ""
      )
      
      if (!is.null(input$resource_file)) {
        file <- input$resource_file
        file_info$file_name <- file$name
        file_info$file_type <- file$type
        file_info$file_size <- file$size
        
        # Create uploads directory if it doesn't exist
        upload_dir <- "shared_resources"
        if (!dir.exists(upload_dir)) {
          dir.create(upload_dir, recursive = TRUE)
        }
        
        # Generate unique filename
        file_ext <- tools::file_ext(file$name)
        unique_filename <- paste0("resource_", as.integer(Sys.time()), "_", user_id(), ".", file_ext)
        file_path <- file.path(upload_dir, unique_filename)
        
        # Copy file to upload directory
        file.copy(file$datapath, file_path)
        file_info$file_path <- file_path
      }
      
      # FIXED: Call share_resource without file_blob parameter
      result <- share_resource(
        conn,
        user_id(),
        input$resource_partner,
        input$resource_title,
        input$resource_description,
        input$resource_type,
        file_info$file_name,
        file_info$file_type,
        file_info$file_size,
        file_info$file_path
      )
      
      if (result$success) {
        showNotification("✅ Resource shared successfully!", type = "message")
        removeModal()
        # Reset modal state
        set_modal_state("resource", FALSE)
        # Refresh resources list
        rv$shared_resources <- get_shared_resources(conn, user_id())
      } else {
        showNotification(paste("❌", result$message), type = "error")
      }
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$cancel_resource, {
      removeModal()
      set_modal_state("resource", FALSE)
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$share_resource, {
      button_key <- "share_resource"
      current_time <- Sys.time()
      
      if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
        last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
        time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
        if (time_diff < 1) {
          return()
        }
      }
      
      rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
      
      if (can_show_modal("resource")) {
        set_modal_state("resource", TRUE)
        show_share_resource_modal()
      }
    })

    observeEvent(input$update_progress, {
      button_key <- "update_progress"
      current_time <- Sys.time()
      
      if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
        last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
        time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
        if (time_diff < 1) {
          return()
        }
      }
      
      rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
      
      if (can_show_modal("progress")) {
        set_modal_state("progress", TRUE)
        show_progress_tracking_modal()
      }
    })
    
    # Message connection from My Connections tab - FIXED
    observe({
      req(rv$connections)
      
      if (!is.data.frame(rv$connections) || nrow(rv$connections) == 0) return()
      
      for (conn_id in rv$connections$partner_id) {
        local({
          local_partner_id <- conn_id
          
          observeEvent(input[[paste0("message_conn_", local_partner_id)]], {
            button_key <- paste0("message_conn_", local_partner_id)
            current_time <- Sys.time()
            
            if (!is.null(rv$button_clicks[[button_key]])) {
              last_click <- rv$button_clicks[[button_key]]
              time_diff <- as.numeric(difftime(current_time, last_click, units = "secs"))
              if (time_diff < 1) {
                return()
              }
            }
            
            rv$button_clicks[[button_key]] <- current_time
            
            updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Messages")
            # Trigger connection selection
            shinyjs::runjs(sprintf("Shiny.setInputValue('%s', %d)", ns("select_connection"), local_partner_id))
          }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
        })
      }
    })
    
    # Navigation buttons
    observeEvent(input$setup_preferences_first, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Setup Preferences")
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$find_partners_now, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Find Partners")
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$view_my_profile, {
      updateTabsetPanel(session, "partner_tabs", selected = "Setup Preferences")
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$how_matching_works, {
      showModal(modalDialog(
        title = "How Partner Matching Works",
        easyClose = TRUE,
        footer = modalButton("Got It"),
        div(
          h5("🎯 Our Matching Algorithm"),
          p("We connect you with partners based on:"),
          tags$ul(
            tags$li(strong("Shared Optional Subjects"), " - Primary matching factor"),
            tags$li(strong("Learning Goals"), " - Exam prep, concepts, projects, etc."),
            tags$li(strong("Interaction Style"), " - One-on-one, groups, etc."),
            tags$li(strong("Proficiency Level"), " - Beginner, Intermediate, Advanced"),
            tags$li(strong("Availability"), " - Matching study schedules")
          ),
          br(),
          h5("💡 Tips for Better Matches"),
          tags$ul(
            tags$li("Complete all your preferences for accurate matching"),
            tags$li("Be specific about topics you want to focus on"),
            tags$li("Keep your availability updated"),
            tags$li("Send personalized connection requests")
          )
        )
      ))
    })
  })
}

mod_studyplan_server <- function(id, is_logged_in = NULL){
  moduleServer(id, function(input, output, session){
    ns <- session$ns
    if (is.null(is_logged_in)) is_logged_in <- reactive(FALSE)
    
    # Fixed %||% operator to handle vectors properly
    `%||%` <- function(a, b) {
      if (is.null(a)) return(b)
      if (length(a) == 0) return(b)
      if (is.character(a) && all(!nzchar(a))) return(b)
      a
    }
    
    # Comprehensive subject-wise topic database
    subject_topics <- list(
      # Compulsory Subjects
      "English Essay" = c(
        "Essay Structure & Types", "Argument Development", "Introduction & Conclusion Writing",
        "Vocabulary Enhancement", "Grammar & Punctuation", "Current Affairs for Essays",
        "Critical Thinking", "Essay Practice - Social Issues", "Essay Practice - Political Issues",
        "Essay Practice - Economic Issues", "Time Management in Essay", "Revision & Feedback"
      ),
      "English Precis & Composition" = c(
        "Precis Writing Fundamentals", "Comprehension Skills", "Grammar Rules Revision",
        "Vocabulary Building", "Sentence Structure", "Paragraph Writing",
        "Letter & Application Writing", "Report Writing", "Precis Practice - Editorials",
        "Error Correction", "Punctuation Rules", "Final Revision"
      ),
      "General Science & Ability" = c(
        "Basic Mathematics", "Algebra & Equations", "Geometry & Trigonometry",
        "Statistics & Probability", "Physics Fundamentals", "Chemistry Basics",
        "Biology - Human Body", "Biology - Cell Structure", "Environmental Science",
        "Computer Basics", "Logical Reasoning", "Quantitative Ability"
      ),
      "Pakistan Affairs" = c(
        "Historical Background", "Freedom Movement", "Constitutional Development",
        "Political History", "Foreign Policy", "Economic Development",
        "Social Issues", "Cultural Heritage", "Geography & Resources",
        "Current Affairs - National", "Current Affairs - International", "National Security"
      ),
      "Islamic Studies" = c(
        "Basic Beliefs", "Prophet's Life", "Quranic Studies",
        "Hadith Sciences", "Islamic Jurisprudence", "Islamic History",
        "Contemporary Issues", "Islamic Civilization", "Comparative Religion",
        "Ethics & Morality", "Social System in Islam", "Political System in Islam"
      ),
      "Comparative Religion" = c(
        "Major World Religions", "Comparative Analysis", "Interfaith Dialogue",
        "Religious Philosophy", "Scriptural Studies", "Historical Development",
        "Contemporary Issues", "Religion & Society", "Mysticism & Spirituality",
        "Ethical Systems", "Religious Practices", "Final Revision"
      ),
      
      # Popular Optional Subjects
      "International Relations" = c(
        "Theories of International Relations", "Foreign Policy Analysis", "Diplomacy & Statecraft",
        "International Organizations", "Global Security Issues", "International Political Economy",
        "Regional Studies", "Conflict Resolution", "International Law Basics",
        "Pakistan's Foreign Policy", "Current Global Issues", "Research Methods in IR"
      ),
      "Political Science" = c(
        "Political Theory", "Comparative Politics", "Political Institutions",
        "Political Ideologies", "Public Administration", "Political Economy",
        "Political Development", "Governance Systems", "Political Parties & Elections",
        "Political Sociology", "Research Methodology", "Contemporary Political Issues"
      ),
      "History of USA" = c(
        "Colonial America", "American Revolution", "Constitutional Development",
        "Civil War & Reconstruction", "Industrialization", "Progressive Era",
        "World Wars & USA", "Cold War Era", "Civil Rights Movement",
        "Modern US History", "US Foreign Policy", "Social & Cultural History"
      ),
      "International Law" = c(
        "Sources of International Law", "Law of Treaties", "State Responsibility",
        "International Human Rights Law", "Law of the Sea", "International Criminal Law",
        "Diplomatic & Consular Law", "Use of Force", "International Organizations Law",
        "International Environmental Law", "Settlement of Disputes", "Contemporary Challenges"
      ),
      "Public Administration" = c(
        "Theories of Public Administration", "Organizational Behavior", "Public Policy Analysis",
        "Financial Administration", "Personnel Administration", "Development Administration",
        "Local Government", "Administrative Law", "Public Sector Reforms",
        "Governance & Accountability", "Comparative Public Administration", "Current Issues"
      ),
      "Constitutional Law" = c(
        "Basic Concepts", "Fundamental Rights", "Principles of Policy",
        "Federal Structure", "Parliamentary System", "Judicial System",
        "Constitutional Amendments", "Emergency Provisions", "Local Government",
        "Comparative Constitutional Law", "Judicial Review", "Contemporary Constitutional Issues"
      ),
      "Sociology" = c(
        "Sociological Theories", "Social Structure", "Social Institutions",
        "Social Change", "Social Stratification", "Culture & Personality",
        "Social Research Methods", "Urban Sociology", "Rural Sociology",
        "Gender Studies", "Development Sociology", "Contemporary Social Issues"
      ),
      "Economics" = c(
        "Microeconomic Theory", "Macroeconomic Theory", "Public Finance",
        "Money & Banking", "International Economics", "Development Economics",
        "Agricultural Economics", "Labor Economics", "Econometrics",
        "Economic Planning", "Islamic Economics", "Current Economic Issues"
      ),
      "Geography" = c(
        "Physical Geography", "Human Geography", "Regional Geography",
        "Economic Geography", "Political Geography", "Environmental Geography",
        "Geographic Information Systems", "Remote Sensing", "Urban Geography",
        "Climate Change", "Natural Resources", "Geopolitics"
      ),
      "Journalism & Mass Communication" = c(
        "Communication Theories", "News Writing & Reporting", "Media Laws & Ethics",
        "Broadcast Journalism", "Digital Media", "Public Relations",
        "Advertising", "Media Management", "Research in Communication",
        "International Communication", "Development Communication", "Media Criticism"
      )
    )
    
    # Generic topics for any other subjects
    generic_topics <- c(
      "Fundamental Concepts", "Theoretical Framework", "Historical Development",
      "Key Principles", "Major Theories", "Practical Applications",
      "Current Trends", "Research Methodologies", "Critical Analysis",
      "Case Studies", "Comparative Studies", "Contemporary Issues",
      "Problem Solving", "Advanced Concepts", "Revision & Synthesis"
    )
    
    # Task templates for dynamic task generation - FIXED to handle placeholders properly
    task_templates <- list(
      beginner = c(
        "Watch documentary on %s",
        "Read basic concepts of %s", 
        "Solve 5 MCQs on %s",
        "Make notes on %s",
        "Watch tutorial videos on %s",
        "Practice basic problems on %s"
      ),
      intermediate = c(
        "Solve past paper Qs on %s",
        "Revise %s + attempt 10 MCQs",
        "Write short note on %s",
        "Practice essay on %s",
        "Solve questions on %s",
        "Create mind maps for %s"
      ),
      advanced = c(
        "Solve complex problems on %s",
        "Write analytical essay on %s",
        "Attempt previous 5 yrs Qs on %s",
        "Teach %s concepts to peer",
        "Solve time-bound tests on %s",
        "Critical analysis of %s"
      )
    )
    
    # Helper function to get topics for any subject
    get_subject_topics <- function(subject) {
      if (subject %in% names(subject_topics)) {
        return(subject_topics[[subject]])
      } else {
        # For unknown subjects, return generic topics with subject name
        return(paste(generic_topics, "in", subject))
      }
    }
    
    # Enhanced study plan generator with dynamic features
    make_dynamic_study_plan <- function(start_date, exam_date, subjects, weak_subject = NULL, 
                                        proficiency = "Intermediate") {
      total_days <- as.numeric(exam_date - start_date) + 1  # Include both start and end dates
      
      if (total_days <= 0) {
        stop("Exam date must be after start date")
      }
      
      # Generate plan
      plan <- data.frame()
      current_date <- start_date
      day_number <- 1
      
      # Calculate total topics across all selected subjects
      all_topics <- list()
      for (subj in subjects) {
        topics <- get_subject_topics(subj)
        all_topics[[subj]] <- topics
      }
      
      # Create a balanced distribution of subjects across days
      total_topics_count <- sum(sapply(all_topics, length))
      
      # Create subject rotation - randomly assign subjects to days but ensure all are covered
      subject_rotation <- c()
      remaining_days <- total_days
      
      while (remaining_days > 0) {
        # Shuffle subjects for each cycle to ensure random distribution
        shuffled_subjects <- sample(subjects)
        cycle_length <- min(length(shuffled_subjects), remaining_days)
        subject_rotation <- c(subject_rotation, shuffled_subjects[1:cycle_length])
        remaining_days <- remaining_days - cycle_length
      }
      
      # Track topic progress for each subject
      subject_progress <- setNames(rep(1, length(subjects)), subjects)
      subject_total <- sapply(subjects, function(s) length(all_topics[[s]]))
      
      # Generate daily plan from today until exam date
      for (day_idx in 1:min(total_days, length(subject_rotation))) {
        current_subject <- subject_rotation[day_idx]
        
        # Check if we have topics left for this subject
        if (subject_progress[current_subject] <= subject_total[current_subject]) {
          # Determine number of topics for this day (1-3 topics)
          remaining_topics <- subject_total[current_subject] - subject_progress[current_subject] + 1
          day_topic_count <- sample(1:min(3, remaining_topics), 1)
          
          # Get topics for the day
          topic_indices <- subject_progress[current_subject]:(subject_progress[current_subject] + day_topic_count - 1)
          day_topics <- all_topics[[current_subject]][topic_indices]
          
          # Update progress
          subject_progress[current_subject] <- subject_progress[current_subject] + day_topic_count
          
          # Create entries for each topic
          for (topic in day_topics) {
            # Dynamic hours assignment (3-6 hours)
            topic_hours <- sample(3:6, 1)
            
            # Dynamic task generation based on proficiency - FIXED to handle placeholders
            task_level <- tolower(proficiency)
            available_tasks <- task_templates[[task_level]] %||% task_templates$intermediate
            
            # Select tasks and properly format them with topics
            selected_tasks <- sample(available_tasks, sample(2:3, 1))
            formatted_tasks <- sapply(selected_tasks, function(task_template) {
              # Safely format the task with the topic
              tryCatch({
                sprintf(task_template, topic)
              }, error = function(e) {
                # If formatting fails, use the template as is
                task_template
              })
            })
            
            all_tasks <- paste(formatted_tasks, collapse = " | ")
            
            # Create plan entry
            plan_entry <- data.frame(
              Date = current_date,
              Day = paste("Day", day_number),
              Subject = current_subject,
              Topic = topic,
              Hours = topic_hours,
              Tasks = all_tasks,
              stringsAsFactors = FALSE
            )
            
            plan <- rbind(plan, plan_entry)
          }
        } else {
          # If no more topics for this subject, create a revision day
          topic_hours <- sample(3:6, 1)
          revision_tasks <- c(
            "Comprehensive revision of all topics",
            "Solve past papers on complete syllabus",
            "Create summary notes for quick revision",
            "Practice time-bound mock tests"
          )
          selected_tasks <- sample(revision_tasks, 2)
          
          plan_entry <- data.frame(
            Date = current_date,
            Day = paste("Day", day_number),
            Subject = current_subject,
            Topic = "Comprehensive Revision",
            Hours = topic_hours,
            Tasks = paste(selected_tasks, collapse = " | "),
            stringsAsFactors = FALSE
          )
          
          plan <- rbind(plan, plan_entry)
        }
        
        current_date <- current_date + 1
        day_number <- day_number + 1
      }
      
      return(plan)
    }
    
    # Per-session public temp path to serve PDF/HTML wrapper
    tmp_alias <- paste0("spdf_", session$token)
    tmp_dir   <- file.path(tempdir(), tmp_alias)
    dir.create(tmp_dir, recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)
    shiny::addResourcePath(tmp_alias, tmp_dir)
    session$onSessionEnded(function(){
      try(shiny::removeResourcePath(tmp_alias), silent = TRUE)
      try(unlink(tmp_dir, recursive = TRUE, force = TRUE), silent = TRUE)
    })
    
    # --- Enhanced plan generator ---
    plan_data <- eventReactive(input$make_plan, {
      req(input$exam_date, input$subjects)
      weak <- if (isTruthy(input$weak_subject) && input$weak_subject != "None") input$weak_subject else NULL
      
      withProgress({
        setProgress(0.3, message = "Generating dynamic study plan...")
        plan <- make_dynamic_study_plan(
          start_date = Sys.Date(),
          exam_date = as.Date(input$exam_date),
          subjects = input$subjects,
          weak_subject = weak,
          proficiency = input$proficiency
        )
        setProgress(1.0, message = "Finalizing plan...")
        plan
      })
    })
    
    # --- Statistics Calculations ---
    study_stats <- reactive({
      df <- plan_data()
      if (is.null(df) || nrow(df) == 0) {
        return(list(days = 0, hours = 0, topics = 0))
      }
      
      total_days <- length(unique(df$Date))
      total_hours <- sum(df$Hours, na.rm = TRUE)
      total_topics <- length(unique(df$Topic))
      
      list(
        days = total_days,
        hours = total_hours,
        topics = total_topics
      )
    })
    
    # --- Statistics Outputs ---
    output$stat_days <- renderUI({
      stats <- study_stats()
      div(class = "stats-card",
          div(class = "stats-value", stats$days),
          div(class = "stats-label", "Study Days")
      )
    })
    
    output$stat_hours <- renderUI({
      stats <- study_stats()
      div(class = "stats-card",
          div(class = "stats-value", stats$hours),
          div(class = "stats-label", "Total Hours")
      )
    })
    
    output$stat_topics <- renderUI({
      stats <- study_stats()
      div(class = "stats-card",
          div(class = "stats-value", stats$topics),
          div(class = "stats-label", "Topics Covered")
      )
    })
    
    # --- Enhanced table view with task formatting ---
    output$plan_tbl <- DT::renderDT({
      df <- req(plan_data())
      
      # Format tasks with badges
      df_display <- df
      df_display$Tasks <- sapply(df$Tasks, function(task_str) {
        tasks <- strsplit(task_str, "\\|")[[1]]
        badges <- sapply(trimws(tasks), function(task) {
          paste0('<span class="task-badge">', task, '</span>')
        })
        paste(badges, collapse = " ")
      })
      
      DT::datatable(
        df_display,
        extensions = c("Responsive", "Buttons"),
        options = list(
          responsive = TRUE, 
          autoWidth = TRUE, 
          pageLength = 10, 
          deferRender = TRUE,
          scrollX = TRUE, 
          dom = 'Bfrtip',
          buttons = c('copy', 'csv', 'excel', 'pdf'),
          columnDefs = list(
            list(targets = "_all", className = "dt-body-left"),
            list(targets = 4, width = "80px"),  # Hours column
            list(targets = 5, width = "300px")  # Tasks column
          )
        ),
        rownames = FALSE,
        class = "compact stripe hover",
        escape = FALSE  # Allow HTML in Tasks column
      )
    }, server = TRUE)
    
    # --- gated download area (CSV + PDF) ---
    output$download_area <- renderUI({
      if (!isTRUE(is_logged_in())) {
        return(actionButton(ns("open_login"), "Sign in / Sign up to download",
                            class = "btn-modern btn-outline-primary-modern mt-2"))
      }
      tagList(
        div(class = "download-area",
            downloadButton(ns("download_plan"), "Download CSV", 
                           class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary-modern"),
            actionButton(ns("download_pdf"), "Download PDF", 
                         class = "btn-modern btn-outline-secondary-modern")
        )
      )
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$open_login, {
      if (exists("mod_auth_ui")) {
        showModal(modalDialog(size = "l", easyClose = TRUE, footer = NULL, mod_auth_ui("auth_modal")))
      } else {
        showNotification("Please sign in from the top-right menu.", type = "message")
      }
    })
    
    # --- CSV download ---
    output$download_plan <- downloadHandler(
      filename = function() paste0("css_buddy_study_plan_", Sys.Date(), ".csv"),
      content = function(file){
        if (!isTRUE(is_logged_in())) stop("Please sign in to download.")
        df <- req(plan_data())
        readr::write_csv(df, file)
      }
    )
    
    # --- PDF helpers ---
    .clean_names <- function(x){
      x <- gsub("[^A-Za-z0-9]+", "_", x)
      tolower(gsub("^_|_$","", x))
    }
    .nice_col_labels <- function(nms){
      out <- gsub("_"," ", nms)
      out <- tools::toTitleCase(out)
      out
    }
    
    # --- PDF generator (grid) - UPDATED COLUMN WIDTHS ---
    make_plan_pdf <- function(df, file, title = "Study Plan", subtitle = NULL,
                              wm_head = "CSS BUDDY", wm_sub = "cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com"){
      grDevices::pdf(file, width = 8.27, height = 11.69, paper = "a4")
      on.exit(grDevices::dev.off(), add = TRUE)
      
      orig_names <- names(df)
      cn <- .clean_names(orig_names)
      
      # UPDATED COLUMN WEIGHTS: Increase Tasks, decrease Hours, Topic, and Day
      wts <- rep(1, length(cn)); names(wts) <- cn
      
      # Set specific weights for each column
      if ("date" %in% cn) wts["date"] <- 0.9
      if ("day" %in% cn) wts["day"] <- 0.6    # DECREASED from 0.9
      if ("subject" %in% cn) wts["subject"] <- 1.1
      if ("topic" %in% cn) wts["topic"] <- 1.2  # DECREASED from 2.0
      if ("hours" %in% cn) wts["hours"] <- 0.5  # DECREASED from 0.8
      if ("tasks" %in% cn) wts["tasks"] <- 3.0  # INCREASED from 2.0
      
      # For any other columns, use default weight of 1
      
      margin_lr <- 0.02
      usable_w  <- 1 - 2*margin_lr
      p <- wts / sum(wts)
      stops  <- c(margin_lr, margin_lr + cumsum(p * usable_w))
      xleft  <- head(stops, -1) + 0.006
      
      char_base <- 110
      wrap_chars <- pmax(8, floor(char_base * p))
      
      title_y <- 0.98; subtitle_y <- 0.955; header_y <- 0.915; bottom_margin <- 0.06
      line_step <- 0.040; row_pad <- 0.018; cex_hdr <- 0.86; cex_cell <- 0.78
      
      draw_watermark <- function(){
        grid::pushViewport(grid::viewport())
        for (yy in seq(0.15, 0.85, by = 0.2)) {
          for (xx in seq(0.12, 0.88, by = 0.26)) {
            grid::grid.text(wm_head, x = xx, y = yy,
                            gp = grid::gpar(col = grDevices::rgb(0,0,0,0.06), cex = 3.0, fontface = 2), rot = 45)
          }
        }
        grid::grid.text(wm_sub, x = 0.98, y = 0.04,
                        gp = grid::gpar(col = grDevices::rgb(0,0,0,0.28), cex = 0.9, fontface = 2), just = "right")
        grid::popViewport()
      }
      
      draw_header <- function(labels){
        grid::pushViewport(grid::viewport())
        grid::grid.text(title, x = 0.5, y = title_y, gp = grid::gpar(fontface = 2, cex = 1.25))
        if (!is.null(subtitle) && nzchar(subtitle)) {
          grid::grid.text(subtitle, x = 0.5, y = subtitle_y, gp = grid::gpar(cex = 0.95))
        }
        header_h <- line_step * 1.4
        grid::grid.rect(x = 0.5, y = header_y, width = 0.96, height = header_h,
                        gp = grid::gpar(fill = "#f3f4f6", col = "#e5e7eb"))
        for (i in seq_along(labels)){
          grid::grid.text(labels[i], x = xleft[i], y = header_y, just = "left", gp = grid::gpar(fontface=2, cex=cex_hdr))
        }
        grid::popViewport()
      }
      
      draw_par <- function(lines, x_left, y_mid, cex){
        if (!length(lines)) return()
        y_start <- y_mid + ((length(lines)-1) * line_step / 2)
        for (k in seq_along(lines)){
          grid::grid.text(lines[k], x = x_left, y = y_start - (k-1)*line_step,
                          just = c("left","centre"), gp = grid::gpar(cex = cex))
        }
      }
      
      draw_row <- function(i, y_top, row_vals, wrap_vec){
        wrapped <- mapply(function(text, w){
          strwrap(as.character(text %||% ""), width = w)
        }, row_vals, wrap_vec, SIMPLIFY = FALSE)
        
        nlines <- max(vapply(wrapped, length, integer(1)))
        h <- (nlines * line_step) + row_pad
        y_c <- y_top - h/2
        
        grid::grid.rect(x = 0.5, y = y_c, width = 0.96, height = h,
                        gp = grid::gpar(fill = if (i %% 2) "#ffffff" else "#fafafa", col = "#e5e7eb"))
        for (xv in stops) {
          grid::grid.lines(x = grid::unit(c(xv, xv), "npc"),
                           y = grid::unit(c(y_top - h, y_top), "npc"),
                           gp = grid::gpar(col = "#e5e7eb"))
        }
        for (j in seq_along(wrapped)){
          draw_par(wrapped[[j]], xleft[j], y_c, cex_cell)
        }
        h
      }
      
      labels <- .nice_col_labels(cn)
      i <- 1; N <- nrow(df)
      while (i <= N) {
        grid::grid.newpage()
        draw_watermark(); draw_header(labels)
        grid::grid.text(paste0("Generated on ", format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M")),
                        x = 0.02, y = 0.02, just = "left", gp = grid::gpar(col = "#9ca3af", cex = 0.7))
        y <- header_y - (line_step * 1.4)/2 - 0.02
        while (i <= N) {
          row_vals <- as.list(df[i, , drop = TRUE]); names(row_vals) <- cn
          h <- draw_row(i, y_top = y, row_vals = row_vals, wrap_vec = wrap_chars)
          y <- y - h
          if ((y - (line_step + row_pad)) < bottom_margin) { i <- i + 1; break } else { i <- i + 1 }
        }
      }
      invisible(file)
    }
    
    # --- PDF: open in new tab (fixed iframe src) ---
    observeEvent(input$download_pdf, {
      if (!isTRUE(is_logged_in())) {
        showNotification("Please sign in to download.", type = "warning"); return()
      }
      
      shiny::withProgress(message = "Preparing PDF…", value = 0, {
        setProgress(0.1)
        df <- isolate(plan_data())
        if (is.null(df) || !nrow(df)) {
          setProgress(1); showNotification("Generate a plan first.", type = "error"); return()
        }
        
        stamp <- as.integer(Sys.time())
        pdf_name  <- sprintf("study_plan_%s.pdf", stamp)
        html_name <- sprintf("view_%s.html", stamp)
        pdf_path  <- file.path(tmp_dir, pdf_name)
        html_path <- file.path(tmp_dir, html_name)
        
        # Subtitle with stats
        stats <- study_stats()
        subtitle <- paste0(
          "Personalized Plan | ", stats$days, " Days | ", 
          stats$hours, " Hours | ", stats$topics, " Topics"
        )
        
        setProgress(0.4)
        make_plan_pdf(df, pdf_path, title = "My Study Plan", subtitle = subtitle)
        
        # Safety: ensure files exist
        if (!file.exists(pdf_path)) { showNotification("PDF not written.", type = "error"); return() }
        
        setProgress(0.8)
        # URL parts
        html_rel <- paste0(tmp_alias, "/", html_name)
        pdf_rel_for_iframe <- paste0("./", basename(pdf_name))
        
        # Wrapper HTML
        html <- sprintf(
          '<!doctype html>
<html lang="en"><head><meta charset="utf-8">
<title>%s</title>
<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1,maximum-scale=1">
<style>
  html,body{height:100%%;margin:0}
  *{box-sizing:border-box;font-family:system-ui,-apple-system,Segoe UI,Roboto,Inter,Arial}
  .header{display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;
    padding:12px 16px;border-bottom:1px solid #e5e7eb;background:#fafafa;position:sticky;top:0;z-index:10}
  .header .brand{font-weight:700;letter-spacing:.5px}
  .header .sub{color:#6b7280;font-weight:600;font-size:0.9rem}
  .viewer{height:calc(100vh - 56px);}
  @media (max-width:575.98px){ .viewer{height:calc(100vh - 54px);} }
  .viewer iframe{width:100%%;height:100%%;border:0}
</style></head>
<body>
  <div class="header">
    <div class="brand">CSS BUDDY</div>
    <div class="sub">cssbuddy.pk@gmail.com</div>
  </div>
  <div class="viewer"><iframe src="%s"></iframe></div>
</body></html>',
          "Dynamic Study Plan",
          pdf_rel_for_iframe
        )
        writeLines(html, html_path, useBytes = TRUE)
        if (!file.exists(html_path)) { showNotification("HTML wrapper not written.", type = "error"); return() }
        
        setProgress(0.98)
        # Build absolute origin
        proto <- session$clientData$url_protocol %||% "http:"
        host  <- session$clientData$url_hostname %||% "localhost"
        port  <- session$clientData$url_port
        path  <- session$clientData$url_pathname %||% "/"
        path  <- sub("/$", "", path)
        origin <- paste0(proto, "//", host, if (nzchar(port)) paste0(":", port) else "", path)
        
        open_url <- paste0(origin, "/", html_rel)
        showNotification(paste("Opening:", open_url), type = "message", duration = 5)
        shinyjs::runjs(sprintf("window.open('%s','_blank');", open_url))
        setProgress(1)
      })
    }, ignoreInit = TRUE)
    
    return(list(exam_date = reactive(input$exam_date)))
  })
}
=== R/mod_roadmap.R ===
# R/mod_roadmap.R — SaaS Roadmap (Phases, checklists, progress, pricing, tech stack)

mod_roadmap_ui <- function(id){
  ns <- NS(id)
  tagList(
    div(class="card-soft p-4 mb-3",
        h3(class="mb-1", icon("map"), " SaaS Roadmap for CSS/PMS Prep"),
        p(class="text-muted mb-0", "Plan out features across MVP → Growth → Scaling, with live checklists and export.")
    ),
    
    fluidRow(
      column(8,
             # Phase 1 — MVP
             div(class="card-soft p-3 mb-3",
                 h5(span(class="badge bg-primary me-2","Phase 1"), "MVP (Launch Fast)"),
                 p("Goal: Launch fast with essentials to attract early adopters."),
                 prettyCheckboxGroup(
                   ns("mvp_core"), "Core Features",
                   choices = c(
                     "Smart Study Planner (exam date → daily/weekly plan)" = "planner",
                     "Past Papers & Notes Hub (searchable + curated notes)" = "papers",
                     "MCQ Practice System (topic-wise quizzes, auto-scoring)" = "mcq",
                     "Current Affairs Digest (daily/weekly summaries)" = "digest"
                   ),
                   icon = icon("check"), status = "primary", outline = TRUE, inline = FALSE, animation = "pulse"
                 ),
                 br(),
                 fluidRow(
                   column(6,
                          p(strong("Monetization:")),
                          tags$ul(
                            tags$li("Freemium: limited quizzes & notes (Free)"),
                            tags$li("Paid: full access + planner + digests"),
                            tags$li("Pricing: PKR 500–1500/month")
                          )
                   ),
                   column(6,
                          progressBar(ns("mvp_prog"), value = 0, total = 100, display_pct = TRUE, status = "primary"),
                          div(class="small text-muted mt-1", "MVP completion")
                   )
                 )
             ),
             
             # Phase 2 — Growth
             div(class="card-soft p-3 mb-3",
                 h5(span(class="badge bg-success me-2","Phase 2"), "Growth Stage"),
                 p("Goal: Engagement & habit-building; users rely on the platform."),
                 prettyCheckboxGroup(
                   ns("growth_core"), "New Features",
                   choices = c(
                     "AI Writing Assistant (essay outline, grammar/style)" = "ai_write",
                     "Précis checker" = "precis",
                     "Mock Exams & Analytics (timed, strengths/weaknesses)" = "mocks",
