                 textInput(ns("essay_title"), "Title*", placeholder = "Enter essay topic title")
          )
        ),
        helpText("* Required fields")
      ))
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$save_essay_topic, {
      if (!nzchar(input$essay_category) || !nzchar(input$essay_title)) {
        showNotification("Category and Title are required fields!", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      tryCatch({
        dbExecute(conn, "
          INSERT INTO essay_topics (category, title, is_active, created_by, created_at)
          VALUES (?, ?, 1, 1, datetime('now'))
        ", params = list(
          input$essay_category,
          input$essay_title
        ))
        
        showNotification("Essay topic saved successfully!", type = "message")
        removeModal()
        
        # Refresh essays table
        state$essays_data <- get_real_essay_topics_data()
      }, error = function(e) {
        showNotification(paste("Error saving essay topic:", e$message), type = "error")
      })
    })
    
    # Notes upload modal
    observeEvent(input$upload_notes, {
      showModal(modalDialog(
        title = "Upload Notes",
        size = "m",
        footer = tagList(
          modalButton("Cancel"),
          actionButton(ns("confirm_upload_notes"), "Upload", class = "btn btn-success")
        ),
        fluidRow(
          column(6,
                 selectizeInput(ns("notes_subject"), "Subject*", 
                                choices = c("Current Affairs", "Pakistan Affairs", "Islamic Studies", "Essay", "English"),
                                options = list(create = TRUE))
          ),
          column(6,
                 fileInput(ns("notes_file"), "Choose PDF File*",
                           accept = c(".pdf"),
                           multiple = FALSE)
          )
        ),
        helpText("PDF files will be stored in /db/notes directory"),
        helpText("* Required fields")
      ))
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$confirm_upload_notes, {
      if (!nzchar(input$notes_subject) || is.null(input$notes_file)) {
        showNotification("Please fill all required fields!", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      tryCatch({
        # Create notes directory if it doesn't exist
        notes_dir <- file.path("db", "notes")
        if (!dir.exists(notes_dir)) {
          dir.create(notes_dir, recursive = TRUE)
        }
        
        # Save file
        file <- input$notes_file
        if (tools::file_ext(file$name) != "pdf") {
          showNotification("Please upload a PDF file!", type = "error")
          return()
        }
        
        # Create filename: Subject_OriginalFilename.pdf
        safe_subject <- gsub("[^a-zA-Z0-9]", "_", input$notes_subject)
        safe_filename <- paste0(safe_subject, "_", file$name)
        file_path <- file.path(notes_dir, safe_filename)
        
        file.copy(file$datapath, file_path)
        
        showNotification("Notes uploaded successfully!", type = "message")
        removeModal()
        
        # Refresh notes table
        state$notes_data <- get_real_notes_data()
      }, error = function(e) {
        showNotification(paste("Error uploading notes:", e$message), type = "error")
      })
    })
    
    # MCQs upload modal
    observeEvent(input$upload_mcqs, {
      showModal(modalDialog(
        title = "Upload MCQs",
        size = "l",
        footer = tagList(
          modalButton("Cancel"),
          actionButton(ns("confirm_upload_mcqs"), "Upload", class = "btn btn-warning")
        ),
        fluidRow(
          column(6,
                 selectizeInput(ns("mcq_subject"), "Subject*", 
                                choices = c("Current Affairs", "Pakistan Affairs", "Islamic Studies", "Essay", "English"),
                                options = list(create = TRUE))
          ),
          column(6,
                 fileInput(ns("mcq_file"), "Choose Excel File*",
                           accept = c(".xlsx", ".xls"),
                           multiple = FALSE)
          )
        ),
        helpText("Excel files will be stored in the data folder and processed into the database"),
        helpText("* Required fields")
      ))
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$confirm_upload_mcqs, {
      if (!nzchar(input$mcq_subject) || is.null(input$mcq_file)) {
        showNotification("Please fill all required fields!", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      tryCatch({
        # Create data directory if it doesn't exist
        data_dir <- "data"
        if (!dir.exists(data_dir)) {
          dir.create(data_dir, recursive = TRUE)
        }
        
        # Save the original Excel file to data folder
        file <- input$mcq_file
        safe_filename <- paste0("mcqs_", gsub("[^a-zA-Z0-9]", "_", input$mcq_subject), "_", format(Sys.time(), "%Y%m%d_%H%M%S"), ".", tools::file_ext(file$name))
        file_path <- file.path(data_dir, safe_filename)
        file.copy(file$datapath, file_path)
        
        showNotification(paste("MCQs file saved to data folder:", safe_filename), type = "message")
        removeModal()
        
        # Refresh MCQs files table
        state$mcq_files_data <- get_mcq_files_data()
      }, error = function(e) {
        showNotification(paste("Error uploading MCQs:", e$message), type = "error")
      })
    })
    
    # Past Papers upload modal with "Other" option
    observeEvent(input$upload_papers, {
      showModal(modalDialog(
        title = "Upload Past Papers",
        size = "m",
        footer = tagList(
          modalButton("Cancel"),
          actionButton(ns("confirm_upload_papers"), "Upload", class = "btn btn-info")
        ),
        fluidRow(
          column(6,
                 selectizeInput(ns("paper_subject"), "Subject*", 
                                choices = c("English", "Essay", "Current Affairs", "Pakistan Affairs", "Islamic Studies", "Other"),
                                options = list(create = TRUE))
          ),
          column(6,
                 fileInput(ns("paper_file"), "Choose PDF File*",
                           accept = c(".pdf"),
                           multiple = FALSE)
          )
        ),
        helpText("PDF files will be stored in: Past Papers/{Subject}/ directory"),
        helpText("* Required fields")
      ))
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$confirm_upload_papers, {
      if (!nzchar(input$paper_subject) || is.null(input$paper_file)) {
        showNotification("Please fill all required fields!", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      tryCatch({
        # Use "Other" folder if subject is "Other"
        subject_folder <- input$paper_subject
        if (subject_folder == "Other") {
          subject_folder <- "Other"
        }
        
        # Create subject directory in Past Papers
        subject_dir <- file.path("Past Papers", subject_folder)
        if (!dir.exists(subject_dir)) {
          dir.create(subject_dir, recursive = TRUE)
        }
        
        # Save PDF file
        file <- input$paper_file
        if (tools::file_ext(file$name) != "pdf") {
          showNotification("Please upload a PDF file!", type = "error")
          return()
        }
        
        # Create filename
        safe_filename <- file$name
        file_path <- file.path(subject_dir, safe_filename)
        
        file.copy(file$datapath, file_path)
        
        showNotification("Past paper uploaded successfully!", type = "message")
        removeModal()
        
        # Refresh papers table
        state$papers_data <- get_real_papers_data(state$selected_subject)
      }, error = function(e) {
        showNotification(paste("Error uploading past paper:", e$message), type = "error")
      })
    })
    
    # Create User modal - FIXED: Removed role field
    observeEvent(input$create_user, {
      showModal(modalDialog(
        title = "Create New User",
        size = "m",
        footer = tagList(
          modalButton("Cancel"),
          actionButton(ns("save_user"), "Create User", class = "btn btn-primary")
        ),
        fluidRow(
          column(6,
                 textInput(ns("user_name"), "Full Name*", placeholder = "Enter full name")
          ),
          column(6,
                 textInput(ns("user_email"), "Email*", placeholder = "Enter email address")
          )
        ),
        fluidRow(
          column(12,
                 passwordInput(ns("user_password"), "Password*", placeholder = "Enter password")
          )
        ),
        helpText("* Required fields")
      ))
    })
    
    observeEvent(input$save_user, {
      if (!nzchar(input$user_name) || !nzchar(input$user_email) || !nzchar(input$user_password)) {
        showNotification("Please fill all required fields!", type = "error")
        return()
      }
      
      tryCatch({
        # Check if email already exists
        existing_user <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id FROM users WHERE email = ?", 
                                    params = list(input$user_email))
        
        if (nrow(existing_user) > 0) {
          showNotification("User with this email already exists!", type = "error")
          return()
        }
        
        # Create user in database - FIXED: removed role field
        dbExecute(conn, "
          INSERT INTO users (name, email, password_hash, created_at)
          VALUES (?, ?, ?, datetime('now'))
        ", params = list(
          input$user_name,
          input$user_email,
          input$user_password  # In production, hash this password
        ))
        
        showNotification("User created successfully!", type = "message")
        removeModal()
        
        # Refresh users table
        state$users_data <- get_real_users_data()
      }, error = function(e) {
        showNotification(paste("Error creating user:", e$message), type = "error")
      })
    })
    
    # Refresh users
    observeEvent(input$refresh_users, {
      state$users_data <- get_real_users_data()
      showNotification("Users list refreshed!", type = "message")
    })
    
  })
}
=== R/utils_db.R ===
# R/utils_db.R — SQLite helpers (users + profiles + optionals) + Essay module (text/PDF) with self-healing migrations
suppressPackageStartupMessages({ library(DBI); library(jsonlite) })

`%||%` <- function(a, b) if (!is.null(a) && !is.na(a) && length(a) > 0 && !(is.character(a) && identical(a, ""))) a else b

# --- Normalization & hashing helpers ---
normalize_email <- function(x) tolower(trimws(x %||% ""))

has_bcrypt <- function() requireNamespace("bcrypt", quietly = TRUE)
has_sodium <- function() requireNamespace("sodium", quietly = TRUE)

is_bcrypt_hash <- function(h) is.character(h) && length(h) == 1 && nzchar(h) && grepl("^\\$2[abxy]?\\$", h)

hash_password <- function(password) {
  stopifnot(nzchar(password))
  if (has_bcrypt()) {
    bcrypt::hashpw(password)
  } else if (has_sodium()) {
    sodium::password_store(password)
  } else stop("Install either 'bcrypt' or 'sodium' for password hashing.")
}

verify_any_hash <- function(stored_hash, password) {
  ok <- FALSE
  if (!ok && has_bcrypt() && is_bcrypt_hash(stored_hash)) ok <- tryCatch(bcrypt::checkpw(password, stored_hash), error = function(e) FALSE)
  if (!ok && has_sodium())                              ok <- tryCatch(sodium::password_verify(stored_hash, password), error = function(e) FALSE)
  if (!ok && has_bcrypt())                              ok <- tryCatch(bcrypt::checkpw(password, stored_hash), error = function(e) FALSE)
  isTRUE(ok)
}

# ---- Migration helpers ----
.table_cols <- function(conn, table){
  tryCatch(dbGetQuery(conn, sprintf("PRAGMA table_info(%s)", DBI::dbQuoteIdentifier(conn, table))), error = function(e) data.frame())$name %||% character()
}
.ensure_col <- function(conn, table, name, sql_type){
  cols <- .table_cols(conn, table)
  if (!length(cols)) return(invisible(FALSE))
  if (!name %in% cols) dbExecute(conn, sprintf("ALTER TABLE %s ADD COLUMN %s %s", table, name, sql_type))
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# ===================== Core app tables =====================
create_tables <- function(conn){
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    name TEXT,
    email TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL,
    created_at TEXT NOT NULL
  )")
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS profiles (
    user_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
    exam_type TEXT DEFAULT 'CSS',
    exam_year INTEGER,
    prep_level TEXT,
    city TEXT,
    mobile TEXT,
    gender TEXT,
    updated_at TEXT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
  )")
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS optionals (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    name TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL
  )")
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS user_optionals (
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    subject_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (user_id, subject_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY(subject_id) REFERENCES optionals(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
  )")
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_user_optionals_user ON user_optionals(user_id)")
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_user_optionals_subject ON user_optionals(subject_id)")
}

# ---- Optionals seeding ----
seed_optionals <- function(conn, subjects){
  if (!length(subjects)) return(invisible(TRUE))
  existing <- tryCatch(dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT name FROM optionals")$name, error = function(e) character())
  to_add <- setdiff(unique(subjects), existing)
  if (!length(to_add)) return(invisible(TRUE))
  dbBegin(conn); on.exit(dbRollback(conn), add = TRUE)
  for (nm in to_add){
    dbExecute(conn, "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO optionals(name) VALUES (?)", params = list(nm))
  }
  dbCommit(conn); on.exit(NULL)
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# ---- Auth helpers ----
user_by_email <- function(conn, email){
  email <- normalize_email(email)
  dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT * FROM users WHERE lower(email) = lower(?) LIMIT 1", params = list(email))
}

create_user <- function(conn, name, email, password){
  email <- normalize_email(email)
  stopifnot(nzchar(email), nzchar(password))
  existing <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id FROM users WHERE lower(email)=lower(?)", params = list(email))
  if (nrow(existing) > 0) stop("Email already registered")
  hash <- hash_password(password)
  now  <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  dbBegin(conn); on.exit(dbRollback(conn), add = TRUE)
  res <- try(dbExecute(conn,
                       "INSERT INTO users(name,email,password_hash,created_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?)",
                       params = list(name %||% "", email, hash, now)), silent = TRUE)
  if (inherits(res, "try-error")) stop("Signup failed. Please try again.")
  id <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT last_insert_rowid() AS id")$id[1]
  dbCommit(conn); on.exit(NULL)
  list(id = id, name = name %||% "", email = email)
}

verify_user <- function(conn, email, password){
  row <- user_by_email(conn, email)
  if (!nrow(row)) return(NULL)
  stored <- row$password_hash[1]
  if (!verify_any_hash(stored, password)) return(NULL)
  list(id = row$id[1], name = row$name[1], email = row$email[1])
}

# ---- Profile helpers ----
get_profile <- function(conn, user_id){
  p <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT * FROM profiles WHERE user_id = ?", params = list(user_id))
  if (!nrow(p)) return(NULL)
  opts <- dbGetQuery(conn,
                     "SELECT o.name FROM user_optionals uo JOIN optionals o ON o.id = uo.subject_id WHERE uo.user_id = ? ORDER BY o.name",
                     params = list(user_id))$name
  p$optional_subjects <- list(opts %||% character())
  p[1,]
}

upsert_profile <- function(conn, user_id,
                           exam_type = "CSS", exam_year = NA_integer_,
                           prep_level = NA_character_,
                           city = NA_character_,
                           mobile = NA_character_,
                           gender = NA_character_){
  now <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  has <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT 1 FROM profiles WHERE user_id = ?", params = list(user_id))
  if (!nrow(has)){
    dbExecute(conn, "INSERT INTO profiles (user_id, exam_type, exam_year, prep_level, city, mobile, gender, updated_at)
                     VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
              params = list(user_id, exam_type, exam_year, prep_level, city, mobile, gender, now))
  } else {
    dbExecute(conn, "UPDATE profiles SET exam_type=?, exam_year=?, prep_level=?, city=?, mobile=?, gender=?, updated_at=? WHERE user_id = ?",
              params = list(exam_type, exam_year, prep_level, city, mobile, gender, now, user_id))
  }
  get_profile(conn, user_id)
}

subject_ids_for <- function(conn, subject_names){
  if (!length(subject_names)) return(integer())
  
  cat("DEBUG: subject_ids_for looking for:", paste(subject_names, collapse=", "), "\n")
  cat("DEBUG: Number of subject names:", length(subject_names), "\n")
  
  placeholders <- paste(rep("?", length(subject_names)), collapse = ",")
  query <- sprintf("SELECT id, name FROM optionals WHERE name IN (%s)", placeholders)
  
  cat("DEBUG: Query:", query, "\n")
  
  q <- dbGetQuery(conn, query, params = as.list(subject_names))
  
  cat("DEBUG: Database returned", nrow(q), "rows\n")
  if (nrow(q) > 0) {
    cat("DEBUG: Found subjects in DB:", paste(q$name, collapse=", "), "\n")
    cat("DEBUG: With IDs:", paste(q$id, collapse=", "), "\n")
  }
  
  # Match the order of input subject_names
  ids <- q$id[match(subject_names, q$name)]
  cat("DEBUG: Final subject IDs to return:", paste(ids, collapse=", "), "\n")
  
  ids
}

upsert_user_optionals <- function(conn, user_id, subject_names){
  # Enhanced debug output
  cat("DEBUG: upsert_user_optionals called with user_id:", user_id, "\n")
  cat("DEBUG: Raw subject_names type:", typeof(subject_names), "\n")
  cat("DEBUG: Raw subject_names length:", length(subject_names), "\n")
  cat("DEBUG: Raw subject_names:", paste(subject_names, collapse=", "), "\n")
  
  # Handle NULL or empty input
  if (is.null(subject_names) || length(subject_names) == 0) {
    cat("DEBUG: No subjects provided, clearing existing optionals\n")
    dbExecute(conn, "DELETE FROM user_optionals WHERE user_id = ?", params = list(user_id))
    return(invisible(TRUE))
  }
  
  # Ensure subject_names is a character vector
  subject_names <- as.character(subject_names)
  cat("DEBUG: Processed subject_names:", paste(subject_names, collapse=", "), "\n")
  cat("DEBUG: Number of subjects to process:", length(subject_names), "\n")
  
  # Clear existing optionals for this user
  dbExecute(conn, "DELETE FROM user_optionals WHERE user_id = ?", params = list(user_id))
  
  # Get subject IDs
  sids <- subject_ids_for(conn, unique(subject_names))
  cat("DEBUG: Found subject IDs:", paste(sids, collapse=", "), "\n")
  cat("DEBUG: Number of subject IDs found:", length(sids), "\n")
  
  if (!length(sids)) {
    cat("DEBUG: No valid subject IDs found\n")
    return(invisible(TRUE))
  }
  
  dbBegin(conn); on.exit(dbRollback(conn), add = TRUE)
  ok <- TRUE
  inserted_count <- 0
  
  for (sid in sids){
    res <- try(dbExecute(conn, "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO user_optionals(user_id, subject_id) VALUES (?,?)",
                         params = list(user_id, sid)), silent = TRUE)
    if (inherits(res, "try-error")) { 
      ok <- FALSE; 
      cat("DEBUG: Error inserting subject", sid, "for user", user_id, ":", res, "\n")
      break 
    } else {
      inserted_count <- inserted_count + 1
      cat("DEBUG: Successfully inserted subject ID:", sid, "\n")
    }
  }
  
  if (!ok) stop("Failed to save optional subjects.")
  dbCommit(conn); on.exit(NULL)
  cat("DEBUG: Successfully inserted", inserted_count, "subjects for user", user_id, "\n")
  invisible(TRUE)
}

get_user_optionals <- function(conn, user_id){
  dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT o.name FROM user_optionals uo JOIN optionals o ON o.id = uo.subject_id WHERE uo.user_id = ? ORDER BY o.name",
             params = list(user_id))$name
}

migrate_optionals_json <- function(conn){
  cols <- .table_cols(conn, "profiles")
  if (!"optional_subjects" %in% cols) return(invisible(TRUE))
  rows <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT user_id, optional_subjects FROM profiles WHERE optional_subjects IS NOT NULL AND TRIM(optional_subjects) <> ''")
  if (!nrow(rows)) return(invisible(TRUE))
  for (i in seq_len(nrow(rows))){
    uid <- rows$user_id[i]
    raw <- rows$optional_subjects[i]
    opts <- tryCatch(jsonlite::fromJSON(raw), error = function(e) character())
    if (length(opts)) upsert_user_optionals(conn, uid, opts)
  }
  dbExecute(conn, "UPDATE profiles SET optional_subjects = NULL WHERE optional_subjects IS NOT NULL")
  invisible(TRUE)
}

ensure_emails_lowercased <- function(conn){
  try({ dbExecute(conn, "UPDATE users SET email = lower(email) WHERE email <> lower(email)") }, silent = TRUE)
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# ===================== Essay schema & helpers =====================

ensure_essay_schema <- function(conn){
  try(DBI::dbExecute(conn, "PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON"), silent = TRUE)
  # Topics
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS essay_topics (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    category TEXT NOT NULL,
    title TEXT NOT NULL,
    is_active INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    created_by INTEGER,
    created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
  )")
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_topics_cat ON essay_topics(category)")
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_topics_active ON essay_topics(is_active)")
  # Essays
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS essays (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    topic_id INTEGER,
    mode TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'text', -- 'text' or 'pdf'
    content_html TEXT,
    content_text TEXT,
    word_count INTEGER,
    duration_seconds INTEGER,
    wpm REAL,
    started_at TEXT,
    submitted_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    pdf_name TEXT,
    pdf_type TEXT,
    pdf_size INTEGER,
    pdf_path TEXT,
    pdf_blob BLOB,
    is_marked INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    marked_at TEXT,
    marked_by INTEGER,
    marks REAL,
    feedback TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY(topic_id) REFERENCES essay_topics(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY(marked_by) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL
  )")
  # Add any missing columns (self-healing for older DBs)
  add <- function(nm, sql) .ensure_col(conn, "essays", nm, sql)
  add("mode", "TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'text'")
  add("pdf_name", "TEXT")
  add("pdf_type", "TEXT")
  add("pdf_size", "INTEGER")
  add("pdf_path", "TEXT")
  add("pdf_blob", "BLOB")
  add("is_marked", "INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0")
  add("marked_at", "TEXT")
  add("marked_by", "INTEGER")
  add("marks", "REAL")
  add("feedback", "TEXT")
  invisible(TRUE)
}

essay_seed_topics <- function(conn){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  already <- tryCatch(dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT COUNT(*) AS n FROM essay_topics"), error = function(e) data.frame(n=0))$n
  if (isTRUE(already > 0)) return(invisible(TRUE))
  seeds <- tibble::tribble(
    ~category,                 ~title,
    "Politics",                "Democracy and Digital Disinformation",
    "Economy",                 "Is Universal Basic Income a Viable Policy for Developing Countries?",
    "Social Issues",           "The Role of Education in Social Mobility",
    "International Relations", "Great-Power Competition in the Indo-Pacific",
    "Environment",             "Climate Change: Adaptation vs. Mitigation for Pakistan",
    "Governance",              "Civil Service Reforms: Balancing Merit and Inclusion",
    "Ethics",                  "AI Ethics: Innovation versus Regulation",
    "Security",                "Cybersecurity as a National Security Imperative"
  )
  dbBegin(conn); on.exit(dbRollback(conn), add = TRUE)
  ok <- TRUE
  for (i in seq_len(nrow(seeds))){
    res <- try(dbExecute(conn,
                         "INSERT INTO essay_topics(category,title,is_active) VALUES (?,?,1)",
                         params = list(seeds$category[i], seeds$title[i])), silent = TRUE)
    if (inherits(res, "try-error")) { ok <- FALSE; break }
  }
  if (!ok) stop("Failed to seed essay topics.")
  dbCommit(conn); on.exit(NULL)
  invisible(TRUE)
}

essay_get_categories <- function(conn){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  out <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT DISTINCT category FROM essay_topics WHERE is_active=1 ORDER BY category")$category
  unique(out[!is.na(out) & nzchar(out)])
}

essay_get_topics <- function(conn, category = NA_character_){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  if (is.na(category) || !nzchar(category)){
    dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, category, title FROM essay_topics WHERE is_active=1 ORDER BY category, title")
  } else {
    dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, category, title FROM essay_topics WHERE is_active=1 AND category=? ORDER BY title",
               params = list(category))
  }
}

essay_random_topic <- function(conn, category = NA_character_){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  if (is.na(category) || !nzchar(category)){
    dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, category, title FROM essay_topics WHERE is_active=1 ORDER BY RANDOM() LIMIT 1")
  } else {
    dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, category, title FROM essay_topics WHERE is_active=1 AND category=? ORDER BY RANDOM() LIMIT 1",
               params = list(category))
  }
}

essay_add_topic <- function(conn, title, category, created_by = NA_integer_){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  if (!nzchar(title) || !nzchar(category)) return(FALSE)
  dbExecute(conn, "INSERT INTO essay_topics(category,title,is_active,created_by) VALUES (?,?,1,?)",
            params = list(category, title, created_by %||% NA))
  TRUE
}

essay_toggle_active <- function(conn, topic_id){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  dbExecute(conn, "UPDATE essay_topics SET is_active = CASE WHEN is_active=1 THEN 0 ELSE 1 END WHERE id = ?",
            params = list(as.integer(topic_id)))
  TRUE
}

essay_list_topics <- function(conn){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, category, title, is_active, created_at FROM essay_topics ORDER BY category, title")
}

# ---- Insert: TEXT mode ----
essay_insert_text <- function(conn, user_id, topic_id = NA, content_html = "", content_text = "",
                              word_count = NA_integer_, duration_seconds = NA_integer_, wpm = NA_real_, started_at = NULL){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  now <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  st  <- started_at %||% now
  dbExecute(conn, "
    INSERT INTO essays(user_id, topic_id, mode, content_html, content_text, word_count, duration_seconds, wpm, started_at, submitted_at)
    VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
            params = list(as.integer(user_id), if (is.na(topic_id)) NA else as.integer(topic_id),
                          "text", content_html %||% "", content_text %||% "",
                          as.integer(word_count %||% 0), as.integer(duration_seconds %||% 0), as.numeric(wpm %||% NA),
                          st, now)
  )
  TRUE
}

# Back-compat alias
essay_insert <- function(conn, user_id, topic_id, content_html, content_text, word_count, duration_seconds, wpm){
  essay_insert_text(conn, user_id, topic_id, content_html, content_text, word_count, duration_seconds, wpm)
}

# ---- Insert: PDF mode (upload) ----
# store_mode: "path" (default) or "blob"
essay_insert_pdf <- function(conn, user_id, topic_id = NA, pdf_name, pdf_type = NA_character_, pdf_size = NA_integer_,
                             pdf_path = NA_character_, pdf_blob = NULL, store_mode = c("path","blob")){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  store_mode <- match.arg(store_mode)
  now <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  params <- list(
    as.integer(user_id),
    if (is.na(topic_id)) NA else as.integer(topic_id),
    "pdf",
    pdf_name %||% "",
    pdf_type %||% "",
    as.integer(pdf_size %||% NA),
    if (identical(store_mode, "path")) (pdf_path %||% "") else NA,
    if (identical(store_mode, "blob")) list(pdf_blob) else NULL,
    now, now
  )
  # Note: pass blob as list(raw) for RSQLite
  dbExecute(conn, "
    INSERT INTO essays(user_id, topic_id, mode, pdf_name, pdf_type, pdf_size, pdf_path, pdf_blob, started_at, submitted_at)
    VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)", params = params)
  TRUE
}

# Back-compat alias
essay_insert_upload <- function(conn, user_id, topic_id = NA, pdf_name, pdf_type = NA_character_, pdf_size = NA_integer_,
                                pdf_path = NA_character_, pdf_blob = NULL, store_mode = c("path","blob")){
  essay_insert_pdf(conn, user_id, topic_id, pdf_name, pdf_type, pdf_size, pdf_path, pdf_blob, store_mode)
}

# ---- Marking ----
essay_mark <- function(conn, essay_id, marked_by, is_marked = TRUE, marks = NULL, feedback = NULL){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  now <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  dbExecute(conn, "
    UPDATE essays
       SET is_marked = ?, marked_at = ?, marked_by = ?, marks = ?, feedback = ?
     WHERE id = ?",
            params = list(as.integer(is_marked), now, as.integer(marked_by %||% NA),
                          if (is.null(marks)) NA else as.numeric(marks),
                          feedback %||% NULL, as.integer(essay_id))
  )
  TRUE
}

# ---- Queries ----
essay_list_user <- function(conn, user_id){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  dbGetQuery(conn, "
    SELECT e.id, e.submitted_at, e.mode,
           e.word_count, e.duration_seconds, e.wpm,
           e.is_marked, e.marks,
           t.title, t.category,
           e.pdf_name, e.pdf_size, e.pdf_type, e.pdf_path
    FROM essays e
    LEFT JOIN essay_topics t ON t.id = e.topic_id
    WHERE e.user_id = ?
    ORDER BY datetime(e.submitted_at) DESC
  ", params = list(as.integer(user_id)))
}

essay_get_one <- function(conn, essay_id, user_id = NULL){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  if (!is.null(user_id)){
    df <- dbGetQuery(conn, "
      SELECT e.*, t.title AS topic_title, t.category AS topic_category
      FROM essays e
      LEFT JOIN essay_topics t ON t.id = e.topic_id
      WHERE e.id = ? AND e.user_id = ?
      LIMIT 1
    ", params = list(as.integer(essay_id), as.integer(user_id)))
  } else {
    df <- dbGetQuery(conn, "
      SELECT e.*, t.title AS topic_title, t.category AS topic_category
      FROM essays e
      LEFT JOIN essay_topics t ON t.id = e.topic_id
      WHERE e.id = ?
      LIMIT 1
    ", params = list(as.integer(essay_id)))
  }
  if (nrow(df)) df[1,] else NULL
}

essay_admin_list <- function(conn){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  dbGetQuery(conn, "
    SELECT e.id, e.user_id, u.email, u.name,
           e.mode, e.submitted_at, e.word_count, e.duration_seconds, e.wpm,
           e.is_marked, e.marks, e.marked_at, e.marked_by, e.feedback,
           t.title AS topic_title, t.category AS topic_category,
           e.pdf_name, e.pdf_size, e.pdf_type, e.pdf_path
    FROM essays e
    LEFT JOIN users u ON u.id = e.user_id
    LEFT JOIN essay_topics t ON t.id = e.topic_id
    ORDER BY datetime(e.submitted_at) DESC
  ")
}

essay_my_stats <- function(conn, user_id){
  ensure_essay_schema(conn)
  dbGetQuery(conn, "
    SELECT
      COUNT(*) AS n_submissions,
      SUM(CASE WHEN mode='text' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS n_text,
      SUM(CASE WHEN mode='pdf'  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS n_pdf,
      AVG(NULLIF(wpm,0)) AS avg_wpm,
      AVG(NULLIF(word_count,0)) AS avg_words,
      SUM(duration_seconds) AS total_seconds,
      SUM(CASE WHEN is_marked=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS n_marked
    FROM essays WHERE user_id = ?
  ", params = list(as.integer(user_id)))
}

# ===================== Environment exports (adds essays) =====================

refresh_user_env <- function(conn, env = .GlobalEnv){
  # Users
  u <- tryCatch(dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, name, email, created_at FROM users ORDER BY id"),
                error = function(e) data.frame())
  
  # Profiles
  p <- tryCatch(dbGetQuery(conn, "
        SELECT user_id, exam_type, exam_year, prep_level, city, mobile, gender, updated_at
        FROM profiles
      "), error = function(e) data.frame())
  if (nrow(p)){
    p$id <- p$user_id
    p <- p[, c("id","exam_type","exam_year","prep_level","city","mobile","gender","updated_at")]
  } else {
    p <- data.frame(id=integer(), exam_type=character(), exam_year=integer(),
                    prep_level=character(), city=character(), mobile=character(),
                    gender=character(), updated_at=character(), stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
  }
  
  # Optional subjects -> readable text
  opt_map <- tryCatch(dbGetQuery(conn, "
        SELECT uo.user_id, o.name
        FROM user_optionals uo JOIN optionals o ON o.id = uo.subject_id
        ORDER BY o.name
      "), error = function(e) data.frame())
  opt_text_map <- if (nrow(opt_map)) {
    tapply(opt_map$name, opt_map$user_id, function(v) paste(v, collapse = ", "), simplify = FALSE)
  } else list()
  p$optional_subjects_text <- vapply(p$id, function(i){ (opt_text_map[[as.character(i)]]) %||% "" }, "")
  
  users_data     <- u
  users_profiles <- merge(u, p, by = "id", all.x = TRUE, sort = FALSE)
  
  # One-hot pivot (optional)
  all_opts <- tryCatch(dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, name FROM optionals ORDER BY name"),
                       error = function(e) data.frame())
  pivot <- if (nrow(u) && nrow(all_opts) && nrow(opt_map)){
    mat <- matrix(0L, nrow = nrow(u), ncol = nrow(all_opts),
                  dimnames = list(as.character(u$id), all_opts$name))
    if (nrow(opt_map)){
      for (r in seq_len(nrow(opt_map))){
        uid <- as.character(opt_map$user_id[r]); nm <- opt_map$name[r]
        if (uid %in% rownames(mat) && nm %in% colnames(mat)) mat[uid, nm] <- 1L
      }
    }
    df <- data.frame(id = as.integer(rownames(mat)), mat, check.names = FALSE)
    merge(u[, c("id","email","name")], df, by = "id", sort = FALSE)
  } else data.frame()
  
  # Essay exports (safe; skip pdf_blob in summary views)
  essay_topics_data <- tryCatch(
    { ensure_essay_schema(conn); dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT id, category, title, is_active, created_by, created_at FROM essay_topics ORDER BY category, title") },
    error = function(e) data.frame()
  )
  essay_submissions_data <- tryCatch(
    { ensure_essay_schema(conn); dbGetQuery(conn, "
      SELECT e.id, e.user_id, u.email, u.name,
             e.mode, e.submitted_at, e.started_at,
             e.word_count, e.duration_seconds, e.wpm,
             e.is_marked, e.marks, e.marked_at, e.marked_by, e.feedback,
             e.topic_id, t.title AS topic_title, t.category AS topic_category,
             e.pdf_name, e.pdf_size, e.pdf_type, e.pdf_path
      FROM essays e
      LEFT JOIN users u ON u.id = e.user_id
      LEFT JOIN essay_topics t ON t.id = e.topic_id
      ORDER BY datetime(e.submitted_at) DESC
    ")},
    error = function(e) data.frame()
  )
  
  assign("users_data", users_data, envir = env)
  assign("users_profiles", users_profiles, envir = env)
  assign("users_optionals_pivot", pivot, envir = env)
  assign("essay_topics_data", essay_topics_data, envir = env)
  assign("essay_submissions_data", essay_submissions_data, envir = env)
  
  invisible(list(
    users_data = users_data,
    users_profiles = users_profiles,
    users_optionals_pivot = pivot,
    essay_topics_data = essay_topics_data,
    essay_submissions_data = essay_submissions_data
  ))
}

# ===================== Study Partner Schema & Helpers =====================

ensure_study_partner_schema <- function(conn) {
  # Study partner preferences table
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS study_partner_preferences (
    user_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
    learning_goals TEXT DEFAULT 'exam_prep',
    interaction_style TEXT DEFAULT 'one_on_one',
    availability TEXT,
    timezone TEXT,
    topics_of_interest TEXT,
    proficiency_level TEXT DEFAULT 'intermediate',
    created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
    updated_at TEXT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
  )")
  
  # Study partner connections table
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS study_partner_connections (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    partner_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending', -- pending, accepted, rejected, blocked
    icebreaker_message TEXT,
    created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
    responded_at TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY(partner_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    UNIQUE(user_id, partner_id)
  )")
  
  # Collaboration tables - FIXED: Added created_by column to study_sessions
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS study_sessions (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    partner_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    title TEXT NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    subject TEXT,
    scheduled_datetime TEXT NOT NULL,
    scheduled_for TEXT,
    duration_minutes INTEGER DEFAULT 60,
    platform TEXT,
    status TEXT DEFAULT 'scheduled',
    created_by INTEGER NOT NULL, -- FIXED: Added created_by column
    created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY(partner_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY(created_by) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
  )")
  
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS shared_goals (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    partner_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    title TEXT NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    deadline TEXT,
    subjects TEXT,
    progress INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY(partner_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
  )")
  
  # FIXED: Enhanced shared_resources table with file storage
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS shared_resources (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    partner_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    title TEXT NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    resource_type TEXT,
    file_name TEXT,
    file_type TEXT,
    file_size INTEGER,
    file_path TEXT,
    file_blob BLOB,
    created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY(partner_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
  )")
  
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS collaboration_progress (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    partner_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    subject TEXT NOT NULL,
    mastery_level INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    notes TEXT,
    updated_at TEXT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY(partner_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
  )")
  
  # Messaging table
  dbExecute(conn, "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS study_partner_messages (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    connection_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    sender_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    message_text TEXT NOT NULL,
    sent_at TEXT NOT NULL,
    is_read INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    FOREIGN KEY(connection_id) REFERENCES study_partner_connections(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY(sender_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
  )")
  
  # Ensure columns exist for backward compatibility
  ensure_study_partner_columns(conn)
  
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# Helper function to ensure all columns exist
ensure_study_partner_columns <- function(conn) {
  # Ensure study_sessions has all required columns including created_by
  .ensure_col(conn, "study_sessions", "user_id", "INTEGER NOT NULL")
  .ensure_col(conn, "study_sessions", "partner_id", "INTEGER NOT NULL")
  .ensure_col(conn, "study_sessions", "title", "TEXT NOT NULL")
  .ensure_col(conn, "study_sessions", "description", "TEXT")
  .ensure_col(conn, "study_sessions", "subject", "TEXT")
  .ensure_col(conn, "study_sessions", "scheduled_datetime", "TEXT NOT NULL")
  .ensure_col(conn, "study_sessions", "scheduled_for", "TEXT")
  .ensure_col(conn, "study_sessions", "duration_minutes", "INTEGER DEFAULT 60")
  .ensure_col(conn, "study_sessions", "platform", "TEXT")
  .ensure_col(conn, "study_sessions", "status", "TEXT DEFAULT 'scheduled'")
  .ensure_col(conn, "study_sessions", "created_by", "INTEGER NOT NULL") # FIXED: Added created_by
  .ensure_col(conn, "study_sessions", "created_at", "TEXT NOT NULL")
  
  # Enhanced shared_resources with file storage
  .ensure_col(conn, "shared_resources", "user_id", "INTEGER NOT NULL")
  .ensure_col(conn, "shared_resources", "partner_id", "INTEGER NOT NULL")
  .ensure_col(conn, "shared_resources", "title", "TEXT NOT NULL")
  .ensure_col(conn, "shared_resources", "description", "TEXT")
  .ensure_col(conn, "shared_resources", "resource_type", "TEXT")
  .ensure_col(conn, "shared_resources", "file_name", "TEXT")
  .ensure_col(conn, "shared_resources", "file_type", "TEXT")
  .ensure_col(conn, "shared_resources", "file_size", "INTEGER")
  .ensure_col(conn, "shared_resources", "file_path", "TEXT")
  .ensure_col(conn, "shared_resources", "file_blob", "BLOB")
  .ensure_col(conn, "shared_resources", "created_at", "TEXT NOT NULL")
}

# ---- Debug function to print study partner tables ----
print_study_partner_tables <- function(conn, user_id) {
  cat("\n🔍 === STUDY PARTNER DATABASE DEBUG ===\n")
  cat("User ID:", user_id, "\n")
  
  # 1. Check study_partner_preferences table
  cat("\n📋 1. STUDY_PARTNER_PREFERENCES:\n")
  prefs <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT * FROM study_partner_preferences WHERE user_id = ?", 
                      params = list(user_id))
  if (nrow(prefs) > 0) {
    print(prefs)
    # Parse JSON fields for readability
    if (!is.na(prefs$availability) && nzchar(prefs$availability)) {
      availability_parsed <- tryCatch(fromJSON(prefs$availability), error = function(e) "Parse Error")
      cat("   📅 Availability (parsed):", paste(availability_parsed, collapse = ", "), "\n")
    }
    if (!is.na(prefs$topics_of_interest) && nzchar(prefs$topics_of_interest)) {
      topics_parsed <- tryCatch(fromJSON(prefs$topics_of_interest), error = function(e) "Parse Error")
      cat("   📚 Topics (parsed):", paste(topics_parsed, collapse = ", "), "\n")
    }
  } else {
    cat("   ❌ No preferences found\n")
  }
  
  # 2. Check user's optional subjects
  cat("\n📖 2. USER'S OPTIONAL SUBJECTS:\n")
  user_subjects <- get_user_optionals(conn, user_id)
  if (length(user_subjects) > 0) {
    cat("   ✅", paste(user_subjects, collapse = ", "), "\n")
  } else {
    cat("   ❌ No optional subjects set\n")
  }
  
  # 3. Check potential partners
  cat("\n👥 3. POTENTIAL PARTNERS:\n")
  partners <- find_potential_partners(conn, user_id, limit = 5)
  if (nrow(partners) > 0) {
    cat("   ✅ Found", nrow(partners), "potential partners\n")
    for(i in 1:min(3, nrow(partners))) {
      cat("   ", i, ".", partners$name[i], "- Subjects:", partners$common_subjects[i], 
          "- Match:", round(partners$match_score[i] * 100), "%\n")
    }
  } else {
    cat("   ❌ No potential partners found\n")
  }
  
  # 4. Check connection requests
  cat("\n📩 4. CONNECTION REQUESTS:\n")
  incoming <- get_connection_requests(conn, user_id, "incoming")
  sent <- get_connection_requests(conn, user_id, "sent")
  cat("   📥 Incoming requests:", nrow(incoming), "\n")
  cat("   📤 Sent requests:", nrow(sent), "\n")
  
  # 5. Check accepted connections
  cat("\n🤝 5. ACCEPTED CONNECTIONS:\n")
  connections <- get_connections(conn, user_id)
  cat("   ✅ Total connections:", nrow(connections), "\n")
  
  cat("====================================\n\n")
}

# ---- Study Partner Preferences ----
get_study_preferences <- function(conn, user_id) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  prefs <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT * FROM study_partner_preferences WHERE user_id = ?", 
                      params = list(user_id))
  if (nrow(prefs) == 0) return(NULL)
  
  # Return basic preferences without complex parsing
  return(prefs[1, , drop = FALSE])
}

upsert_study_preferences <- function(conn, user_id, 
                                     learning_goals = "exam_prep",
                                     interaction_style = "one_on_one",
                                     availability = NULL,
                                     timezone = NULL,
                                     topics_of_interest = NULL,
                                     proficiency_level = "intermediate") {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  now <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  
  # Convert lists to JSON safely
  availability_json <- if (!is.null(availability) && length(availability) > 0) {
    toJSON(as.character(availability))
  } else {
    "[]"
  }
  
  topics_json <- if (!is.null(topics_of_interest) && length(topics_of_interest) > 0) {
    toJSON(as.character(topics_of_interest))
  } else {
    "[]"
  }
  
  # Handle NULL timezone
  timezone <- if (is.null(timezone) || !nzchar(timezone)) NA_character_ else timezone
  
  existing <- dbGetQuery(conn, "SELECT 1 FROM study_partner_preferences WHERE user_id = ?", 
                         params = list(user_id))
  
  if (nrow(existing) == 0) {
    dbExecute(conn, "
      INSERT INTO study_partner_preferences 
      (user_id, learning_goals, interaction_style, availability, timezone, topics_of_interest, proficiency_level, created_at, updated_at)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
    ", params = list(
      user_id, learning_goals, interaction_style, availability_json, timezone, 
      topics_json, proficiency_level, now, now
    ))
  } else {
    dbExecute(conn, "
      UPDATE study_partner_preferences 
      SET learning_goals = ?, interaction_style = ?, availability = ?, timezone = ?, topics_of_interest = ?, proficiency_level = ?, updated_at = ?
      WHERE user_id = ?
    ", params = list(
      learning_goals, interaction_style, availability_json, timezone, 
      topics_json, proficiency_level, now, user_id
    ))
  }
  
  # Print debug info
  cat("💾 STUDY PREFERENCES SAVED:\n")
  cat("   User:", user_id, "\n")
  cat("   Goals:", learning_goals, "\n")
  cat("   Style:", interaction_style, "\n")
  cat("   Level:", proficiency_level, "\n")
  cat("   Availability:", availability_json, "\n")
  cat("   Topics:", topics_json, "\n")
  
  get_study_preferences(conn, user_id)
}

# ---- Find Potential Partners ----
find_potential_partners <- function(conn, user_id, limit = 20) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  # Get user's optional subjects
  user_subjects <- get_user_optionals(conn, user_id)
  if (length(user_subjects) == 0) {
    cat("❌ No optional subjects found for user", user_id, "\n")
    return(data.frame())
  }
  
  cat("🔍 FINDING PARTNERS FOR USER:", user_id, "\n")
  cat("   User subjects:", paste(user_subjects, collapse = ", "), "\n")
  
  # Find users with matching optional subjects (excluding self)
  subject_placeholders <- paste(rep("?", length(user_subjects)), collapse = ",")
  
  query <- sprintf("
    SELECT DISTINCT u.id, u.name, u.email, p.exam_type, p.prep_level, p.city,
           GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT o.name) AS common_subjects,
           sp.learning_goals, sp.interaction_style, sp.proficiency_level,
           (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM study_partner_connections spc 
            WHERE ((spc.user_id = ? AND spc.partner_id = u.id) OR (spc.user_id = u.id AND spc.partner_id = ?))
            AND spc.status = 'accepted') AS is_connected,
           (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM study_partner_connections spc 
            WHERE spc.user_id = ? AND spc.partner_id = u.id AND spc.status = 'pending') AS has_pending_request,
           (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM study_partner_connections spc 
            WHERE spc.user_id = u.id AND spc.partner_id = ? AND spc.status = 'pending') AS has_incoming_request
    FROM users u
    JOIN user_optionals uo ON uo.user_id = u.id
    JOIN optionals o ON o.id = uo.subject_id
    LEFT JOIN profiles p ON p.user_id = u.id
    LEFT JOIN study_partner_preferences sp ON sp.user_id = u.id
    WHERE u.id != ? 
      AND o.name IN (%s)
    GROUP BY u.id
    ORDER BY 
      COUNT(DISTINCT o.name) DESC,
      sp.learning_goals = (SELECT learning_goals FROM study_partner_preferences WHERE user_id = ?) DESC,
      sp.proficiency_level = (SELECT proficiency_level FROM study_partner_preferences WHERE user_id = ?) DESC
    LIMIT ?
  ", subject_placeholders)
  
  params <- c(
    user_id, user_id,   # for is_connected (both directions)
    user_id,            # for outgoing pending requests
    user_id,            # for incoming pending requests
    user_id,            # exclude self
    as.list(user_subjects),
    user_id, user_id,   # for ordering
    limit
  )
  
  partners <- dbGetQuery(conn, query, params = params)
  
  if (nrow(partners) > 0) {
    partners$common_subjects_list <- strsplit(partners$common_subjects, ",")
    partners$match_score <- sapply(partners$common_subjects_list, length) / length(user_subjects)
    
    # Determine request direction for UI
    partners$request_direction <- "none"
    partners$request_direction[partners$has_pending_request == 1] <- "outgoing"
    partners$request_direction[partners$has_incoming_request == 1] <- "incoming"
    partners$request_direction[partners$has_pending_request == 1 & partners$has_incoming_request == 1] <- "mutual"
    
    cat("   ✅ Found", nrow(partners), "potential partners\n")
  } else {
    cat("   ❌ No partners found with matching subjects\n")
  }
  
  partners
}

# ---- Connection Management ----
send_connection_request <- function(conn, user_id, partner_id, icebreaker_message = "") {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  cat("📤 SENDING CONNECTION REQUEST:\n")
  cat("   From user:", user_id, "\n")
  cat("   To partner:", partner_id, "\n")
  cat("   Message:", icebreaker_message, "\n")
  
  # Check if connection already exists
  existing <- dbGetQuery(conn, 
                         "SELECT status FROM study_partner_connections WHERE user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?",
                         params = list(user_id, partner_id))
  
  if (nrow(existing) > 0) {
    cat("   ❌ Connection already exists with status:", existing$status[1], "\n")
    return(list(success = FALSE, message = "Connection request already exists"))
  }
  
  now <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  
  result <- tryCatch({
    dbExecute(conn, "
      INSERT INTO study_partner_connections (user_id, partner_id, icebreaker_message, created_at)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
    ", params = list(user_id, partner_id, icebreaker_message, now))
    cat("   ✅ Connection request sent successfully\n")
    list(success = TRUE, message = "Connection request sent successfully")
  }, error = function(e) {
    cat("   ❌ Failed to send connection request:", e$message, "\n")
    list(success = FALSE, message = paste("Failed to send connection request:", e$message))
  })
  
  result
}

get_connection_requests <- function(conn, user_id, type = "incoming") {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  if (type == "incoming") {
    query <- "
      SELECT spc.*, u.name, u.email, p.exam_type, p.prep_level,
             GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT o.name) AS subjects
      FROM study_partner_connections spc
      JOIN users u ON u.id = spc.user_id
      LEFT JOIN profiles p ON p.user_id = u.id
      LEFT JOIN user_optionals uo ON uo.user_id = u.id
      LEFT JOIN optionals o ON o.id = uo.subject_id
      WHERE spc.partner_id = ? AND spc.status = 'pending'
      GROUP BY spc.id
      ORDER BY spc.created_at DESC
    "
    params <- list(user_id)
  } else {
    query <- "
      SELECT spc.*, u.name, u.email, p.exam_type, p.prep_level,
             GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT o.name) AS subjects
      FROM study_partner_connections spc
      JOIN users u ON u.id = spc.partner_id
      LEFT JOIN profiles p ON p.user_id = u.id
      LEFT JOIN user_optionals uo ON uo.user_id = u.id
      LEFT JOIN optionals o ON o.id = uo.subject_id
      WHERE spc.user_id = ? AND spc.status = 'pending'
      GROUP BY spc.id
      ORDER BY spc.created_at DESC
    "
    params <- list(user_id)
  }
  
  dbGetQuery(conn, query, params = params)
}

update_connection_status <- function(conn, connection_id, user_id, status) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  cat("🔄 UPDATING CONNECTION STATUS:\n")
  cat("   Connection ID:", connection_id, "\n")
  cat("   User ID:", user_id, "\n")
  cat("   New Status:", status, "\n")
  
  now <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  
  result <- tryCatch({
    dbExecute(conn, "
      UPDATE study_partner_connections 
      SET status = ?, responded_at = ?
      WHERE id = ? AND partner_id = ?
    ", params = list(status, now, connection_id, user_id))
    cat("   ✅ Connection", status, "successfully\n")
    list(success = TRUE, message = paste("Connection", status))
  }, error = function(e) {
    cat("   ❌ Failed to update connection:", e$message, "\n")
    list(success = FALSE, message = paste("Failed to update connection:", e$message))
  })
  
  result
}

get_connections <- function(conn, user_id) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  query <- "
    SELECT 
      CASE 
        WHEN spc.user_id = ? THEN spc.partner_id
        ELSE spc.user_id
      END AS partner_id,
      u.name, u.email, p.exam_type, p.prep_level, p.city,
      GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT o.name) AS subjects,
      sp.learning_goals, sp.interaction_style, sp.proficiency_level
    FROM study_partner_connections spc
    JOIN users u ON u.id = CASE 
      WHEN spc.user_id = ? THEN spc.partner_id
      ELSE spc.user_id
    END
    LEFT JOIN profiles p ON p.user_id = u.id
    LEFT JOIN user_optionals uo ON uo.user_id = u.id
    LEFT JOIN optionals o ON o.id = uo.subject_id
    LEFT JOIN study_partner_preferences sp ON sp.user_id = u.id
    WHERE (spc.user_id = ? OR spc.partner_id = ?) AND spc.status = 'accepted'
    GROUP BY partner_id
    ORDER BY u.name
  "
  
  dbGetQuery(conn, query, params = list(user_id, user_id, user_id, user_id))
}

# ---- Collaboration Functions ----

# FIXED: Study Sessions with proper parameter handling including created_by
schedule_study_session_fixed <- function(conn, user_id, partner_id, title, description, subject, 
                                         scheduled_date, scheduled_time, duration, platform) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    # Validate required parameters
    if (is.null(scheduled_date) || is.null(scheduled_time)) {
      return(list(success = FALSE, message = "Date and time are required"))
    }
    
    # Combine date and time into a single datetime string
    scheduled_datetime <- paste(scheduled_date, scheduled_time)
    
    # Use parameterized query to avoid SQL injection
    query <- "
      INSERT INTO study_sessions 
      (user_id, partner_id, title, description, subject, scheduled_datetime, scheduled_for, duration_minutes, platform, created_by, created_at)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
    "
    
    dbExecute(conn, query, params = list(
      user_id, 
      partner_id, 
      title, 
      description %||% "", 
      subject %||% "General", 
      scheduled_datetime,
      scheduled_datetime, # Populate both for backward compatibility
      duration %||% 60, 
      platform %||% "Zoom",
      user_id  # FIXED: Added created_by parameter
    ))
    
    list(success = TRUE, message = "Study session scheduled successfully")
  }, error = function(e) {
    # More detailed error logging
    cat("❌ ERROR in schedule_study_session_fixed:", e$message, "\n")
    list(success = FALSE, message = paste("Failed to schedule session:", e$message))
  })
}

# FIXED VERSION: Get study sessions with better datetime handling
get_study_sessions_fixed <- function(conn, user_id) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    sessions <- dbGetQuery(conn, "
      SELECT 
        ss.*,
        u.name as partner_name,
        CASE 
          WHEN ss.user_id = ? THEN 'You scheduled'
          ELSE 'Scheduled with you'
        END as session_type
      FROM study_sessions ss
      JOIN users u ON u.id = CASE 
        WHEN ss.user_id = ? THEN ss.partner_id
        ELSE ss.user_id
      END
      WHERE (ss.user_id = ? OR ss.partner_id = ?)
      ORDER BY 
        CASE 
          WHEN ss.scheduled_datetime IS NOT NULL THEN ss.scheduled_datetime
          ELSE ss.scheduled_for
        END DESC
    ", params = list(user_id, user_id, user_id, user_id))
    
    # Ensure proper datetime handling
    if (nrow(sessions) > 0) {
      # Handle both datetime formats
      sessions$scheduled_datetime <- as.character(sessions$scheduled_datetime)
      sessions$scheduled_for <- as.character(sessions$scheduled_for)
    }
    
    sessions
  }, error = function(e) {
    message("Error getting study sessions (fixed): ", e$message)
    return(data.frame())
  })
}

# Shared Goals - FIXED: Proper date handling
create_shared_goal <- function(conn, user_id, partner_id, title, description, deadline, subjects) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    # Ensure deadline is in proper YYYY-MM-DD format
    if (!is.null(deadline) && nzchar(deadline)) {
      deadline <- format(as.Date(deadline), "%Y-%m-%d")
    }
    
    dbExecute(conn, "
      INSERT INTO shared_goals (user_id, partner_id, title, description, deadline, subjects, progress, created_at)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 0, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
    ", params = list(user_id, partner_id, title, description, deadline, subjects))
    
    list(success = TRUE, message = "Shared goal created successfully")
  }, error = function(e) {
    list(success = FALSE, message = paste("Failed to create shared goal:", e$message))
  })
}

get_shared_goals <- function(conn, user_id) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    dbGetQuery(conn, "
      SELECT 
        sg.*,
        u.name as partner_name
      FROM shared_goals sg
      JOIN users u ON u.id = CASE 
        WHEN sg.user_id = ? THEN sg.partner_id
        ELSE sg.user_id
      END
      WHERE (sg.user_id = ? OR sg.partner_id = ?)
        AND sg.progress < 100
      ORDER BY sg.deadline ASC
    ", params = list(user_id, user_id, user_id))
  }, error = function(e) {
    message("Error getting shared goals: ", e$message)
    return(data.frame())
  })
}

  tryCatch({
    dbExecute(conn, "
      UPDATE shared_goals 
      SET progress = ?
      WHERE id = ?
    ", params = list(progress, goal_id))
    
    list(success = TRUE, message = "Goal progress updated successfully")
  }, error = function(e) {
    list(success = FALSE, message = paste("Failed to update goal progress:", e$message))
  })
}

# ENHANCED: Shared Resources with file upload support - FIXED VERSION
share_resource <- function(conn, user_id, partner_id, title, description, resource_type, 
                           file_name = NULL, file_type = NULL, file_size = NULL, file_path = NULL) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    # Handle file parameters safely - ensure they are not NULL
    file_name <- file_name %||% ""
    file_type <- file_type %||% ""
    file_size <- if (!is.null(file_size)) as.integer(file_size) else NA_integer_
    file_path <- file_path %||% ""
    
    # FIXED: Remove file_blob parameter since we're storing files on disk
    dbExecute(conn, "
      INSERT INTO shared_resources 
      (user_id, partner_id, title, description, resource_type, file_name, file_type, file_size, file_path, created_at)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
    ", params = list(
      user_id, 
      partner_id, 
      title, 
      description %||% "", 
      resource_type %||% "Other",
      file_name,
      file_type,
      file_size,
      file_path
    ))
    
    list(success = TRUE, message = "Resource shared successfully")
  }, error = function(e) {
    # More detailed error logging
    cat("❌ ERROR in share_resource:", e$message, "\n")
    list(success = FALSE, message = paste("Failed to share resource:", e$message))
  })
}

get_shared_resources <- function(conn, user_id) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    dbGetQuery(conn, "
      SELECT 
        sr.*,
        u.name as shared_by
      FROM shared_resources sr
      JOIN users u ON u.id = sr.user_id
      WHERE sr.partner_id = ? OR sr.user_id = ?
      ORDER BY sr.created_at DESC
    ", params = list(user_id, user_id))
  }, error = function(e) {
    message("Error getting shared resources: ", e$message)
    return(data.frame())
  })
}

# NEW: Download shared resource
download_shared_resource <- function(conn, resource_id, user_id) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    resource <- dbGetQuery(conn, "
      SELECT * FROM shared_resources 
      WHERE id = ? AND (user_id = ? OR partner_id = ?)
    ", params = list(resource_id, user_id, user_id))
    
    if (nrow(resource) == 0) {
      return(list(success = FALSE, message = "Resource not found or access denied"))
    }
    
    resource <- resource[1, ]
    list(success = TRUE, resource = resource)
  }, error = function(e) {
    list(success = FALSE, message = paste("Failed to download resource:", e$message))
  })
}

  })

get_collaboration_progress <- function(conn, user_id) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    progress <- dbGetQuery(conn, "
      SELECT subject, AVG(mastery_level) as mastery_level
      FROM collaboration_progress
      WHERE user_id = ? OR partner_id = ?
      GROUP BY subject
      ORDER BY mastery_level DESC
    ", params = list(user_id, user_id))
    
    # FIXED: Ensure mastery_level is properly formatted as numeric
    if (nrow(progress) > 0) {
      progress$mastery_level <- as.numeric(progress$mastery_level)
    }
    
    progress
  }, error = function(e) {
    message("Error getting collaboration progress: ", e$message)
    return(data.frame())
  })
}

# Active Collaborations
get_active_collaborations <- function(conn, user_id) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    dbGetQuery(conn, "
      SELECT 
        u.id as partner_id,
        u.name as partner_name,
        GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT o.name) as subjects,
        (SELECT title FROM shared_goals 
         WHERE (user_id = ? AND partner_id = u.id) OR (user_id = u.id AND partner_id = ?)
         AND progress < 100 ORDER BY deadline ASC LIMIT 1) as current_focus,
        (SELECT MAX(created_at) FROM study_sessions ss WHERE (ss.user_id = ? AND ss.partner_id = u.id) OR (ss.user_id = u.id AND ss.partner_id = ?)) as last_activity
      FROM users u
      JOIN study_partner_connections spc ON (
        (spc.user_id = ? AND spc.partner_id = u.id) OR 
        (spc.user_id = u.id AND spc.partner_id = ?)
      )
      LEFT JOIN user_optionals uo ON uo.user_id = u.id
      LEFT JOIN optionals o ON o.id = uo.subject_id
      WHERE spc.status = 'accepted'
      GROUP BY u.id, u.name
      ORDER BY last_activity DESC
    ", params = list(user_id, user_id, user_id, user_id, user_id, user_id))
  }, error = function(e) {
    message("Error getting active collaborations: ", e$message)
    return(data.frame())
  })
}

# ---- Messaging System ----
send_message <- function(conn, connection_id, sender_id, message_text) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  if (!nzchar(message_text)) {
    return(list(success = FALSE, message = "Message cannot be empty"))
  }
  
  now <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  
  tryCatch({
    dbExecute(conn, "
      INSERT INTO study_partner_messages (connection_id, sender_id, message_text, sent_at)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
    ", params = list(connection_id, sender_id, message_text, now))
    
    list(success = TRUE, message = "Message sent successfully")
  }, error = function(e) {
    list(success = FALSE, message = paste("Failed to send message:", e$message))
  })
}

# Get messages for a connection - FIXED: Use proper parameterized query
get_messages <- function(conn, connection_id, limit = 100) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    dbGetQuery(conn, "
      SELECT 
        m.*,
        u.name as sender_name,
        u.email as sender_email
      FROM study_partner_messages m
      JOIN users u ON u.id = m.sender_id
      WHERE m.connection_id = ?
      ORDER BY m.sent_at ASC
      LIMIT ?
    ", params = list(connection_id, limit))
  }, error = function(e) {
    message("Error getting messages: ", e$message)
    return(data.frame())
  })
}

# FIXED VERSION: Get connection by users with better error handling
get_connection_by_users_fixed <- function(conn, user_id, partner_id) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    result <- dbGetQuery(conn, "
      SELECT * FROM study_partner_connections 
      WHERE ((user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?) OR (user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?))
      AND status = 'accepted'
      LIMIT 1
    ", params = list(user_id, partner_id, partner_id, user_id))
    
    if (nrow(result) > 0) {
      return(result[1, ])
    } else {
      return(data.frame())
    }
  }, error = function(e) {
    message("Error in get_connection_by_users_fixed: ", e$message)
    return(data.frame())
  })
}

# Mark messages as read
mark_messages_as_read <- function(conn, connection_id, user_id) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    dbExecute(conn, "
      UPDATE study_partner_messages 
      SET is_read = 1
      WHERE connection_id = ? AND sender_id != ?
    ", params = list(connection_id, user_id))
  }, error = function(e) {
    message("Error marking messages as read: ", e$message)
  })
}

# Get unread message count
get_unread_message_count <- function(conn, user_id) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  tryCatch({
    result <- dbGetQuery(conn, "
      SELECT COUNT(*) as unread_count
      FROM study_partner_messages m
      JOIN study_partner_connections c ON c.id = m.connection_id
      WHERE ((c.user_id = ? AND c.partner_id = m.sender_id) OR (c.partner_id = ? AND c.user_id = m.sender_id))
      AND m.sender_id != ?
      AND m.is_read = 0
    ", params = list(user_id, user_id, user_id))
    
    result$unread_count %||% 0
  }, error = function(e) {
    message("Error getting unread message count: ", e$message)
    return(0)
  })
}

# ---- Connection Scenario Helpers ----
check_incoming_request <- function(conn, user_id, partner_id) {
  tryCatch({
    result <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, 
                              "SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM study_partner_connections 
                               WHERE user_id = ? AND partner_id = ? AND status = 'pending'",
                              params = list(partner_id, user_id))
    return(result$count > 0)
  }, error = function(e) {
    message("Error checking incoming request: ", e$message)
    return(FALSE)
  })
}

accept_mutual_connection <- function(conn, user_id, partner_id) {
  tryCatch({
    # Accept the incoming request (partner -> user)
    DBI::dbExecute(conn,
                   "UPDATE study_partner_connections 
                    SET status = 'accepted'
                    WHERE user_id = ? AND partner_id = ? AND status = 'pending'",
                   params = list(partner_id, user_id))
    
    # Delete the outgoing request (user -> partner) 
    DBI::dbExecute(conn,
                   "DELETE FROM study_partner_connections 
                    WHERE user_id = ? AND partner_id = ? AND status = 'pending'",
                   params = list(user_id, partner_id))
    
    return(list(success = TRUE, message = "Connection established"))
  }, error = function(e) {
    return(list(success = FALSE, message = e$message))
  })
}

cancel_connection_request <- function(conn, from_user_id, to_user_id) {
  tryCatch({
    result <- DBI::dbExecute(conn,
                             "DELETE FROM study_partner_connections 
                              WHERE user_id = ? AND partner_id = ? AND status = 'pending'",
                             params = list(from_user_id, to_user_id))
    
    return(list(success = result > 0, message = ifelse(result > 0, "Request cancelled", "No request found")))
  }, error = function(e) {
    return(list(success = FALSE, message = e$message))
  })
}

cancel_connection_request_by_id <- function(conn, request_id, user_id) {
  tryCatch({
    result <- DBI::dbExecute(conn,
                             "DELETE FROM study_partner_connections 
                              WHERE id = ? AND user_id = ? AND status = 'pending'",
                             params = list(request_id, user_id))
    
    return(list(success = result > 0, message = ifelse(result > 0, "Request cancelled", "No request found")))
  }, error = function(e) {
    return(list(success = FALSE, message = e$message))
  })
}

# ===================== Database Migration Helpers =====================

# Run database migrations for study partner module
migrate_study_partner_database <- function(conn) {
  cat("🔧 Migrating Study Partner Database...\n")
  
  # 1. Ensure study_sessions table has created_by column
  tryCatch({
    cols <- dbGetQuery(conn, "PRAGMA table_info(study_sessions)")$name
    if (!"created_by" %in% cols) {
      cat("   Adding created_by column to study_sessions...\n")
      dbExecute(conn, "ALTER TABLE study_sessions ADD COLUMN created_by INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1")
    }
    
    # 2. Ensure shared_resources table has file storage columns
    if (!"file_name" %in% cols) {
      cat("   Adding file storage columns to shared_resources...\n")
      dbExecute(conn, "ALTER TABLE shared_resources ADD COLUMN file_name TEXT")
      dbExecute(conn, "ALTER TABLE shared_resources ADD COLUMN file_type TEXT")
      dbExecute(conn, "ALTER TABLE shared_resources ADD COLUMN file_size INTEGER")
      dbExecute(conn, "ALTER TABLE shared_resources ADD COLUMN file_path TEXT")
      dbExecute(conn, "ALTER TABLE shared_resources ADD COLUMN file_blob BLOB")
    }
    
    cat("   ✅ Database tables migrated\n")
  }, error = function(e) {
    cat("   ❌ Error migrating database:", e$message, "\n")
  })
  
  # Ensure all study partner tables have correct structure
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  cat("✅ Database migration completed!\n")
}

# Auto-migrate when this file is sourced
.migrate_on_load <- function(conn) {
  tryCatch({
    migrate_study_partner_database(conn)
  }, error = function(e) {
    cat("⚠️  Migration failed:", e$message, "\n")
  })
}
# --- Clear any non-accepted requests between two users (both directions)
clear_nonaccepted_requests <- function(conn, user_a, user_b) {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  try({
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "
      DELETE FROM study_partner_connections
       WHERE ((user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?) OR (user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?))
         AND status <> 'accepted'
    ", params = list(as.integer(user_a), as.integer(user_b),
                     as.integer(user_b), as.integer(user_a)))
  }, silent = TRUE)
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# --- New, tolerant request-creation flow
send_connection_request <- function(conn, user_id, partner_id, icebreaker_message = "") {
  ensure_study_partner_schema(conn)
  
  cat("📤 SENDING CONNECTION REQUEST:\n")
  cat("   From user:", user_id, "\n")
  cat("   To partner:", partner_id, "\n")
  cat("   Message:", icebreaker_message, "\n")
  
  now <- format(Sys.time(), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
  
  # 1) If there is an INCOMING pending (partner -> user), accept it = instant connection
  incoming <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "
    SELECT id FROM study_partner_connections
     WHERE user_id = ? AND partner_id = ? AND status = 'pending'
     LIMIT 1
  ", params = list(as.integer(partner_id), as.integer(user_id)))
  
  if (nrow(incoming) > 0) {
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "
      UPDATE study_partner_connections
         SET status = 'accepted', responded_at = ?
       WHERE id = ?
    ", params = list(now, incoming$id[1]))
    cat("   🤝 Incoming pending found — accepted. Connection established.\n")
    return(list(success = TRUE, message = "Connection established"))
  }
  
  # 2) If there’s an ACCEPTED connection already (either direction), block duplicate
  accepted <- DBI::dbGetQuery(conn, "
    SELECT 1 FROM study_partner_connections
     WHERE ((user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?) OR (user_id = ? AND partner_id = ?))
       AND status = 'accepted'
     LIMIT 1
  ", params = list(as.integer(user_id), as.integer(partner_id),
                   as.integer(partner_id), as.integer(user_id)))
  
  if (nrow(accepted) > 0) {
    cat("   ✅ Already connected — not sending a new request.\n")
    return(list(success = FALSE, message = "Already connected"))
  }
  
  # 3) Clear any non-accepted (rejected/cancelled/old pending) requests both ways
  clear_nonaccepted_requests(conn, user_id, partner_id)
  
  # 4) Insert a fresh pending request (user -> partner)
  res <- tryCatch({
    DBI::dbExecute(conn, "
      INSERT INTO study_partner_connections (user_id, partner_id, icebreaker_message, created_at)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
    ", params = list(as.integer(user_id), as.integer(partner_id), icebreaker_message %||% "", now))
    cat("   ✅ Connection request sent successfully\n")
    list(success = TRUE, message = "Connection request sent successfully")
  }, error = function(e) {
    cat("   ❌ Failed to send connection request:", e$message, "\n")
    # Try one more time with a hard clear in case of a last-millisecond race:
    clear_nonaccepted_requests(conn, user_id, partner_id)
    try({
      DBI::dbExecute(conn, "
        INSERT INTO study_partner_connections (user_id, partner_id, icebreaker_message, created_at)
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
      ", params = list(as.integer(user_id), as.integer(partner_id), icebreaker_message %||% "", now))
      cat("   ✅ Retried and sent after clearing\n")
      return(list(success = TRUE, message = "Connection request sent successfully"))
    }, silent = TRUE)
    list(success = FALSE, message = paste("Failed to send connection request:", e$message))
  })
  
  res
}

  year = rep(2014:2024, each = 6),
  subject = rep(compulsory_subjects, times = 11),
  topic = sample(unlist(topics_bank[compulsory_subjects]), size = 11*6, replace = TRUE)

=== R/utils_generators.R ===

safe_pick <- function(x, n = 1) sample(x, size = min(n, length(x)), replace = FALSE)

make_study_plan <- function(start_date, exam_date, subjects, weak_subject = NULL, proficiency = c("Beginner","Intermediate","Advanced")) {
  proficiency <- match.arg(proficiency)
  days <- as.integer(exam_date - start_date) + 1
  req(days > 0)
  topics <- purrr::map(subjects, ~ topics_bank[[.x]] %||% c("General Review"))
  names(topics) <- subjects

  weights <- rep(1, length(subjects))
  if (!is.null(weak_subject) && weak_subject %in% subjects) {
    weights[subjects == weak_subject] <- 1.8
  }
  weights <- weights / sum(weights)

  hrs <- switch(proficiency, Beginner = 5, Intermediate = 4, Advanced = 3)

  schedule <- tibble::tibble(day = 1:days, date = seq.Date(start_date, exam_date, by = "day")) |>
    dplyr::rowwise() |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      subject = sample(subjects, 1, prob = weights),
      topic = sample(topics[[subject]], 1),
      hours = hrs,
      tasks = paste("Focus on:", topic, "| Revise + attempt 10 MCQs + 1 short note")
    ) |>
    dplyr::ungroup()

  schedule <- schedule |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      tasks = ifelse(weekdays(date) == "Sunday",
                     paste(tasks, "+ Weekly Mock (2 hrs)"),
                     tasks)
    )
  schedule
}

make_mcq <- function(subject, topic, difficulty = c("Easy","Medium","Hard")) {
  difficulty <- match.arg(difficulty)
  stem <- glue::glue("[{difficulty}] In {subject}, regarding '{topic}', which of the following is most accurate?")
  opts_base <- c("A comprehensive framework", "An underlying principle", "A historical event", "A policy instrument",
                 "A key challenge", "An empirical observation", "A normative stance", "A methodological tool")
  options <- safe_pick(opts_base, 4)
  correct <- sample(LETTERS[1:4], 1)
  tibble::tibble(type = "MCQ", question = as.character(stem),
         A = options[1], B = options[2], C = options[3], D = options[4],
         correct = toupper(correct))
}

make_short <- function(subject, topic, difficulty = c("Easy","Medium","Hard")) {
  difficulty <- match.arg(difficulty)
  stem <- glue::glue("[{difficulty}] Write 4–6 lines on: {topic} ({subject}).")
  tibble::tibble(type = "Short", prompt = as.character(stem))
}

make_essay <- function(subject, topic, difficulty = c("Easy","Medium","Hard")) {
  difficulty <- match.arg(difficulty)
  stem <- glue::glue("[{difficulty}] Critically analyze: '{topic}' in the context of {subject}. Develop a structured essay with thesis, arguments, counter-arguments, and conclusion.")
  tibble::tibble(type = "Essay", prompt = as.character(stem))
}

make_questions <- function(subject, topic, qtype = c("MCQ","Short","Essay"), difficulty = c("Easy","Medium","Hard"), n = 5) {
  qtype <- match.arg(qtype)
  difficulty <- match.arg(difficulty)
  if (qtype == "MCQ") {
    purrr::map_dfr(seq_len(n), ~ make_mcq(subject, topic, difficulty))
  } else if (qtype == "Short") {
    purrr::map_dfr(seq_len(n), ~ make_short(subject, topic, difficulty))
  } else {
    purrr::map_dfr(seq_len(n), ~ make_essay(subject, topic, difficulty))
  }
}

make_guess_paper <- function(subject, top_n = 8) {
  t <- past_trends |> dplyr::filter(subject == !!subject) |> dplyr::arrange(dplyr::desc(appearances))
  if (nrow(t) == 0) return(tibble::tibble())
  top_topics <- t |> dplyr::slice_max(order_by = appearances, n = min(top_n, nrow(t)))
  prompts <- purrr::map_chr(top_topics$topic, ~ glue::glue("Critically evaluate '{.x}' with contemporary examples."))
  tibble::tibble(section = paste("Guess Paper —", subject), question_no = seq_along(prompts), prompt = prompts)
}

fetch_rss <- function(url, n = 15) {
  out <- tibble::tibble(title = character(), link = character(), published = character(), summary = character())
  try({
    doc <- xml2::read_xml(url)
    items <- xml2::xml_find_all(doc, "//item")
    if (length(items) == 0) items <- xml2::xml_find_all(doc, "//entry")
    titles <- xml2::xml_text(xml2::xml_find_all(items, "title"))
    links <- xml2::xml_text(xml2::xml_find_all(items, "link"))
    if (length(links) == 0) links <- xml2::xml_attr(xml2::xml_find_all(items, "link"), "href")
    pubs <- xml2::xml_text(xml2::xml_find_all(items, "pubDate"))
    if (length(pubs) == 0) pubs <- xml2::xml_text(xml2::xml_find_all(items, "updated"))
    desc <- xml2::xml_text(xml2::xml_find_all(items, "description"))
    if (length(desc) == 0) desc <- xml2::xml_text(xml2::xml_find_all(items, "summary"))

    out <- tibble::tibble(
      title = titles %||% NA_character_,
      link = links %||% NA_character_,
      published = pubs %||% NA_character_,
      summary = desc %||% NA_character_
    ) |>
      head(n)
  }, silent = TRUE)
  out
}
